Chapter 1148: The Previous Generation’s Fire King!

Chapter 1148: The Previous Generation’s Fire King

!【Third update】

“The Fire King’s master!”

Many of the pinnacle Dao Ancestors were deeply puzzled. They had never heard that the Fire King had any master, and the aura of this newcomer was vastly stronger than the Fire King’s—he was clearly an invincible Dao Ancestor.

But as for this invincible Dao Ancestor’s origins, they had never heard of him before.

“The previous generation’s Fire King, Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire!”

Matchless Dao Ancestor said.

Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire was somewhat surprised and said, “You know me?”

His reputation was not well known, and his former identity had been Fire King. Others all called him Fire King, so people only knew the title Fire King, but not the name Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire.

“What, the previous generation’s Fire King?”

The many pinnacle Dao Ancestors were all astonished.

“Could it be that the legend is true—that the Ten Kings of Black Wind Mountain are merely a title, a title passed down from generation to generation, and not specifically ten fixed individuals 10?!”

Myriad Sword Dao Ancestor of the Heavenly Sword Sect said in shock.

The expressions of the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors changed drastically one after another. If this guess were true, then Black Wind Mountain’s strength was far from as simple as it appeared before them! The Ten Kings represented ten 10 pinnacle Dao Ancestors. Although in the battle when the domain realm shattered, four of the Ten Kings had fallen 44, leaving only six kings, if the previous generation and the generation before that of the Ten Kings were still alive, then just how many pinnacle Dao Ancestors did Black Wind Mountain have? How many invincible Dao Ancestors? “Of course I know you!”

Matchless Dao Ancestor said, “Though I don’t know much about your Black Wind Mountain, I do know a few people, and one of them is you, Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire. It’s said that you once came to one of our Mitian Sect’s secret realms to steal, but were driven back by one of our Mitian Sect’s invincible Dao Ancestors!”

“That did happen. That was all a very long time ago 04!”

Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire sighed.

Then, Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire glanced at the Fire King, then looked at Matchless Dao Ancestor and said, “Today, give me some face. Let this matter end here, how about it?”

“In your dreams. How could a single forbidden treasure possibly be left at that?”

Matchless Dao Ancestor charged at Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire, showing no fear of him at all.

“Looks like we still have to fight!”

Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire muttered.

Boom!!!! Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire and Matchless Dao Ancestor, the two invincible Dao Ancestors, began battling, while the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors all turned their eyes toward the Fire King.

The current Fire King was on the verge of death. This was precisely the best time to kill him.

Wind King’s expression changed, and he hurriedly tried to take Fire King away and flee, but there were simply too many pinnacle Dao Ancestors around—nearly dozens of them.

Wanting to rescue Fire King from the hands of so many pinnacle Dao Ancestors was difficult enough to rival the difficulty of killing an invincible Dao Ancestor.

Right at this moment.

Several figures appeared, and voices rang out at the same time.

“Wind King, Fire King, we’ve come to help you!”

Boom!!!! The other four kings of Black Wind Mountain had also arrived! “Gold King, Wood King, Ice King, Time King!”

When the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors saw these four pinnacle Dao Ancestors, they still felt not the slightest fear.

They had dozens of pinnacle Dao Ancestors, while Black Wind Mountain had only brought six pinnacle Dao Ancestors this time, and of those currently able to fight, there were only five pinnacle Dao Ancestors. They posed no threat to them at all.

However, just as the many pinnacle Dao Ancestors were about to charge in and kill, another forbidden treasure appeared—and two of them appeared all at once.

“....”

Quite a few pinnacle Dao Ancestors hesitated for a moment, then quickly made their decision.

Swoosh swoosh swoosh!!!! One pinnacle Dao Ancestor after another tore through space and left, going to seize the forbidden treasures.

After all, although some pinnacle Dao Ancestors also desired the Forbidden Fire Lotus, the forbidden treasure might not necessarily suit them. Besides, with so many pinnacle Dao Ancestors competing for a single forbidden treasure, and with two invincible Dao Ancestors present, the chance of successfully seizing it was not high.

Since that was the case, it was better to go seize the forbidden treasures that had just appeared.

In the blink of an eye, most of the pinnacle Dao Ancestors had all left, leaving behind the three pinnacle Dao Ancestors of the Mitian Sect and a few other pinnacle Dao Ancestors. Even joining forces, these pinnacle Dao Ancestors found it difficult to seize the treasure on Fire King’s person.

Just like that.

The five kings of Black Wind Mountain protected Fire King and calmly withdrew, and the Forbidden Fire Lotus fell into Black Wind Mountain’s hands.

After the six kings of Black Wind Mountain came out of the Fireflame Forbidden Land, Fire King said gratefully, “Many thanks to all my brothers for helping me!”

“You should be thanking Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire instead!”

Time King said, “For your sake, even Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire’s existence has been exposed. That is not a good thing for our Black Wind Mountain. All at once, we’ve become the target of many great factions.

Also, Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire told us to withdraw from the Fireflame Forbidden Land immediately and not get involved any further. Even if more precious treasures appear, we are not to go in again!”

“Why?”

Wind King asked.

He still hadn’t gained anything this time. If he returned like this to sleep, the loss would be enormous! He could be said to have emerged twice already. If he were to emerge again next time, it would probably be after a very, very long time.

“Not sure!”

Time King shook his head. “But we must obey Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire’s order.

I have a guess: probably large numbers of invincible Dao Ancestors will descend upon the Fireflame Forbidden Land. If that happens, then with one careless mistake, we may fall.

Dao Ancestor Flowing Fire is also thinking of our safety and does not wish for us to be sacrificed!”

“Sigh, then let’s go back!”

Wind King said unwillingly.

Wind King, Fire King, Time King, Gold King, Wood King, and Ice King returned one after another to the small domain realm, then entered the place of slumber and began sleeping once more, no longer paying attention to matters in the Fireflame Forbidden Land, lest they be unable to resist running out again.

....“Damn, a forbidden treasure!”

Ye Tian was quite surprised. He had just been walking around casually, yet he actually came across a forbidden treasure.

Could his luck really be this good? This time entering the Fireflame Forbidden Land, he truly had never expected to obtain a forbidden treasure. His sole purpose had merely been to obtain more forbidden oddities.

He knew very well that at this moment, there were definitely many pinnacle Dao Ancestors who had entered the Fireflame Forbidden Land. There might even be invincible Dao Ancestors descending here.

If he were to seize a forbidden treasure, that would not be a good thing. He had no desire to experience being besieged by pinnacle Dao Ancestors.

But....“A forbidden treasure has been delivered right in front of me, and there aren’t even any other True Ancestors nearby. If I still don’t take it, that’d be going too far!”

Ye Tian thought to himself.

Thus.

Ye Tian captured a dozen or so magma monsters and sent them one by one before this forbidden treasure, which resembled a rod-like stake.

Boom boom boom!!!! A great terror was triggered, and one magma monster after another was obliterated by the great terror.

Only after nine magma monsters had died did the great terror completely dissipate.

One could well imagine just how terrifying the great terror triggered by a forbidden treasure was. If Ye Tian had faced that kind of great terror directly, he too would probably have fallen and died.

“Go!”

Ye Tian grabbed this forbidden treasure staff and was just about to leave.

But at this moment, a pinnacle Dao Ancestor had already arrived.

This pinnacle Dao Ancestor was Dao Ancestor Tianxiu of the Myriad Domains Divine Hall. Sensing Ye Tian’s presence, he immediately shouted in anger, “Nine Extremes Heavenly General, stay right there!”

Dao Ancestor Tianxiu was furious. Earlier, Black Wind Mountain’s Fire King had seized the Forbidden Fire Lotus. He had finally sensed the aura of another forbidden treasure, yet unexpectedly it had still been snatched away by Black Wind Mountain’s Nine Extremes Heavenly General.

“Damn it, your Black Wind Mountain is too overbearing!”

Dao Ancestor Tianxiu roared.

He might not be able to kill Black Wind Mountain’s Fire King, but could he still not kill a mere True Ancestor?

He also knew Ye Tian was Black Wind Mountain’s pinnacle True Ancestor. If he could kill Ye Tian, it would be comparable to killing a pinnacle Dao Ancestor—enough to make Black Wind Mountain ache terribly.

Boom!!! Dao Ancestor Tianxiu threw a punch, ignoring the distance as it descended directly upon Ye Tian.

“Great Desolate Dharma Body!”

The mid-thousand Dao technique at the limit level erupted to defend against Dao Ancestor Tianxiu’s punch. Although it was still shattered, the passive defensive Dao technique Vajra Battle Body was not broken. Then, after being weakened by sixty percent of the forbidden body, the remaining impact could not injure Ye Tian in the slightest.

“What? Limit-level Vajra Battle Body, limit-level Great Desolate Dharma Body, and even a sixty percent forbidden body!”

Dao Ancestor Tianxiu was stunned.

In such a short time, Ye Tian had actually cultivated Vajra Battle Body and Great Desolate Dharma Body to the limit level, and had even raised his forbidden body to sixty percent. This speed was simply terrifying! He also knew a little about pinnacle True Ancestors, but not to the point of such monstrous talent! However, what he could never have imagined was that Ye Tian had fused hundreds of Dao-level innate talents, and in addition had the assistance of seven 7 ancient world records in cultivation, making his cultivation speed surpass that of others by no small amount....

Aside from Ouyang Jiu’er, the reincarnation of a half-step Domain Ancestor, the progress speed of all other pinnacle True Ancestors was far inferior to his.

“Myriad Fiend True Spear!”

Ye Tian struck back with... a blow.

Boom! A strike from the Myriad Fiend True Spear sent Dao Ancestor Tianxiu flying back and even split one of his hands open, threads of fresh blood flowing out.

Although Dao Ancestor Tianxiu’s wound recovered in an instant, leaving not the slightest injury.

Dao Ancestor Tianxiu’s eyes widened, revealing an expression of utter disbelief.

“What a monster. Still at the True Ancestor level, yet already enough to rival an ordinary Fourth Heaven Dao Ancestor—is this what a pinnacle True Ancestor is?”

Dao Ancestor Tianxiu muttered.

Chapter 1149 Ouyang Jiu'er Has Arrived!

Chapter 1149: Ouyang Jiu'er Has Arrived

!【Fourth Update】

Ancestor Tiansiu knew he couldn't kill Ye Tian, but he also didn't want to let Ye Tian get away.

A forbidden pinnacle treasure! Although he didn't know what kind of forbidden pinnacle treasure it was, how could he possibly give up the chase so easily? Ancestor Tiansiu moved swiftly through space, pursuing Ye Tian.

Ye Tian unleashed Heavenly Gang Extreme Speed, but this was only a mid-tier Dao technique. Even though he had cultivated it to the limit, its speed still wasn't all that fast.

But Ancestor Tiansiu was different. He possessed a pinnacle Dao technique, and his speed was astonishing. In no time at all, he caught up to Ye Tian and began battling him again.

And at this moment, the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors were also about to arrive.

“I can't let Ancestor Tiansiu hold me back, otherwise once the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors arrive, I won't be able to get away at all!”

Ye Tian said with a frown.

But his strength was comparable to Ancestor Tiansiu's, though in truth he was still a bit weaker. It was only because his forbidden body had been tempered to sixty percent, while Ancestor Tiansiu's forbidden body had only just reached minor completion, that he could weaken more of the incoming attacks. That was why he was able to fight Ancestor Tiansiu to a standstill.

But in reality, his speed was much inferior to Ancestor Tiansiu's, and even his strongest attack power was slightly weaker.

Given this comparison in battle, he had no way to shake off Ancestor Tiansiu.

Boom!!!! Another pinnacle Dao Ancestor descended—it was Ancestor Bayun of the Heavenly Sword Sect, a pinnacle Dao Ancestor even more powerful than Ancestor Tiansiu.

“Ancestor Tiansiu, is the forbidden pinnacle treasure on you?”

Ancestor Bayun demanded.

“Ancestor Bayun, can't you see that I'm stopping Jiuji Tianjiang from leaving? The forbidden pinnacle treasure is on him!”

Ancestor Tiansiu said coldly.

Ancestor Bayun immediately joined the siege against Ye Tian. The two pinnacle Dao Ancestors easily suppressed Ye Tian, even beating him until he was constantly injured.

Suddenly.

Yet another pinnacle Dao Ancestor's aura drew near, and Ye Tian knew he could not delay any longer.

He took out a leaf. It was none other than a Forbidden Void Leaf, a forbidden wonder used for escape. Among the forbidden wonders he possessed, it was one of the more valuable ones, and he had always been reluctant to use it. But now, he had no choice.

Whoosh! The Forbidden Void Leaf transformed into forbidden laws that wrapped around Ye Tian, instantly tearing through the space of the forbidden land and taking him away. It was so fast that even Ancestor Bayun and Ancestor Tiansiu couldn't stop him.

“A forbidden wonder for escape? Hmph, we have those too!”

Ancestor Bayun and Ancestor Tiansiu also used similar escape-type forbidden wonders and chased after Ye Tian.

It had to be said that Ye Tian had underestimated these pinnacle Dao Ancestors. Any powerhouse who could cultivate to the level of a pinnacle Dao Ancestor had almost no shortcomings. They were well-rounded in every aspect, which made it incredibly difficult to shake off even a single pinnacle Dao Ancestor! Somewhere within the Flame Blaze Forbidden Land, Ye Tian's figure appeared, and then he quickly left again.

But unfortunately, the pinnacle Dao Ancestors' pursuit abilities were too strong. Almost instantly, they arrived there as well, sensed Ye Tian's location, and gave chase once more.

As far as... the pinnacle Dao Ancestors were concerned, all of Ye Tian's divine abilities and secret arts for concealing his aura were useless. There was no way he could escape.

Very soon, the news that Ye Tian had snatched a forbidden pinnacle treasure spread out, and many powerful figures learned of it.

In another part of the Flame Forbidden Land.

General Bloodfiend, General Motian, and the others also heard the news and all frowned in concern.

“Lord Jiuji Tianjiang is being hunted by multiple pinnacle Dao Ancestors. This is a bit dangerous!”

General Bloodfiend muttered.

“Can we ask Wind King and the others to help rescue Lord Jiuji Tianjiang?” Tian General asked.

“No!”

General Bloodfiend shook his head. “I tried contacting Wind King. Wind King has already returned to Black Wind Mountain, and he said he won't be getting involved this time. He even told us that if we can leave, we should leave, and not get involved in the struggle over the Flame Blaze Forbidden Land.

But how could we be willing to give up? There are too many forbidden wonders here. Just searching around casually would let us obtain quite a lot.”

General Motian also sighed. There was no way they could just give up, and since Wind King was unwilling to get involved, there was no way to support Jiuji Tianjiang.

“We can only rely on Lord Jiuji Tianjiang himself now!”

General Bloodfiend said with a sigh.

Time slowly passed, and more and more pinnacle Dao Ancestors joined the pursuit of Ye Tian. Of course, not all the pinnacle Dao Ancestors came after him. After all, there weren't just... one or two forbidden pinnacle treasures in the Flame Blaze Forbidden Land. As more and more forbidden pinnacle treasures appeared, the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors also went off to snatch them.

But Ancestor Bayun and Ancestor Tiansiu refused to give up and kept pursuing Ye Tian, forcing him to use quite a few forbidden wonders, yet he still couldn't shake them off.

Suddenly.

While Ye Tian was moving through space, he was suddenly grabbed by a fair, tender hand.

Ye Tian had been about to resist, but when he sensed a familiar aura, he stopped at once.

“Jiu'er!”

Seeing the person before him, Ye Tian exclaimed in delight.

“Hide your aura as much as possible. I'll use Shadowless Divine Steps. That way, even the pinnacle Dao Ancestors won't be able to sense your existence!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said hurriedly.

“Mm!”

Ye Tian nodded.

Ye Tian's aura vanished. With the help of Shadowless Divine Steps, it was as if he had completely ceased to exist between heaven and earth. It was as though there was no longer any information or past concerning him in this world. No karma or spacetime Dao technique could detect his existence.

Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!! Ancestor Bayun and Ancestor Tiansiu descended into this region, but they could no longer sense Ye Tian's presence. They used various tracking secret techniques, but still could not find him, and immediately frowned.

“How is this possible? How did Jiuji Tianjiang's aura disappear?”

Ancestor Tiansiu was puzzled.

“I can't find him either!”

Ancestor Bayun said, “Could he have fallen?”

“Impossible for him to have fallen!”

Ancestor Tiansiu immediately refuted, “His strength isn't much weaker than the strength we've displayed, and he's also a Pinnacle True Ancestor. No matter how severe his injuries are, he can repair them with source power. His source power is endless—how could he be killed so easily, let alone instantly? Unless a Domain Ancestor made a move, that would be more believable!”

“He probably used some treasure he'd been reluctant to use all along and completely hid himself away!”

Ancestor Bayun guessed.

Since they could no longer find Ye Tian, the two pinnacle Dao Ancestors didn't want to waste time, so they quickly left to go seize other forbidden pinnacle treasures.

“Jiu'er, thank you!”

Ye Tian said gratefully.

Had it not been for Ouyang Jiu'er this time, he would have been in real trouble. He probably wouldn't have died, but at most he would have lost this copied body, along with a large number of forbidden wonders and one forbidden pinnacle treasure.

“I also heard the news about you, so I came over. You've got quite some nerve. You knew full well that forbidden pinnacle treasures were things the pinnacle Dao Ancestors were fighting over, and you still dared to snatch one.

Did you think you were me, able to easily avoid the detection of the pinnacle Dao Ancestors?”

Ouyang Jiu'er rolled her eyes and said.

“I really didn't go to snatch a forbidden pinnacle treasure. But when a forbidden pinnacle treasure practically appeared right in my face, if I didn't take it, wouldn't that be too foolish?”

Ye Tian explained.

“Let's not talk about that for now. I've already confirmed where the forbidden pinnacle treasure stored inside the Heavenly Emperor Palace within the Flame Blaze Forbidden Land is!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said mysteriously.

“You found that forbidden pinnacle treasure?!”

Ye Tian was instantly tempted, then asked, “Can we take it away?”

“No, unless we pack up the entire Flame Blaze Forbidden Land and take it with us!”

Ouyang Jiu'er joked.

Ye Tian then said, “Isn't that forbidden pinnacle treasure able to simulate future paths? Shouldn't we go activate it first and let it simulate our future paths for us?”

“No!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said, “That forbidden pinnacle treasure is called the Haotian Emperor Mirror. Activating it requires a tremendous amount of the life-blood of True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors. Otherwise, relying on our own power, we wouldn't be able to activate it for long.

During this period, quite a few True Ancestors have fallen, and I've been collecting corpses.

You should also hurry and collect some corpses. Corpses of forbidden bloodline creatures will work too. Once we've gathered enough, we'll offer them as sacrifices to the Haotian Emperor Mirror!”

“Alright!”

Ye Tian nodded.

Immediately, the two of them began moving through the Flame Blaze Forbidden Land, collecting forbidden wonders while also gathering the corpses and blood of True Ancestors, Dao Ancestors, and forbidden bloodline creatures.

And so, time gradually passed, and another day went by.

At this time, nine forbidden pinnacle treasures had already appeared in the Flame Blaze Forbidden Land.

Of these, Ye Tian had seized one, Ouyang Jiu'er had already seized one earlier, Fire King had seized one, the Tianhai Sect had seized one, the Myriad Domains Divine Hall had seized one, and the Mitian Sect had seized one.

As for the whereabouts of the other three forbidden pinnacle treasures, no one knew.

“Brother Ye, let's hurry to the Haotian Emperor Mirror now. Most of the forbidden pinnacle treasures have already appeared, and the Heavenly Emperor Palace may reveal the Haotian Emperor Mirror at any moment and activate their plan. So we should go use the Haotian Emperor Mirror first!”

Ouyang Jiu'er urged.

Immediately, the two set out, quickly heading for the place where the Haotian Emperor Mirror was located.

Chapter 1150: A Massacre!

Chapter 1150: A Massacre

!【Fifth Update】

In the Fiery Flame Forbidden Land stood a gourd-shaped mountain.

Rivers of lava encircled it on all sides, while manifestations of laws appeared on the mountain, forming clouds of forbidden laws one after another.

Suddenly.

Two figures arrived here—it was Ye Tian and Ouyang Jiu'er.

“This is the place!”

Ouyang Jiu'er pointed at the gourd-shaped mountain before them and said.

Ye Tian swept it with his divine sense, but did not discover the Haotian Emperor Mirror. Instead, he found quite a few forbidden exotic objects.

“The Haotian Emperor Mirror isn’t on the mountain, but in the clouds of laws. There’s a vast space inside. We’ll know once we go in!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said.

Whoosh, whoosh! Ye Tian and Ouyang Jiu'er flew into the clouds of laws and indeed arrived in a gigantic space.

Within this space, an enormous... black-gold mirror floated in the void, connected to the laws of heaven and earth.

It stood there as if naturally formed, without the slightest trace of outside interference.

“If you hadn’t told me, Jiu'er, then even if I saw this Haotian Emperor Mirror, I would’ve thought it was born here naturally. I’d never believe someone had placed it here!”

Ye Tian murmured.

Ouyang Jiu'er said, “The Haotian Emperor Mirror is a very secret forbidden pinnacle treasure of the Heavenly Emperor Palace. Even some of the Emperors of the Heavenly Emperor “Zero Four Seven”

Palace don’t know of this treasure’s existence. After all, the price to activate it is far too great. The Heavenly Emperor Palace can’t use the lives of countless True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors just to help a single Dao Ancestor simulate the path of the future! If this pinnacle treasure were exposed, many Emperors would probably develop dangerous thoughts! If I didn’t have a special information channel, I probably wouldn’t know the Heavenly Emperor Palace possessed the Haotian Emperor Mirror either!”

“Let’s begin. This place will probably be exposed very soon. Even if no one discovers it, if the Heavenly Emperor Palace makes the slightest move and causes even a minor anomaly here, a huge number of True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors will definitely rush over. When that happens, we’ll be in trouble!”

Ouyang Jiu'er urged.

“Mm!”

Ye Tian took out the large number of True Ancestor corpses he had collected, along with some Dao Ancestor corpses, and offered them as sacrifices to the Haotian Emperor Mirror before him.

On the other side, Ouyang Jiu'er also began sacrificing those True Ancestor and Dao Ancestor corpses.

Boom!!!!! The Haotian Emperor Mirror emitted light, continuously absorbing the blood and life force of those powerful beings.

Suddenly.

Through the Haotian Emperor Mirror, Ye Tian saw scenes of the future related to cultivation. These scenes felt as if he were experiencing them personally, showing him all kinds of future possibilities, and in the end finding for him the road most suited to him.

Of course, this was not the true future—it merely provided a correct path of cultivation.

But this was even better than directly seeing the future. At the very least, he would not take detours, and not everyone’s future necessarily followed the right road; many had gone astray.

Ye Tian saw himself continuously comprehending and cultivating the Forbidden Dao, understanding one forbidden dao after another, until he finally grasped the complete Forbidden Dao, then merged it with his own Endless Great Dao to form an Endless Forbidden Dao unique to himself.

After that, he used the Endless Forbidden Dao to break through into the Dao Ancestor realm.

Further on, he created his own Forbidden Dao Art, one that stood above the strongest Dao Arts, invincible in the world, making him the strongest invincible Dao Ancestor.

After that, he comprehended a trace of the mysteries of the Domain Ancestor, cultivated unceasingly, and advanced toward the Half-Step Domain Ancestor realm.

But suddenly, the images disappeared, and all those insights came to an abrupt halt.

He saw that the countless corpses had already turned to ashes. The sacrificial power had been exhausted, causing the future path he was watching to be cut off.

This feeling was awful! At that moment, Ye Tian almost wanted to go kill countless True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors just to continue observing the path of the future.

But very quickly, Ye Tian calmed down.

“Hah, no wonder Jiu'er said that once the Haotian Emperor Mirror appears, countless True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors will die. The temptation of the Haotian Emperor Mirror is too great. Even an exalted True Ancestor like me, who doesn’t worry about the future at all, almost lost myself to it. Those pinnacle Dao Ancestors who can’t see the road ahead will surely go even crazier.

The invincible Dao Ancestors might even want to kill pinnacle Dao Ancestors. One corpse of a pinnacle Dao Ancestor is worth countless True Ancestor corpses. And the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors would spare no cost to slaughter other True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors, all just so the simulation of their future path could go farther!”

Ye Tian thought to himself.

On the other side.

Ouyang Jiu'er also finished simulating the Dao path and seemed to have gained something as well. She wore a smile, in an excellent mood.

“Come on, let’s keep collecting corpses! But you need to stay calm. We’re not making a move ourselves—we’ll only collect the corpses of the True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors who get killed!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said.

“Mm!”

Ye Tian nodded.

He had long since calmed down, so naturally he would not act rashly.

After Ye Tian and Ouyang Jiu'er left, a True Ancestor arrived and discovered the Haotian Emperor Mirror. He wanted to take it away, but found that he simply couldn’t.

Not long after, the news of the Haotian Emperor Mirror, this forbidden pinnacle treasure, spread out, drawing a huge number of True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors. Even pinnacle Dao Ancestors were attracted over.

Before the Haotian Emperor Mirror.

A group of True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors gathered here, and none of them made a move. They seemed very harmonious, because there was no way to take away the Haotian Emperor Mirror, so fighting and killing seemed unnecessary.

Boom!!! The first pinnacle Dao Ancestor descended—it was Dao Ancestor Tianxiu of the Hall of Myriad Domains.

Afterward, Dao Ancestor Tianqi, Dao Ancestor Tianqi, Dao Ancestor Pokong, Dao Ancestor Zhanyin, Dao Ancestor Xuegang, Dao Ancestor Shisha, Dao Ancestor Mijian, Dao Ancestor Wanjian, Dao Ancestor Bayun... one pinnacle Dao Ancestor after another descended, each trying to seize the Haotian Emperor Mirror. But they soon discovered that even they could not take away this forbidden pinnacle treasure.

“This forbidden pinnacle treasure is completely locked together with this large forbidden treasure land. It should be the most precious forbidden pinnacle treasure in this large forbidden treasure land!”

Dao Ancestor Bayun evaluated.

Immediately after, they began studying the use of this forbidden exotic object.

They saw that when Dao Ancestor Bayun poured his own power into the Haotian Emperor Mirror, he unexpectedly glimpsed an image of a future path.

Unfortunately, the power was consumed too quickly, so he did not continue pouring power into it.

“This is a forbidden pinnacle treasure that simulates the future path!”

Dao Ancestor Bayun was incomparably excited.

He knew very well what this represented.

With this forbidden pinnacle treasure, he could simulate the path to becoming an invincible Dao Ancestor, and even the path toward Half-Step Domain Ancestor. The future was bright; no shackles would remain at all.

At once, he went mad... He understood very clearly that what this kind of forbidden pinnacle treasure lacked was a certain form of energy. As long as the energy requirement was met, it could remain activated indefinitely.

He tried to fuse some forbidden dao stones into the Haotian Emperor Mirror, but it was of no use.

Very soon, he figured it out.

What the Haotian Emperor Mirror needed was energy containing life aura, but he alone could not satisfy the Haotian Emperor Mirror’s energy requirements.

Immediately, he turned his gaze toward those True Ancestors and the weaker Dao Ancestors.

Boom!!! Dao Ancestor Bayun attacked those True Ancestors. His Dao Ancestor power transformed into thread after thread, easily piercing through the bodies of one True Ancestor after another.

One True Ancestor after another fell dead. In the blink of an eye, several thousand True Ancestors had perished.

“Dao Ancestor Bayun, have you gone mad?”

The other pinnacle Dao Ancestors flew into a rage.

Among the True Ancestors who had been killed were members of their own sects. Dao Ancestor Bayun was trying to start an all-out war with them! Yet Dao Ancestor Bayun paid no attention, continuing to slaughter those True Ancestors. He even killed several Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestors as well, collecting all of their corpses.

A few seconds later, another pinnacle Dao Ancestor—Dao Ancestor Mijian—made his move. He did not stop Dao Ancestor Bayun either, but also went to kill those True Ancestors.

At this point, no matter how foolish the other pinnacle Dao Ancestors were, they understood. Recalling Bayun and Mijian’s earlier actions, they quickly figured out the Haotian Emperor Mirror’s effect.

In an instant, the True Ancestors became the targets of their slaughter. Even... even when their own juniors from their sects were killed, they no longer cared.

Compared to the future path, nothing was more important than this.

Dao Ancestor Bayun proposed.

No matter how powerful an invincible Dao Ancestor was, they were still far from being a match for a half-step Domain Ancestor. The gap in strength between the two sides was even greater than the gap between an invincible True Ancestor and a Pinnacle True Ancestor.

Fireflame Forbidden Land.

In truth, they did indeed succeed in the deduction, and it revealed a future path at the half-step Domain Ancestor level, allowing them to clearly see the direction ahead.

But seeing it clearly was one thing; actually achieving it was another.

According to that manifested future path, these invincible Dao Ancestors had gained hope of breaking into the half-step Domain Ancestor realm, but if they truly wanted to reach that level, it would require an extremely long span of time.

The first condition was that the forbidden body had to be tempered to the major accomplishment realm, with half of one’s Dao power transformed into forbidden power. Transformed into forbidden power—not merely containing forbidden properties. Those two meanings were different.

And this mysterious person’s forbidden body had already reached major accomplishment, estimated to have achieved eighty percent tempering. This was no ordinary major accomplishment.

Moreover, the set of forbidden weapons on him was incomparably precious and could likewise amplify battle power.

The reason they hundred percent concluded the other party was a Half-Step Domain Ancestor was that his body contained a trace of Domain Ancestor aura. This was the signature proof of identity of a Half-Step Domain Ancestor.

Chapter 1156: Forging a Forbidden Weapon, the Heaven-Slaying Spear

!【Sixth Update】

The fusion of the Forbidden Dao and the Endless Great Dao was not particularly difficult. One only needed to wrap both the Forbidden Dao and the Endless Great Dao with the power of origin and merge them together. This process, however, consumed an enormous amount of origin power.

But once it succeeded, the origin power contained within Ye Tian’s pinnacle Dao source would also transform into forbidden origin power.

At that time, the speed at which Ye Tian tempered his forbidden body would increase greatly. He could even use forbidden origin power to temper it, making the process countless times faster than before. There was even hope that before becoming a Dao Ancestor, he could temper his forbidden body to the level of sixty-nine percent.

Once he broke through to the Dao Ancestor realm, the tempering level of his forbidden body would also surge by a large margin, directly breaking through the bottleneck from minor completion to major completion, and pushing his forbidden body straight into the major completion stage—perhaps even directly close to eighty percent.

What kind of concept was that? Some half-step Domain Ancestors had only just reached major completion in their forbidden body cultivation. One could imagine just how heaven-defying it was for a pinnacle Dao Ancestor to fuse with the Forbidden Dao.

But Ye Tian’s experience was almost impossible to replicate, so others could only envy him in vain.

In order to speed up the fusion of the Forbidden Dao and the Endless Great Dao, Ye Tian paid a huge price to set up a hundred-thousandfold time acceleration array, using forbidden objects as the cost 21 to establish this time formation. He only needed to replenish the forbidden objects regularly.

This consumed forbidden objects at a shocking rate, but Ye Tian had plenty of them on him, so there was no reason not to use them.

And so, day after day within the hundred-thousandfold time formation, Ye Tian used origin power to promote the compatibility and fusion of the Forbidden Dao and the Endless Great Dao.

One year in the outside world meant one hundred thousand years inside the time formation; it was almost as though one-thousandth was fused each year, %.

Finally, after a thousand years had passed in the outside world, Ye Tian at last completed the fusion of the Forbidden Dao and the Endless Great Dao.

Originally, Ye Tian’s forbidden body had remained at the sixty percent level, but now it quickly broke into the progress of sixty-one percent.

His forbidden body was continuously tempered, and the improvement effect far surpassed anything from before.

Unfortunately, Ye Tian’s True Ancestor power, physical body power, and soul power had already reached the limit of a pinnacle True Ancestor, so they could no longer improve.

But to his astonishment, Ye Tian discovered that his soul was becoming more and more solid, and was even imbued with forbidden attributes.

In this way, it would become much more difficult for others to annihilate his soul—unless the difference in strength was truly too great.

This transformation lasted a full ten years before finally coming to an end.

Xuanxu Ancient Realm, the Fireflame Forbidden Land.

Ye Tian muttered.

As it happened, he had previously obtained a rod-type forbidden treasure, and it was the best possible embryo for a forbidden weapon.

Originally, he had wanted to forge a saber, but a rod-type forbidden treasure was most suitable for forging a spear-type weapon.

Supreme Saber Dao, pinnacle Sword Dao, pinnacle Spear Dao... and so on... all Great Daos were merely derivative branches evolved from the Forbidden Dao.

Therefore, for Ye Tian, whether he used a spear or a saber would have no effect whatsoever on his strength.

Yet how long had it been, and now he was proposing that they submit to other forces? If they had known it would turn out like this, they should have pledged allegiance from the start—at least then they could have gained quite a few benefits.

If they submitted now, leaving aside whether those forces would even accept them, even if they did, there would basically be no favorable treatment at all.

“Dao Ancestor Xutian, back then it was you who insisted on not joining any force, and that’s why we followed you in forming the Pantheon. Now you’re saying this—are you trying to abandon the Pantheon? It sounds like two suggestions, but really it’s just one suggestion: to submit to another force!”

Dao Ancestor Goldsilver sneered.

“Dao Ancestor Goldsilver, what do you mean by that? I was the one who advocated establishing the Pantheon, yes, but didn’t all of you fail to object as well? And now that something has gone wrong, you want to push all the responsibility onto me?”

Dao Ancestor Xutian was enraged as well.

As Dao Ancestor Xutian and Dao Ancestor Goldsilver argued heatedly, Dao Ancestor Battle Axe spoke up to persuade them, “Everyone, calm down. Don’t argue anymore! How about this—let’s put it to a vote. Should we dissolve the Pantheon, or continue maintaining it? Once it’s dissolved, what each force does next will be its own business!”

“Fine, let’s vote. I agree!”

Dao Ancestor Xutian nodded.

Immediately, the Dao Ancestors began voting one by one.

Before long, the vote was over.

Nearly ninety percent of the Dao Ancestors agreed to dissolve the Pantheon. Clearly, no one had much confidence in its future anymore, or perhaps they had already decided in their hearts to submit to some other force.

“Then let it be dissolved!”

Dao Ancestor Xutian let out a sigh.

And just like that, the Pantheon, an alliance force that had not been established for very long, was dissolved.

Not long afterward, the other alliance forces in the Daoshan Realm also disbanded one after another. At this point, the power structure of the Daoshan Realm had effectively collapsed.

After some more time passed—roughly around a hundred years later—

one force after another submitted to the upper three heaven-level forces. In the last great war at the Huoyan Forbidden Land, the upper three heaven-level forces had lost too many True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors, so they urgently needed to expand their strength, and thus they accepted those forces that came to submit.

Of course, they paid no price for this and gave no benefits at all. They even accepted tribute from those forces instead.

Xutian True Nation, Human Race.

Dao Ancestor Xutian’s avatar descended once again and arrived at Ye Tian’s residence.

At this meeting, Dao Ancestor Xutian discovered that he could no longer see through this disciple of his. It was as though the other party’s strength had already reached a very high level.

He knew that his disciple was now no weaker than a Fourth Heaven Dao Ancestor, and his strength was gradually closing in on his own.

“Master!”

Ye Tian still remained extremely respectful toward Dao Ancestor Xutian and hurriedly came forward to receive him.

“Disciple, I came to see you this time because of something!”

Dao Ancestor Xutian said somewhat awkwardly.

“What is it?”

Ye Tian asked curiously.

“The Pantheon has disbanded. I want to bring the Xutian lineage into Black Wind Mountain!”

Dao Ancestor Xutian said: “.

But I don’t know the Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain, nor can I contact them, while you are a Heavenly General of Black Wind Mountain, with status second only to the Ten Kings, so I want to ask you to help speak to the kings of Black Wind Mountain!”

“Join Black Wind Mountain?”

Ye Tian frowned.

This would not be easy to handle, because up to now Black Wind Mountain had not taken in a single subordinate force. It was all the peak masters and generals recruiting members themselves to develop Black Wind Mountain, or else recruiting talents through the various inheritance grounds of Black Wind Mountain.

Therefore.

He also did not know whether King Wind and the others would be willing to accept the Xutian lineage. If King Wind disagreed, there was nothing he could do.

“Disciple, your master truly has no other choice. Once the Ancient Realm is born and the Dao Ancestors are no longer restricted, I fear quite a few upper three heaven-level forces will seek to eliminate me!”

Dao Ancestor Xutian said worriedly.

“Master, I’ll go discuss it with King Wind!”

Ye Tian said at once.

“Good!”

Dao Ancestor Xutian nodded.

Afterward.

Ye Tian arranged for this avatar of Dao Ancestor Xutian to stay among the human race, while he personally entered King Wind’s minor realm and used the Heavenly General token to contact King Wind.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly General, why have you contacted me?”

King Wind’s voice spread all around Ye Tian.

“King Wind, my master, Dao Ancestor Xutian, wishes to bring the Xutian lineage into Black Wind Mountain. May Black Wind Mountain accept them?”

Ye Tian explained.

“Black Wind Mountain does not accept subordinate forces, as they are too difficult to manage!”

King Wind replied.

“Is there no other way?”

Ye Tian frowned.

At this moment, King Wind fell silent for a moment, then said, “There is still one method. Let Dao Ancestor Xutian join Black Wind Mountain and become one of the Heavenly Kings, while the members of the Xutian lineage are placed into a legion under his command. In that way, they would also count as members of Black Wind Mountain! However, the name ‘Xutian lineage’ would be abolished from then on, and they could only be called the Xutian Legion! If he is willing, then I will agree to let him join Black Wind Mountain. If he is unwilling, then we will not accept him!”

“Many thanks, King Wind!”

Ye Tian also knew that this was the greatest concession King Wind could make, and so he left King Wind’s minor realm.

Chapter 1158: The Void Heaven Legion!

Chapter 1158: The Void Heaven Legion

!【Eighth Update】

Human Race.

After Ye Tian returned, he contacted Void Heaven Dao Ancestor and met him once again.

“Master, King Feng has given his reply!”

Ye Tian said unhurriedly, “King Feng said that Black Wind Mountain does not accept subordinate factions. If the Void Heaven lineage wishes to join Black Wind Mountain, there is only one way: Master must become one of Black Wind Mountain’s Heavenly Kings, and the Void Heaven lineage will become one of Black Wind Mountain’s legions under the name Void Heaven Legion, directly under your command!”

Void Heaven Dao Ancestor’s face turned pale, and he quickly asked, “Does that mean the Void Heaven lineage will exist in name only, and can only act under the identity of the Void Heaven Legion?”

“Yes!”

Ye Tian nodded.

“Can I think about it for a while?”

Void Heaven Dao Ancestor said in conflict.

“Master can go back and think it over slowly. If you come to a decision, then inform your disciple!”

Ye Tian did not urge Void Heaven Dao Ancestor, because this was all he could do. If Void Heaven Dao Ancestor truly was unwilling, there was nothing he could do about it.

He also understood very clearly that it was extremely difficult for Void Heaven Dao Ancestor to make this choice.

After all, before today, he had still been the leader of a major power. For him to become merely one of the ordinary upper echelons of another major power, while his own faction instantly dissolved and no longer retained its name, was naturally something he could not accept all at once.

Void Heaven Dao Ancestor’s avatar did not disperse and stayed among the humans, thinking it over slowly.

Days passed one after another.

A full three months went by before Void Heaven Dao Ancestor finally made his decision.

“Disciple, I am willing to join Black Wind Mountain!”

Void Heaven Dao Ancestor sighed.

He also knew he had to make this choice. His relationship with the other Upper Triple Heaven forces was not very good, so joining Black Wind Mountain was the best option.

If he did not join, then when those Upper Triple Heaven forces came in the future, he would not be able to stop them at all, and might even die and have his Dao vanish.

But if he joined Black Wind Mountain, with its protection, he could not say for sure about other things, but his safety would at least be sufficiently guaranteed. As long as he did not court death himself, it would not be easy for him to die.

Of course, if he insisted on fighting over opportunities and got killed by others, then it could only be said that his strength was insufficient.

Now that Void Heaven Dao Ancestor had agreed, the rest was simple.

King Feng’s consciousness avatar appeared and personally tested Void Heaven Dao Ancestor. After a simple assessment, Void Heaven Dao Ancestor successfully passed and became one of Black Wind Mountain’s Heavenly Kings, with a status roughly equal to Ye Tian’s.

Void Heaven Dao Ancestor originally wanted the other Dao Ancestors of the Void Heaven lineage to become Heavenly Kings as well, but unfortunately their strength did not meet the standard. After all, Black Wind Mountain’s standards for Heavenly Kings were extremely high.

Therefore, those Dao Ancestors of the Void Heaven lineage could only be reduced to positions such as deputy legion commanders and other posts under the Void Heaven Legion.

Soon after, Void Heaven Dao Ancestor announced to the outside world that he had joined Black Wind Mountain, and the Void Heaven lineage was officially renamed the Void Heaven Legion.

This news was transmitted to the Void Heaven Hall of the Void Heaven True Kingdom and also sent back to the Void Heaven Realm.

At first, quite a few people opposed it, but those who opposed it were suppressed.

Gradually, the Dao Ancestors and True Lords of the Void Heaven lineage all accepted their identities as members of a legion.

Not long after.

Quite a few True Ancestors of the Void Heaven Legion moved into the Fire King Minor Domain and were assigned to a certain space there, which was now the Void Heaven Space.

The Void Heaven Legion was undoubtedly very powerful, and it controlled an enormous True Kingdom that could provide Black Wind Mountain with a large number of geniuses. Thus, the appearance of the Void Heaven Legion brought many benefits to Black Wind Mountain.

The Upper Triple Heaven forces had little reaction to the matter of the Void Heaven Legion. After all, the Void Heaven lineage was, at most, only a Fifth Heaven-level force. Why would they pay attention to the Void Heaven lineage? At most, a few True Ancestors discussed it privately, but it was not enough to attract the attention of those Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors and pinnacle Dao Ancestors.

In the blink of an eye.

The Void Heaven Legion’s move into Black Wind Mountain had already stabilized, and Void Heaven Dao Ancestor had gradually accepted the fact that he had become a Heavenly King of Black Wind Mountain.

However.

The Mysterious Void Ancient Realm had still not transformed into an Ancient Realm, so Void Heaven Dao Ancestor and the other Dao Ancestors still could not enter it. Normally, they could only enter Black Wind Mountain with avatars to handle certain matters.

As time passed, Ye Tian’s cultivation gradually entered a bottleneck as well, because he had already reached the absolute limit of a Pinnacle True Ancestor.

“My Forbidden Body has been tempered to sixty-nine percent. Sure enough, it can no longer be tempered by even the slightest bit!”

Ye Tian muttered.

At his current level, he truly could advance no further. No matter how heaven-defying he was, he could not break through this bottleneck, because a Pinnacle True Ancestor was already... the ultimate limit of the True Ancestor realm. He still had no way to open up an entirely new True Ancestor realm above the level of Pinnacle True Ancestor.

If he were really that incredible, then he could probably change the rules of the Dark Forbidden Domain with a single word and set the rules himself! ....After Ye Tian’s strength reached the ultimate limit of a Pinnacle True Ancestor, he rarely cultivated anymore. Instead, he turned to teaching his son and daughter, while also guiding his wife and younger sister in cultivation so that they could continuously improve their strength.

Under Ye Tian’s unremitting efforts, Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue both stepped into the combat power of Invincible Dao Ancestors, while Xiao Yue and Ye Yu steadily advanced toward the ultimate limit of Invincible True Ancestors. However, this step was extremely, extremely difficult.

Ye Yu also obtained a Dao-level innate talent after receiving a single Natal Talent Fruit from Ye Xingyue, but obtaining a Dao-level innate talent did not mean one could step into the ultimate limit of an Invincible Dao Ancestor.

The ultimate limit of an Invincible Dao Ancestor was an extremely difficult level to reach. Among the countless Invincible True Ancestors in the Mysterious Void Ancient Realm, only a few had advanced to that level.

However.

In the years that followed, Ye Tian used the excuse that he had obtained some pinnacle treasure and fooled Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, Xiao Yue, and the others into refining this treasure, saying that it could grant them Dao-level innate talents, while in reality he secretly bestowed Dao-level innate talents upon them.

Under such circumstances, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, Xiao Yue, and Ye Yu all obtained Dao-level innate talents that suited them extremely well.

With multiple Dao-level innate talents, they cultivated one Middle Thousand Dao Technique after another with almost no flaws. Coupled with the continuous tempering of their Forbidden Bodies, their combat strength improved at an astonishing pace.

One hundred thousand years! One million years! Finally, another three million years passed in the Mysterious Void Ancient Realm.

By this time, Ye Xingchen had reached top-tier Invincible Dao Ancestor combat power, Ye Xingyue had also reached top-tier Invincible Dao Ancestor combat power, Ye Yu had reached top-tier Invincible Dao Ancestor combat power, and Xiao Yue had the greatest combat strength of them all. After all, she had received Ye Tian’s special care, with endless resources supplied to her, and thus she directly stepped into the ultimate limit of Invincible Dao Ancestor combat power.

Perhaps if Xiao Yue were given a single opportunity, she could step into the ranks of Pinnacle True Ancestors, because her bottleneck had long since been broken by the Heavenly Forbidden Tree Core, and her hope of reaching the Pinnacle True Ancestor realm was extremely great.

On this day.

In the Dao Mountain Realm, one chaotic region after another was occupied by the forces of the Upper Three Heavens, where they established branch divisions and handed them over to their subordinate forces for management.

After all, the Dao Mountain Realm was simply too vast. The Dao Ancestors of the Upper Three Heavens forces had no way to manage it all. Even if one True Ancestor were assigned to manage each Chaos Continent, sending out every single True Ancestor still would not be enough to govern all the Chaos Continents.

Besides that, the Dao Mountain Realm also contained a huge number of Dao Realms, Great Universes, ordinary universes, and all kinds of special worlds, treasure lands, forbidden zones, and so on....

So at a time like this, subordinate forces became useful, managing things on their behalf and periodically handing over a portion of geniuses and resources.

Faced with the overwhelming might of the Upper Three Heavens forces, many major factions in the Dao Mountain Realm did not dare resist at all. If the force they relied on was strong enough, they could still preserve part of their territory. But if the backing force was not strong enough, they could only hand over their ter“0.4.7”

ritory.

Moreover, the Upper Three Heavens forces were also in competition with one another, and many times they had to fight a battle before they could occupy a chaotic territory.

Of course, to the Upper Three Heavens forces, the Mysterious Void Ancient World was the truly most precious world. The territory here was incomparably valuable, practically worth its weight in gold inch for inch. Any random planet here was more valuable than a Chaos Continent within the Chaos.

This time, Black Wind Mountain had also stepped into the open and occupied one territory after another, each managed by a peak master or a general. Their legions were stationed there in peacetime, so the upper echelon of Black Wind Mountain did not need to worry about it.

It was worth mentioning that the human race led their people out of the Xutian True Nation.

For the human race, the Xutian True Nation was still a little too small at present.

In a territory not too far from the Xutian True Nation, Ye Tian chose a region dozens of times larger than the Xutian True Nation and directly declared it occupied. With Black Wind Mountain at his back, hardly anyone dared provoke him.

Besides, the place he occupied was not large at all in the context of the entire Mysterious Void Ancient World—it was... nothing more than a tiny patch of land, so no one cared.

The human race had a large number of True Ancestors, so Ye Tian did not need to concern himself with the migration work.

At this moment.

Ye Tian announced to his family that he was entering seclusion.

Ye Tian was going to charge toward the Dao Ancestor realm, while his family also needed to increase their strength and strive to step into the ranks of Pinnacle True Ancestors.

On this day.

After refining a large amount of Primordial Chaos Origin Qi, Xiao Yue’s origin was elevated, and her body was tempered by the Primordial Chaos Origin Qi. It was... this very bit of improvement that allowed her to completely shatter the shackles, directly give birth to a pinnacle Dao origin, and step into the ranks of Pinnacle True Ancestors.

As soon as Xiao Yue broke through, Ye Tian learned of it immediately.

He was not surprised in the slightest. After all, Xiao Yue had no bottleneck. She only needed a slight increase in strength to break the shackles and advance to become a Pinnacle True Ancestor. If she had failed to break through, that would have been strange! As for Ye Yu, Ye Xingchen, and Ye Xingyue, if they wanted to break through to Pinnacle True Ancestor, they would probably still need quite a bit of time. Primordial Chaos Origin Qi could only help them strengthen their origin and raise their foundation a little; in the short term, there was no way it could help them step into the ranks of Pinnacle True Ancestors.

“Time to begin the breakthrough!”

Ye Tian gathered his mind and no longer paid attention to external matters, focusing wholeheartedly on breaking through to the Dao Ancestor realm.

For a True Ancestor to step into Dao Ancestor meant... merging with the Dao. He had long since unified essence, qi, and spirit, so merging with the Dao was not difficult for him. It could even be said to be extremely easy.

Therefore, he had to cultivate a Dao-merging secret art! The so-called Dao-merging secret art was... to fuse the soul, body, and True Ancestor power into a single point, making them perfectly one, and then merge that with one’s own Great Dao to completely reconstruct the body.

At that point, one’s very self would be the Great Dao! And what Ye Tian needed was to merge with the Endless Forbidden Dao, so that every movement he made would be a manifestation of the Endless Forbidden Dao—he would become the incarnation of the Endless Forbidden Dao! Of course, the Dao-merging secret art had to be flawless and perfect, without any errors or defects, or else the foundation would be unstable.

The reason why the Dao Ancestors of places like the Forbidden Hall within the Dao Mountain Realm had unstable foundations and flawed origins was because the Dao-merging secret art passed down by the Dao Mountain Dao Ancestor was either incomplete or deeply defective. Although it could still allow a True Ancestor to merge with the Dao and become a Dao Ancestor, the flaws were far too great.

It was only after a very long span of time that the many Dao Ancestors of the Dao Mountain Realm gradually perfected the Dao-merging secret art. It could not be called completely flawless, but it no longer had any major defects.

As for the Dao-merging secret art Ye Tian was cultivating now, it came from Black Wind Mountain. It was the most flawless Dao-merging secret art, with no problems whatsoever, and it could use Dark Forbidden Power as the medium for Dao merging. It could even allow True Ancestors who were unable to master Dark Forbidden Power to possess a trace of forbidden attribute after merging with the Dao... This was the most perfect Dao-merging method! Boom! The Dao-merging secret art began to operate—Ye Tian’s body, soul, and True Ancestor power seemed to be absorbed by a certain point inside his body, and in a short time his entire body transformed into a black dot. At the same time, the three forces of essence, qi, and spirit began trying to fuse together.

Other people would be stuck at this step and need external objects to accomplish it, but Ye Tian had already fully completed it long ago.

As Ye Tian continuously operated the Dao-merging secret art, the forbidden dao stones and a small piece of forbidden mother stone that had long been arranged around the secluded cultivation chamber were drawn in by the Dao-merging secret art, transforming into incomparably pure Dark Forbidden Power that poured into that black dot.

Using the purest Dark Forbidden Power to merge with the Dao and establish his foundation, once Ye Tian successfully merged with the Dao, not only would his Dao Ancestor power become exceptionally pure forbidden dao power, even his soul and body would become: incomparably powerful, with an incomparably deep foundation.

For others, using Dark Forbidden Power to merge with the Dao and establish a foundation was very dangerous, but for Ye Tian, who had mastered Dark Forbidden Power, this method of foundation-building was extremely safe.

After a long time, that unified point began to expand and transform into a humanoid form, beginning to reconstruct a Dao Ancestor body, also known as a Great Dao body! Blood, bones, the five viscera and six bowels, skin, hair.... one bodily component after another condensed into being, making Ye Tian become: flawless and perfect, as though he were a creation of heaven and earth2.

2, the most perfect body wrought by creation.

At the same time, Ye Tian’s aura also grew stronger and stronger, as countless strands of forbidden origin power surged forth, tempering Ye Tian’s Great Dao body.

Soon, a large amount of forbidden dao power was born within Ye Tian’s body, and his soul also became incomparably solid, containing powerful forbidden attributes. His forbidden body instantly shattered its shackles as well, being tempered to the major accomplishment realm, and was still: rapidly rising.

No one knew how much time had passed before Ye Tian’s realm finally stabilized.

Chapter 1161: The Heavenly Emperor Palace Appears

Ye Tian murmured.

Moreover, he was not the kind of... newly advanced Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestor, but one of the absolute top Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestors, far, far stronger than before.

More importantly, he possessed a perfected forbidden body. Even if he were to fight several top Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestors alone, he would not fear them in the slightest, and he could even preserve his life against an ordinary Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor.

Besides, he had only just advanced to the Dao Ancestor realm, so his strength would definitely surge greatly in a short time.

For example, casually cultivating a Grand Dao Art, or cultivating a Dao Ancestor-level technique, and so on....

In short, as long as he was given.... a little more time, he would be able to easily break into the Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor realm.

At the same time.

In the Xuanxu Ancient World, a great many True Ancestors successively broke through into the Dao Ancestor realm.

With the rules no longer restricting them, as long as the True Ancestors were confident in advancing to Dao Ancestors, they could go ahead and do so.

Although, after the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s repeated schemes, a great many True Ancestors throughout the Xuanxu Ancient World had fallen, there were still quite a few who had reached the standard for advancement.

However, some True Ancestors succeeded in advancing, while others failed.

The Human Race.

After a period of migration, the Human Race had basically settled into a brand-new territory, a territory that completely belonged to the Human Race.

Moreover, the Human Race had also given birth to several Dao Ancestors.

After all, not everyone aimed to advance into a top True Ancestor, a pinnacle True Ancestor, or an invincible True Ancestor. Many people lacked resources, and their talent was only average. After reaching the peak of Great Dao cultivation, they began trying to merge with the Dao.

Under such circumstances, it was only natural for the Human Race to produce a few lucky ones who succeeded in merging with the Dao in one fell swoop.

And as time passed, the number of Dao Ancestors in the Human Race would inevitably grow greater and greater.

However, Ye Tian had very strict requirements for the Nine Extremes Legion: anyone who could not reach the level of a pinnacle Dao Ancestor should not even try to advance to Dao Ancestor.

Pinnacle Dao Ancestor was the minimum requirement he set for those genius Dao Ancestors in the Nine Extremes Legion. If someone could advance to an invincible Dao Ancestor first and then attempt to break through to Dao Ancestor, that would naturally be even better, but that... kind of difficulty was far too great.

In the blink of an eye, a thousand years passed.

The Xuanxu Ancient World had long since initially stabilized, and large amounts of ownerless territory had been divided up among the various forces.

And because many fragments of world realms had been fused into the Xuanxu Ancient World and transformed into ancient continents, many sects had also moved from their various relic spaces onto the ancient continents of the Xuanxu Ancient World, recruiting geniuses from the entire Xuanxu Ancient World.

The Xuanxu Ancient World had gradually taken on a bit of the atmosphere of a realm domain, and was even developing in that direction.

In addition, the Xuanxu Ancient World also continued the vast power classification system, dividing powers from First Heaven to Ninth Heaven. If a force did not meet the standard of a First Heaven force, then it would be unable to occupy territory and would be limited to the various starry-sky continents, certain stars, and worlds.

Those native forces of the Daoshan Realm Domain were basically classified as Second Heaven and Third Heaven forces. The Star-Horn Beast Clan was classified as a Fifth Heaven force, and the Forbidden Hall was also classified as a Fifth Heaven force.

Unfortunately, among the original forces of the Daoshan Realm Domain, not a single force had been classified as a Sixth Heaven force, because at present, the original forces of the Daoshan Realm Domain did not have even one Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor.

Of course.

The forces from the Vast Sea Realm Domain were also basically considered to have merged into the Daoshan Realm Domain, and could no longer be regarded as forces of the Shentian Realm Domain. Everyone no longer really distinguished between each other.

“Today, the Heavenly Emperor Palace appears!”

Secondly, one Emperor Lord after another stood around the Heavenly Emperor Palace, their invincible figures seeming to stand within time and space itself. There were dozens of them in total, and such a terrifying number left countless forces dumbfounded.

This meant that the Heavenly Emperor Palace possessed at least dozens of invincible Dao Ancestors, while those three Ninth Heaven forces had at most only a few invincible Dao Ancestors. As for Black Wind Mountain, the number of its invincible Dao Ancestors was unclear, but it certainly would not be too many.

After all, invincible Dao Ancestors were not... so easy to break into. For a Dao Ancestor to elevate their own Great Dao to the utmost extreme and thereby sublimate into the invincible Dao Ancestor realm was inevitably an incomparably difficult task.

Secondly, the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s Heavenly Army appeared! The true Heavenly Army of the Heavenly Emperor Palace was composed of Dao Ancestors: First Heaven to Third Heaven Dao Ancestors served as soldiers, Fourth Heaven Dao Ancestors served as squad captains, Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestors served as regiment commanders, and pinnacle Dao Ancestors served as army commanders.

And Heavenly Army was a general term, not the name of a single legion.

Each legion had one hundred thousand members, representing one hundred thousand Dao Ancestors. Ten 10 legions meant a total of 1 million Dao Ancestors.

Seeing so many Dao Ancestors, not a single person was not shocked. Even Ye Tian’s pupils contracted as he finally understood the power of the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

“No wonder the Heavenly Emperor Palace isn’t panicking at all. It keeps scheming others to death and isn’t afraid in the slightest. So its strength has already reached this level. No wonder back in the Vast Sea Realm Domain, not a single force dared provoke the Heavenly Emperor Palace.”

Ye Tian murmured.

Now, although the Vast Sea Domain Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace was absent, with this level of strength, probably no one would dare provoke the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Of course, the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s prestige was certainly much weaker than before.

They might not show it on the surface, but in secret they were probably grinding their teeth in hatred, and perhaps one day they would retaliate against the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

After displaying its strength, the Heavenly Emperor Palace made no major moves and only announced one heavenly rule.

All Ninth Heaven forces must offer up some resources to the Heavenly Emperor Palace, and geniuses from any place in the Xuanxu Ancient World could choose to join the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s reserve army and genius training camp.

Back then, the Heavenly Emperor Palace collected tributes in the Vast Sea Domain Realm. But the Vast Sea Domain Realm belonged to both the Vast Sea Domain Ancestor and the Heavenly Emperor Palace, so when the Heavenly Emperor Palace collected tribute, no one dared object, nor did anyone say anything.

But now, this was the Profound Void Ancient Realm, and the Heavenly Emperor Palace still wanted to act the same way. How could the other factions be willing? Boom!!!! A consciousness incarnation of a Half-Step Domain Ancestor descended, approaching the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

This... Half-Step Domain Ancestor was none other than Zhenyu Dao Ancestor! “Palace Master Azure Dragon, your Heavenly Emperor Palace is being far too overbearing. On what grounds should we offer up resources? This is the Profound Void Ancient Realm, not the Vast Sea Domain Realm!”

Zhenyu Dao Ancestor said coldly.

Swish! Palace Master Azure Dragon appeared and sneered, “What, you were once under the jurisdiction of our Heavenly Emperor Palace, and now that you’ve come to the Daoshan Boundary, you want to break away from us? As for on what grounds, let me tell you—what the Heavenly Emperor Palace relies on is strength!”

Zhenyu Dao Ancestor said with a smile, “I admit that your Heavenly Emperor Palace is far stronger than Ninth Heaven-level forces, but without a Domain Ancestor, you can no longer be considered a legendary-level force.

Your Heavenly Emperor Palace currently has only three Half-Step Domain Ancestors, but in the Profound Void Ancient Realm, besides your Heavenly Emperor Palace, there are more than just three Half-Step Domain Ancestors!”

He was threatening the Heavenly Emperor Palace: if they enraged everyone, and all the Half-Step Domain Ancestors joined forces, the Heavenly Emperor Palace would not be able to withstand them.

“Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, are you threatening me?”

Palace Master Azure Dragon said coldly.

“I wouldn’t dare!”

Zhenyu Dao Ancestor cupped his hands slightly. “I am merely explaining the pros and cons to Palace Master Azure Dragon. I have no intention of threatening the Heavenly Emperor Palace!”

“You think our Heavenly Emperor Palace can’t kill you?”

Palace Master Azure Dragon was furious. Since when had a mere Half-Step Domain Ancestor dared threaten the Heavenly Emperor Palace? “The Heavenly Emperor Palace certainly has the ability to kill me, but can it kill all three of us Half-Step Domain Ancestors?”

As soon as Zhenyu Dao Ancestor finished speaking, two more auras of Half-Step Domain Ancestors emerged.

Swish swish!!!! Two incarnations of Half-Step Domain Ancestors descended and arrived before the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

These two were respectively the Half-Step Domain Ancestor of Mitian Sect—Migu Dao Ancestor—and the Half-Step Domain Ancestor of Tianhai Sect—Tianfan Dao Ancestor! Palace Master Azure Dragon stared carefully at Migu Dao Ancestor and Tianfan Dao Ancestor, and quickly recognized them as well.

“Migu Dao Ancestor, Tianfan Dao Ancestor—I didn’t expect the two of you to have stepped into the Half-Step Domain Ancestor realm as well!”

Palace Master Azure Dragon was somewhat surprised.

At this moment, he finally understood why Zhenyu Dao Ancestor had become so confident. Back when Zhenyu Dao Ancestor had encountered Palace Master Zhenwu, he had not been nearly so bold.

Now, Zhenyu Dao Ancestor had reached some kind of cooperative agreement with Migu Dao Ancestor and Tianfan Dao Ancestor. The three Half-Step Domain Ancestors had joined forces to oppose the three great palace masters of the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

“Interesting. You think that just because your number of Half-Step Domain Ancestors matches that of our Heavenly Emperor Palace, you can contend against us? Today, I’ll let you understand that not all Half-Step Domain Ancestors are the same!”

“I alone am enough to suppress the three of you!”

Palace Master Azure Dragon shouted coldly.

Boom! The aura belonging to a Half-Step Domain Ancestor erupted wildly, instantly shattering the incarnations of Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, Migu Dao Ancestor, and Tianfan Dao Ancestor, then swept toward the true bodies of the three Half-Step Domain Ancestors.

Rumble!!!! Migu Dao Ancestor, Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, and Tianfan Dao Ancestor all stepped out from within their sects in person and began fighting Palace Master Azure Dragon in the endless void.

They also wanted to know just how powerful Palace Master Azure Dragon, who had not made a move for endless ages, truly was.

And this battle drew far too many Dao Ancestors to observe. As for True Ancestor-level beings—sorry, they were not even qualified to spectate.

If a True Ancestor dared observe a battle of this level, even a mere wisp of aura could ignore distance across time and space and injure them. Only Pinnacle True Ancestors were qualified to watch such a great battle.

Zhenyu Dao Ancestor and the others had originally thought that with three against one, they would hold the advantage, but they discovered they were wrong.

Just as Palace Master Azure Dragon had said, there were differences even among Half-Step Domain Ancestors.

“A ninety-percent forbidden body—how did you achieve that?”

Zhenyu Dao Ancestor stared in disbelief at Palace Master Azure Dragon, who was continuously fighting while activating his ninety-percent forbidden body, and exclaimed in shock.

Although the three of them also possessed perfected forbidden bodies, they had only tempered theirs to a little over eighty percent. It was not that they did not want to continue tempering them, but that it was simply far too difficult.

After tempering their forbidden bodies to just over eighty percent, it was as if they had fallen into a bottleneck. No matter how many... forbidden wonders or even forbidden treasures they refined, they had no way to continue tempering their forbidden bodies.

Yet Palace Master Azure Dragon had actually tempered his forbidden body to ninety percent. How heaven-defying was that?! “Ignorant fools. How could the foundation of our Heavenly Emperor Palace be something you can imagine?”

Palace Master Azure Dragon mocked.

Palace Master Azure Dragon’s power was not limited to his ninety-percent forbidden body. The forbidden Dao power throughout his entire body was also incomparably pure, as if it had already been completely transformed into dark forbidden power.

In addition, Palace Master Azure Dragon had mastered many forbidden Dao arts, and his comprehension of the Forbidden Dao was also extremely profound, far beyond that of experts who had only just entered the Half-Step Domain Ancestor realm.

Although Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, Migu Dao Ancestor, and Tianfan Dao Ancestor were not newly advanced Half-Step Domain Ancestors, compared to Palace Master Azure Dragon, they were still far too immature.

Battles between Half-Step Domain Ancestors were not especially flashy. What they had was merely close-quarters combat, where every casual strike was a perfect application of forbidden power, far surpassing those so-called pinnacle Dao arts.

Ye Tian was also observing this battle and was utterly captivated. Those combat techniques seemed to transcend the Great Dao, transcend everything.

It had to be said that compared to these Half-Step Domain Ancestors, the gap between him and them was truly enormous—not a gap in strength, but a gap in realm.

Boom! Palace Master Azure Dragon sent Zhenyu Dao Ancestor flying with a punch, then kicked Migu Dao Ancestor away, and with a collision of his body, directly smashed Tianfan Dao Ancestor flying across countless territories.

The battle among the four Half-Step Domain Ancestors gradually entered the spacetime turbulent flow, where they stirred up one spacetime storm after another.

And by this point, even fewer people were able to enter the spacetime turbulent flow to observe; basically, only relatively powerful Dao Ancestors could do so.

As time passed, Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, Migu Dao Ancestor, and Tianfan Dao Ancestor unexpectedly began to suffer injuries, which was enough to prove that Palace Master Azure Dragon truly possessed the strength to kill them one-on-one.

Of course, if Palace Master Azure Dragon wanted to kill any one of those Half-Step Domain Ancestors, it would still be rather difficult. Half-Step Domain Ancestors were not so easy to kill.

Suddenly.

Zhenyu Dao Ancestor took out his forbidden weapon, which was impressively a top-grade forbidden weapon.

Migu Dao Ancestor and Tianfan Dao Ancestor were no exception; they too brought out forbidden weapons, both ranked among the top grade. spoon.

Once the three great Half-Step Domain Ancestors used top-grade forbidden weapons, their strength surged by a level, and at once they were able to contend with Palace Master Azure Dragon.

“.

Heh, you think you’re the only ones with forbidden weapons?”

Palace Master Azure Dragon sneered.

Immediately, he drew a sword that carried the aura of a Domain Ancestor.

The moment this sword appeared, Zhenyu Dao Ancestor, Migu Dao Ancestor, and Tianfan Dao Ancestor all changed expression and cried out in unison, “A half-domain weapon!!!!”
