Chapter 1163: The First Generation Time King and Space King

!【Fourth Update】

Strictly speaking, a semi-domain weapon was also a kind of forbidden weapon, but it surpassed top-tier forbidden weapons while still falling short of a true domain weapon.

Even so, semi-domain weapons were extremely precious. They could unleash a trace of a Domain Ancestor’s might, and the boost they gave to combat power was terrifying.

In addition, semi-domain weapons were incredibly sharp, easily capable of piercing an ordinary forbidden body.

Then they saw the Azure Dragon Palace Master holding the semi-domain weapon Azure Dragon Sword, casually thrusting a sword toward Ancestor Dao Zhenyu. No matter how powerful Ancestor Dao Zhenyu’s defensive forbidden Dao arts were, they were still pierced through by this strike, which then also pierced his body.

This sword strike had injured him, and not lightly! With the Azure Dragon Sword in hand, the Azure Dragon Palace Master’s combat power surged by a significant margin. He now truly possessed the means to kill a half-step Domain Ancestor—not by slowly wearing one down over time, but by directly slaying one head-on in a short period.

Even so, though the three half-step Domain Ancestors were besieging the Azure Dragon Palace Master, if this dragged on, all three of them might end up falling.

Ancestor Dao Zhenyu finally understood why the Azure Dragon Palace Master had been so confident. Even with the three of them arriving, the other party had never taken them seriously at all.

It turned out the gap in strength between the two sides really was enormous.

“Leave at once.

Withdraw, and agree to the demands of our Heavenly Emperor Palace. Otherwise, I won’t mind killing a half-step Domain Ancestor today!”

Palace Master Long threatened.

Ancestor Dao Zhenyu, Ancestor Dao Migu, and Ancestor Dao Tianfan all felt deeply conflicted. Back in the Vast Sea Domain Realm, with Vast Sea Domain Ancestor suppressing them from above, they had not dared act arrogantly in the slightest. They had not even dared show their faces, only hoping that one day they could break into the Domain Ancestor realm and stand on equal footing with Vast Sea Domain Ancestor.

But they had underestimated how difficult it was to become a Domain Ancestor, and even now they were still very far from that level.

They had thought that after arriving in the Daoshan Realm Domain, they could break free from the control of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, and from then on rule their own lives, stand above the rules, and become the ones moving the pieces on the board.

But to their utter surprise, they still could not defeat the Azure Dragon Palace Master and were still being threatened by him.

They were unwilling to accept it! In the Xuanxu Ancient Realm.

A great number of Dao Ancestors were observing this battle, and all of them were similarly shocked by the Azure Dragon Palace Master’s invincible battle strength. One man suppressing three half-step Domain Ancestors—what kind of overwhelming and terrifying power was this! “I didn’t expect that even the three half-step Domain Ancestors of the Mitian Sect, the Myriad Domain Divine Hall, and the Tianhai Sect would be unable to contend with the Azure Dragon Palace Master of the Heavenly Emperor Palace!”

Ye Tian muttered.

In that case, even if the Heavenly Emperor Palace had only three Palace Masters, no other force would be able to contend with it at all.

The only question was whether Black Wind Mountain would have a half-step Domain Ancestor step in this time.

Just as Ye Tian was thinking this, a change occurred in the battle within the spacetime turbulent flow.

Boom!!! The spacetime turbulent flow suddenly froze, as if someone had instantly frozen the spacetime here. Even the thoughts of many Dao Ancestors were frozen within the spacetime turbulent flow.

This sudden development caused many, many Dao Ancestors to panic, not understanding what exactly had happened.

But those… relatively powerful Dao Ancestors could all tell clearly that a half-step Domain Ancestor proficient in the Dao of time and space had made a move.

“The first-generation Time King and first-generation Space King of Black Wind Mountain—is it you two?”

the Azure Dragon Palace Master said sternly.

He could disregard the Myriad Domain Divine Hall, Mitian Sect, and Tianhai Sect, even view them as ants, but he could not afford not to take Black Wind Mountain seriously.

Because Black Wind Mountain was an outside force, and it had existed for far too long—so long that even its origins could not be traced.

In short, Black Wind Mountain was even older than the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Back when Vast Sea Domain Ancestor was still an Invincible Dao Ancestor, the first-generation Time King and first-generation Space King had already hidden themselves behind the scenes. At that time, no one even knew how many generations of kings Black Wind Mountain had already developed through.

But when Vast Sea Domain Ancestor became a half-step Domain Ancestor and fought for the position of Realm Lord, the Time King and Space King had also appeared. However, they were defeated by Vast Sea Domain Ancestor, severely injured, and fled. Their whereabouts became unknown.

Later, after Vast Sea Domain Ancestor took control of the Realm Lord position and used the resources of an entire domain realm to achieve the Domain Ancestor realm, he had originally intended to wipe out Black Wind Mountain and kill the Time King and Space King. But he was unable to sense the existence of Black Wind Mountain’s half-step Domain Ancestors.

Because he was wary of Black Wind Mountain’s mystery, and because Black Wind Mountain also did not stir up trouble and was not too great a threat, Vast Sea Domain Ancestor let Black Wind Mountain off.

But now, the Time King and Space King had appeared again.

Toward these two powerful half-step Domain Ancestors who had once fought Vast Sea Domain Ancestor, the Azure Dragon Palace Master had no choice but to take them seriously.

Originally, he had hoped that after these two left the Vast Sea Domain Realm, they had not followed the domain realm fragments to the Daoshan Realm Domain.

But his guess had been wrong. These two had really come! That made things extremely frightening. To be able to evade even Vast Sea Domain Ancestor’s detection meant that Black Wind Mountain’s strength was unfathomable.

Swish! Two figures walked out from the depths of the spacetime turbulent flow. They were not wearing masks, because they were no longer the Time King and Space King of Black Wind Mountain.

Black Wind Mountain’s Ten Kings would forever number only ten. Once one stepped down, one had to restore one’s original title.

“Azure Dragon Palace Master, you may call me Eternal Dao Ancestor!”

the first-generation Time King said.

“Azure Dragon Palace Master, you may call me Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor!”

the first-generation Space King said.

“Eternal Dao Ancestor, Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor, understood!”

The Azure Dragon Palace Master nodded slightly, then immediately asked, “Why have you two come here?”

Eternal Dao Ancestor said, “Nothing much. It’s just that the Heavenly Emperor Palace ordering all forces to hand over resources is somewhat excessive. I think the Heavenly Emperor Palace should revoke this rule. What does Azure Dragon Palace Master think?”

“Fine!”

the Azure Dragon Palace Master said with a smile. “But you must first defeat me. At that time, I’d like to see what the two who once contended with Vast Sea Domain Ancestor are capable of today.”

Dense battle intent erupted from the Azure Dragon Palace Master’s body, faintly carrying a trace of a Domain Ancestor’s bearing.

“I’ll fight the Azure Dragon Palace Master!”

Eternal Dao Ancestor said.

As soon as the words fell, Eternal Dao Ancestor and the Azure Dragon Palace Master clashed. The two of them wasted almost no words.

Rumble!!! The great battle set off the collapse of the spacetime turbulent flow. Section after section of the region broke apart, almost affecting the operation of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, causing the flow of time in many areas to begin changing.

The Azure Dragon Palace Master had the Azure Dragon Sword, but Eternal Dao Ancestor also had a semi-domain weapon—the Time Divine Eye! This Time Divine Eye had fused into Eternal Dao Ancestor’s eyes. It could freeze spacetime and release terrifying forbidden time laws. Combined with Eternal Dao Ancestor’s forbidden time Dao arts, it could throw other half-step Domain Ancestors into temporal chaos, making battle extremely painful for them.

As the Azure Dragon Palace Master fought fiercely with Eternal Dao Ancestor, he too fell into this frustrating state. The other party’s attainments in time were too profound, and Eternal Dao Ancestor’s forbidden body had also reached eighty to ninety percent completion, only slightly weaker than his own.

Overall, Eternal Dao Ancestor was a bit weaker than him, but he still had no way to do anything to Eternal Dao Ancestor.

At this moment.

Chapter 1164: Great Heavenly King!

Chapter 1164: Great Heavenly King

!【Fifth update】

The strength of Dao Ancestor Shenxu was about the same as Dao Ancestor Eternal's. He could be considered one of the best among half-step Domain Ancestors, only slightly weaker than Palace Master Azure Dragon.

But the key point was that Dao Ancestor Shenxu and Dao Ancestor Eternal specialized respectively in the forbidden Dao of Time and the forbidden Dao of Space. When the two joined forces, their power was far greater than one plus one, so the moment Dao Ancestor Shenxu joined the battle, he and Dao Ancestor Eternal instantly suppressed Palace Master Azure Dragon.

Boom! Palace Master Azure Dragon was instantly blasted away by the two forbidden Dao arts of Dao Ancestor Eternal and Dao Ancestor Shenxu. Even the Azure Dragon Sword in his hand was sent flying, though he summoned it back at once.

Blood was seeping from Palace Master Azure Dragon's hand. Although it was not really an injury worth mentioning, it represented a signal.

He could not defeat the combined forces of Dao Ancestor Shenxu and Dao Ancestor Eternal! Boom!! Palace Master White Tiger and Palace Master Zhenwu also descended, arriving at Palace Master Azure Dragon's side and confronting Dao Ancestor Shenxu and Dao Ancestor Eternal.

“Palace Master Azure Dragon, revoke the previous announcement. The Heavenly Emperor Palace is absolutely not allowed to collect resources from the various major factions, nor may it order other factions to do things. If the Heavenly Emperor Palace wants to take subordinate forces, that is your own affair, but the powers of the Upper Three Heavens are not permitted to become subordinate forces!”

Dao Ancestor Eternal proposed.

Palace Master Azure Dragon still wanted to flare up, but Palace Master White Tiger at the side agreed instead: “Fine!”

The moment those words were spoken, it meant the Imperial Palace had backed down.

Palace Master Azure Dragon was furious and looked at Palace Master White Tiger. “Palace Master White Tiger, why did you agree? With the strength of our Heavenly Emperor Palace, there is no need to fear Black Wind Mountain!”

No one knew what Palace Master White Tiger transmitted to him secretly, but after hearing it, Palace Master Azure Dragon quickly calmed down. He turned and left the region of spacetime turbulence together with Palace Master White Tiger and Palace Master Zhenwu, returning to the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Dao Ancestor Shenxu and Dao Ancestor Eternal also turned and left! The three half-step Domain Ancestors from the Vast Heaven Sect, Sky Sea Sect, and Myriad Domain Divine Hall also departed one by one. The spacetime turbulence began to stabilize as well; before long, this place would recover.

The many Dao Ancestors watching also withdrew their divine senses one after another, each discussing the matter in private.

This time.

Although the Heavenly Emperor Palace had displayed terrifying strength, the other factions—especially Black Wind Mountain—had unexpectedly sent out two half-step Domain Ancestors at once, enough to intimidate all powers. They all began to rank Black Wind Mountain as a colossal force second only to the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

....Human race.

Standing beside Ye Tian was a woman—Ouyang Jiu'er.

At this moment, Ouyang Jiu'er had also stepped into the Dao Ancestor realm.

“Jiu'er, the Heavenly Emperor Palace doesn't seem all that powerful, does it? I didn't expect Black Wind Mountain to have two half-step Domain Ancestors. In that case, wouldn't Black Wind Mountain be able to contend against the Heavenly Emperor Palace just by joining forces with any Ninth Heaven faction?”

Ye Tian said in a low voice.

“Big Brother Ye, you're underestimating the forces of the Vast Sea Domain Realm! In the Divine Heaven Realm, revealing all your strength is practically the same as not being far from destruction. If a sect-destroying war doesn't break out, no one knows just how terrifying a faction's foundations are. Can you really be sure the Heavenly Emperor Palace has only three half-step Domain Ancestors?”

“This....”

Ye Tian shook his head. He really could not guarantee that.

“Not to mention anything else, Black Wind Mountain definitely has more than just two half-step Domain Ancestors!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said.

“What? Black Wind Mountain has more than two half-step Domain Ancestors?” Ye Tian was shocked.

Ouyang Jiu'er smiled and said, “Do you still remember the three mountain masters I mentioned to you before?”

“I remember!”

Ye Tian nodded.

“Dao Ancestor Eternal and Dao Ancestor Shenxu are not… mountain masters. They are the first-generation Time King and Space King, subordinate to the three great mountain masters!”

Ouyang Jiu'er explained, “Back then, the identities of those three great mountain masters were also extremely mysterious, and they are far too ancient. There isn't much information recorded about them, so even I don't know much.

But if they are still alive, then their strength would definitely be greater than that of the Time King and the Space King! Besides, the first generation of the Ten Kings does not necessarily mean... the strongest! Take your master for example—right now, he is no longer your match.

Could it be that just because his seniority is higher, his strength must definitely be greater than those who came later?”

“That makes sense too!”

Ye Tian suddenly understood.

Put that way, Black Wind Mountain's strength was simply too terrifying! “Actually, this time, the Heavenly Emperor Palace didn't really want to rule over all the major factions. They were only testing the waters!”

Ouyang Jiu'er guessed.

“Testing the waters? Could it be that Azure Dragon was acting all along?”

Ye Tian frowned.

“Not exactly acting, but Palace Master Azure Dragon probably only wanted to force out the half-step Domain Ancestors hiding behind the scenes. This time, being able to force out five half-step Domain Ancestors means the Heavenly Emperor Palace's objective was achieved!”

“The Heavenly Emperor Palace has hidden quite a bit of its strength. It didn't reveal it this time, but the Palace Master really is the strongest combat power of the Heavenly Emperor Palace. At most, the Heavenly Emperor Palace has concealed a few half-step Domain Ancestors; it hasn't hidden as deeply as Black Wind Mountain. After all, the Heavenly Emperor Palace is relatively young, unlike Black Wind Mountain, which is so ancient.

But the Heavenly Emperor Palace does, after all, have a living Domain Ancestor and has left behind many trump cards. Who knows—perhaps some of those trump cards can kill a half-step Domain Ancestor in a single strike!”

Ouyang Jiu'er explained.

Listening to Ouyang Jiu'er's explanation, Ye Tian could not help sighing that the forces of the Divine Heaven Realm were almost all full of schemes, unlike the forces of the Daoshan Realm, where each and every one of them was relatively straightforward and had almost no hidden power.

On this day.

Ye Tian arrived at the Wind King's minor realm.

This time, he had come to see the Wind King and, at the same time, officially become a Heavenly King of Black Wind Mountain. After all, he was already a Dao Ancestor, so continuing to serve as a Heavenly General was no longer quite appropriate.

Of course, the status of a Heavenly General was itself higher than that of an ordinary Heavenly King, so when Ye Tian became a Heavenly King, he was not an ordinary one, but a Great Heavenly King, standing above all other Heavenly Kings and below only the Ten Kings.

0“Wind King!”

Ye Tian saw the Wind King's true body. Unlike before, the Wind King was wearing a mask this time, making his true appearance impossible to discern. Clearly, the face shown by his previous consciousness incarnation must have been an illusion rather than his real appearance; otherwise, there would be no need to wear a mask now.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly General, you've come. No, I should call you Nine Extremes Heavenly King!”

the Wind King said.

Then, the Wind King took out a Heavenly King token—a pure black Heavenly King token containing forbidden laws. This was Black Wind Mountain's rare Great Heavenly King token.

The Wind King handed the Great Heavenly King token to Ye Tian, signifying that Ye Tian had become a Great Heavenly King of Black Wind Mountain.

Afterward, a grand banquet was held within Black Wind Mountain to celebrate Ye Tian's becoming a Great Heavenly King. Those present at the gathering were not only many Heavenly Kings, but also the Wind King, Fire King, Metal King, Wood King, Ice King, and Time King.

However, the lofty Invincible Dao Ancestors and half-step Domain Ancestors did not attend.

That was only normal. If they had to show up for the banquet of a mere Great Heavenly King, wouldn't they be worked to death? If the Heavenly Emperor Palace hadn't forced Dao Ancestor Eternal and Dao Ancestor Shenxu to reveal themselves this time, even Black Wind Mountain's Heavenly Kings would not have known that Black Wind Mountain was actually so powerful! After the banquet ended, Ye Tian entered Black Wind Mountain's Heavenly King Library.

Chapter 1165: Success in Creating the Technique, the Nine Extremes Dao Canon! ..

Chapter 1165: Success in Creating the Technique, the Nine Extremes Dao Canon

!【Sixth Update】

The power of a Great Thousand Dao Art was far greater than that of a Middle Thousand Dao Art. At Ye Tian’s current level, even if a Middle Thousand Dao Art was cultivated to its limit, its power would only amount to that much—at best comparable to an entry-level Great Thousand Dao Art.

But some powerful Great Thousand Dao Arts, once merely at the beginner level, were already much stronger than Middle Thousand Dao Arts at their limit.

Ye Tian had yet to master a single Great Thousand Dao Art, so naturally he had come to choose some.

Black Wind Mountain’s Heavenly King Library held quite a few Great Thousand Dao Art inheritances, numbering several hundred in total. These were all public inheritances, and anyone who had just become a Heavenly King was qualified to choose three Great Thousand Dao Arts.

As for Ye Tian, as a Great Heavenly King, he had the authority to choose ten Great Thousand Dao Arts. This was one of the benefits of being a Great Heavenly King—there was no need to worry about lacking Great Thousand Dao Arts.

As for Dao Ancestors from some minor factions, let alone Great Thousand Dao Arts, they had no way even to obtain Middle Thousand Dao “zero four seven”

Arts.

Ye Tian flipped through the brief introductions to one Great Thousand Dao Art inheritance after another. After a long while, he finally settled on ten Great Thousand Dao Arts.

Great Thousand Dao Art—Heavenly Illusion Divine Step! Great Thousand Dao Art—Nine Revolutions Indestructible Golden Body! Great Thousand Dao Art—Primordial Slashing Art! Great Thousand Dao Art—Soul Golden Bell【】Art! Great Thousand Dao Art—Primordial Desolate Body! These five Great Thousand Dao Arts were the ones Ye Tian was most satisfied with. Among them, Primordial Desolate Body was the advanced Great Thousand Dao Art version of the Great Desolate Dharma Body. He had already cultivated the Great Desolate Dharma Body to its limit, so cultivating Primordial Desolate Body would be much easier for him.

In addition, he chose the binding-type Great Thousand Dao Art—Ten Directions Space-Fixing Art, and the tracking-type Great Thousand Dao Art—Three-Fruit Heavenly Eye Art! The remaining three were all offensive Great Thousand Dao Arts—Five Elements Holy Light Art, Boundless Spatial Divine Spear, and Space-Time Severance Art.

Of these, Space-Time Severance Art was the strangest. Although it was an offensive Dao Art, it did not directly injure people. Instead, it severed a person’s body into two parts and sent them into different space-times, making it difficult for the enemy to heal their body back together.

But once one gave up one half of the body, one’s strength would also decline considerably.

However, this Great Thousand Dao Art’s offensive power was somewhat too weak. Against an enemy of the same level, it simply could not cut through the opponent’s body.

Therefore, it was a somewhat useless Great Thousand Dao Art! Yet nothing was absolute; under certain circumstances, Space-Time Severance Art was definitely an extraordinarily remarkable Great Thousand Dao Art.

After choosing these ten Dao Arts, Ye Tian inherited them one by one.

After that, Ye Tian continued browsing all kinds of ancient texts in one library after another, expanding his knowledge and deepening his foundations.

He still needed to create a Dao Canon cultivation art suited to himself. Otherwise, at the Dao Ancestor level, he could only slowly accumulate forbidden Dao power and soul power. At first, this would not have much effect on the improvement of his strength, but in the later stages it would become rather difficult.

Therefore, it was imperative to create a Dao Canon cultivation art perfectly suited to himself.

If Ye Tian were to create it slowly on his own, it would probably take an extremely long time, but Black Wind Mountain had no shortage of foundations.

For example, Heavenly Kings could enter the Black Wind Technique Creation Hall to create cultivation arts.

The Technique Creation Hall contained the insights of countless senior experts who had created techniques, and it could also greatly enhance one’s comprehension. At the same time, it had been built with a hundred-thousandfold time acceleration, making it the most suitable place for creating techniques.

Of course.

When opening the Technique Creation Hall, Black Wind Mountain would provide the resources for the first thousand years; after that, one had to provide them oneself.

Under normal circumstances, ten thousand years was enough for a Dao Ancestor to create a Dao Canon suitable for oneself.

But Ye Tian was different. His foundation was too profound, and the Dao Canon cultivation art suited to him was bound to be extremely powerful. Thus, the time he required would certainly be very long—definitely far more than ten thousand years.

The Technique Creation Hall was exceedingly ancient and simple in style. After entering, Ye Tian directly sat down cross-legged on the central platform specially used for creating techniques.

Then, the Technique Creation Hall was activated.

Boom!!!! One illusory figure after another appeared—ancient seniors one and all. Ye Tian saw fragments of their insights when creating techniques. Each of them had left behind their understanding of technique creation. What one person left behind might be limited, but what countless people had left behind was incomparably precious.

Ye Tian comprehended bit by bit, and once again began from scratch to create a Dao Canon that belonged to him, step by step building its foundation.

Time slowly passed, and in the outside world, ten thousand years gradually went by.

And Ye Tian replenished the energy required to keep the Technique Creation Hall running. A great number of energy Dao stones were consumed, but Ye Tian did not care in the slightest.

And so, ten thousand years passed after ten thousand years.

It was not until the outside world had reached the one hundred and thirtieth thousand year that Ye Tian finally stopped the operation of the Technique Creation Hall... “At last, I’ve created it!”

Ye Tian walked out of the Technique Creation Hall and let out a sigh of relief.

After such an extremely long span of years, and after using several forbidden treasures capable of enhancing comprehension, only by studying the experiences of countless seniors in creating techniques had he finally succeeded in creating a Dao Canon that belonged to him.

Ye Tian named this Dao Canon the Nine Extremes Dao Canon! The Nine Extremes Dao Canon involved a portion of the forbidden Dao; if others tried to cultivate it, they simply would not be able to. It was only suitable for him.

It could allow Ye Tian to use the forbidden Dao to improve his cultivation and strength, continuously strengthening his body, soul, and forbidden Dao power, far beyond what other Dao Canons could compare to.

“Now, I have the Dao Canon, and I also have Great Thousand Dao Arts. Next, it’s time to go back into secluded cultivation!”

Ye Tian murmured.

This time, in seclusion, he believed his strength would definitely surge greatly. Stepping into the combat power of a Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor was a certainty! Whoosh! Ye Tian left the Wind King Minor Domain and returned to the human race.

....In the days that followed, Ye Tian began his closed-door cultivation, focusing wholeheartedly on cultivating the Great Thousand Dao Arts and the Nine Extremes Dao Canon.

As the days passed, the changes in the Xuanxu Ancient World were simply advancing with each passing day.

The human race became: stronger and stronger, with more and more True Ancestors being born, and more and more geniuses emerging.

And throughout the Xuanxu Ancient World, Primordial Chaos Lifeforms also gradually began to appear! 2.

These Primordial Chaos beings were each powerful and monstrously gifted, and were successively taken into various major forces to be nurtured.

After all, any Primordial Chaos Lifeform, with only a little training, could grow into a True Ancestor.

Therefore, Primordial Chaos Lifeforms were absolutely one of the favorite races for the major sects to recruit. They almost did not need to undergo any assessment at all—they were directly accepted.

At the same time, many genius disciples of the major forces also went about issuing challenges everywhere, making names for themselves throughout the Xuanxu Ancient World.

For example, Fengyang Imperial Son, one of the ten great Imperial Sons of this generation from the Heavenly Emperor Palace, challenged the True Ancestors of one mid-third-heaven force after another, defeating the invincible True Ancestors of one sect after another. His fame shook the entire Xuanxu Ancient World. Even some invincible Dao Ancestors from the upper third heavens who wanted to challenge him were easily defeated by him as well.

On this day.

He passed by the human race and wanted to challenge the True Ancestors of the human race.

Chapter 1166: The Emperor's Son Arrives! First Update, Please...

Chapter 1166: The Emperor's Son Arrives

!【First update, please subscribe to the full series】

Outside the territory of the human race, a group had arrived here.

It was a group of Dao Ancestors escorting a young man clad in golden armor, and this young man was one of the ten Emperor's Sons of the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

The status of an Emperor's Son was exceedingly noble. In terms of potential, talent, and strength, they were among the absolute top ten geniuses in the Heavenly Emperor Palace's genius camp, and they also had to be sufficiently young, otherwise they would not be qualified to become an Emperor's Son.

Moreover, once an Emperor's Son was surpassed by someone else, they would be stripped of the title.

Thus, the Emperor's Sons of the Heavenly Emperor Palace were all trying every possible means to increase their strength and display their might.

Fengyang Emperor's Son was the first to walk out of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, challenging the True Ancestors of various factions and making a name for himself throughout the Xuanxu Ancient Realm. If he successfully swept through the disciples of countless forces, then once he returned to the Heavenly Emperor Palace, he would surely receive tremendous rewards.

“Fengyang Emperor's Son, the human race doesn't have any particularly powerful True Ancestors. The former Myriad Laws True Ancestor was indeed very strong, an exalted True Ancestor, but now he is already a Dao Ancestor.

Aside from Myriad Laws Dao Ancestor, the human race's geniuses are far too weak!”

said one of the accompanying Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestors.

He was one of Fengyang Emperor's Son's guards—Leiyun Dao Ancestor. Although he was a Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestor, he had no real potential left, so he had been assigned to Fengyang Emperor's Son's side, serving as captain of the guard.

“Leiyun, it's precisely because the human race has no powerful True Ancestors that I want to challenge them. If I sweep through the human race's True Ancestors, will that Myriad Laws Dao Ancestor be furious? I just love seeing monsters like him get angry!”

Fengyang Emperor's Son said coldly.

But hidden in his words was still a trace of jealousy.

That's right, he was... jealous of Ye Tian.

Why was Ye Tian able to break into the ranks of exalted True Ancestors, while he could not?

He had already reached the very limit of invincible True Ancestors; there was almost no way for his strength to improve further. There were two choices before him: one was to charge into the Dao Ancestor level, and the other was to continue striving for the rank of exalted True Ancestor.

But he was unwilling! That was why this time he had come out to challenge the genius True Ancestors of the major sects—not only to stabilize his own position, but also in hopes of gaining a hint of enlightenment in battle, thereby breaking into the ranks of exalted True Ancestors.

Though this step was extremely, extremely difficult, with almost no hope, as long as there was even a sliver of hope, he would do it.

Soon, Fengyang Emperor's Son descended upon the human race.

The human race's True Ancestors had naturally heard of Fengyang Emperor's Son's fame, and knowing that he came from the Heavenly Emperor Palace, they dispatched many people to welcome him.

Human race, outside the Holy Hall.

Many human True Ancestors as well as some Dao Ancestors had appeared. Some of the Dao Ancestors were relatively weak, belonging to the First or Second Heaven Dao Ancestor level, and their status might not even be higher than that of the strongest True Ancestors.

The human race's true geniuses were basically still in the True Ancestor realm, constantly accumulating strength and unwilling to break through lightly into the Dao Ancestor realm.

At this moment, the Dao Ancestor responsible for receiving Fengyang Emperor's Son was the human Dao Ancestor—Qintian Dao Ancestor. He had once also been one of the human race's top geniuses, and with some opportunities added in, he later became a top-tier True Ancestor. However, because of an accident, he fell into a forbidden land and had no way to contact the outside world, so he could only break into the Dao Ancestor realm and forcibly break out of the forbidden land.

At present, he was also the strongest among the human race's Dao Ancestors besides Ye Tian, a top-tier Second Heaven Dao Ancestor who was not far from breaking through to the Third Heaven Dao Ancestor.

“Qintian Dao Ancestor, this time I'm passing through human territory, and I want to spar with the human race's geniuses. No problem, right?”

Fengyang Emperor's Son spoke.

“This....”

Qintian Dao Ancestor hesitated.

“Could it be that the human race is unwilling to give me face?”

Fengyang Emperor's Son feigned anger.

“Of course not!”

Qintian Dao Ancestor hurriedly explained, “Our human True Ancestors are no match for Fengyang Emperor's Son. A contest like this would have no meaning!”

“How about this: I will suppress my cultivation and strength to spar with your human race's geniuses. If any of them can injure me in the slightest, I will bestow upon that True Ancestor an inheritance of a medium thousand Dao technique. What do you think?”

Fengyang Emperor's Son said.

“What? An inheritance of a medium thousand Dao technique!!!”

Not only were the True Ancestors tempted, even Qintian Dao Ancestor was tempted.

How precious was an inheritance of a medium thousand Dao technique? The human race had very few of them! Ye Tian had been able to cultivate many medium thousand Dao techniques and even great thousand Dao techniques because they came from Black Wind Mountain, and those Dao technique inheritances were not permitted to be passed on to others.

Over such a long stretch of time, Ye Tian had also slain many True Ancestors and even Dao Ancestors, but those... Dao Ancestors and True Ancestors almost had no Dao technique inheritances on them. Even if they did, they were only inheritances of minor thousand Dao techniques.

Thus, in the Holy Hall's inheritance treasury of the human race, there were quite a few minor thousand Dao technique inheritances, but medium thousand Dao technique inheritances were exceedingly scarce, only about a dozen or so.

Furthermore, each medium thousand Dao technique inheritance was consumed after use; only by cultivating that medium thousand Dao technique to major accomplishment or above could one create an inheritance.

But as for the medium thousand Dao technique inheritances Ye Tian had seized, he had never cultivated them, so he had no way to create inheritances from them, and the human race's experts did not dare trouble Ye Tian to create inheritances either.

Therefore, the human race's medium thousand Dao technique inheritances diminished by one with each use. Without enormous merit, it was nearly impossible to obtain a medium thousand Dao technique inheritance.

Even Qintian Dao Ancestor himself had currently only been granted one medium thousand Dao technique, so he too wanted more medium thousand Dao techniques.

“As expected of the weakly founded human race—just a mere medium thousand Dao technique inheritance is enough to make them reveal greedy, excited looks!”

Fengyang Emperor's Son sneered inwardly.

Of course, the value of a medium thousand Dao technique inheritance was still extremely precious, and he would not casually grant one to others. Saying this was merely to get the human race's True Ancestors to spar with him; he did not believe these True Ancestors could injure him at all.

So, the human race shouldn't even dream of obtaining his medium thousand Dao technique inheritance.

“Alright, our human race agrees!”

Qintian Dao Ancestor agreed.

Very soon.

One human genius True Ancestor after another rushed over from all corners of human territory. Every genius True Ancestor who arrived had reached the level of a top-tier True Ancestor, which in the past would have been unimaginable.

Back then, even the powerful Xutian True Kingdom only had a few top-tier True Ancestors, but now the human race's top-tier True Ancestors—dozens could casually appear at any time.

On the battle arena outside the Holy Hall.

Fengyang Emperor's Son had the human geniuses come up one by one, while he kept both hands behind his back. Displaying only a portion of his strength, he easily defeated one top-tier True Ancestor after another.

Boom! Yet another top-tier True Ancestor was severely wounded by a single finger strike from Fengyang Emperor's Son and retreated from the arena.

“Does the human race not have any strongest True Ancestors? Your Myriad Laws Dao Ancestor used to be an exalted True Ancestor. The human race is also a powerful racial force—surely you don't not even have strongest True Ancestors, do you?”

Fengyang Emperor's Son mocked.

Qintian Dao Ancestor was also a bit angered now. He could tell—Fengyang Emperor's Son was... deliberately here to provoke the human race.

It wasn't that the human race had no strongest True Ancestors; it even had invincible True Ancestors.

For example, the wife of Myriad Laws True Ancestor—Xiao Yue—and his younger sister Ye Yu were both invincible True Ancestors, but it was impossible to have them take action, nor were they qualified to mobilize the family of Myriad Laws True Ancestor.

In addition, among the Nine Extremes Legion there were also strongest True Ancestors, but the strongest True Ancestors of the Nine Extremes Legion had long been cultivating in Nine Extremes Space.

Aside from them, there was one other place in the human race that had strongest True Ancestors, and that was the human race's Guardians, who belonged to the Holy Hall. They were geniuses personally nurtured by Ye Tian and had long been stationed in the depths of the human race's Holy Hall.

Normally, they were all cultivating, and only moved when missions appeared! “Let the Holy Hall Guardians take action!”

Qintian ordered someone to invite the Holy Hall Guardians.

The human race could lose, but it absolutely could not be mocked.

At present, the human race has no pinnacle True Ancestor to answer the challenge. one guardian joked.

one guardian said.

He was Anlan True Ancestor among the guardians. He had once secretly served as Ye Xingchen’s protector, and not long ago had also reached the level of pinnacle True Ancestor. He was one of the strongest guardians, ranked among the top few in strength.

This was a sword-qi spell! Puff!!!! Little Tiangang Sword instantly slashed toward Prince Fengyang, but Prince Fengyang caught it with one hand.

Dao Ancestor Qin Tian was furious, clenching his fists tightly.

They had clearly agreed to suppress strength for a spar, but this was what he called suppressing strength? If the other party was a top True Ancestor, then he suppressed himself to pinnacle True Ancestor; if the other party was a pinnacle True Ancestor, then he suppressed himself to the very peak of pinnacle True Ancestor.

This was called suppression? But he did not dare question Prince Fengyang, because the human race could not afford to provoke the Heavenly Emperor Palace, nor could they afford to provoke Prince Fengyang.

Standing behind Prince Fengyang was a group of Dao Ancestors, every one of them above the level of Third Heaven Dao Ancestor. The strongest among them, Dao Ancestor Leiyun, had even reached Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestor.

Within the human race, if Ye Tian did not appear, no one was a match for them.

Although the Heavenly Emperor Palace had not yet emerged into the world at that time, it had still gathered intelligence on such matters.

In his impression, Ye Xingchen was still at the level of a pinnacle True Ancestor. Even if his strength had advanced greatly, he might not necessarily have entered the invincible True Ancestor realm.

Besides, in his eyes, even ordinary invincible True Ancestors were merely weaklings.

But at this moment, as Ye Xingchen stood there, he actually brought him a faint trace of pressure.

“How is that possible? I am an expert at the very limit of invincible True Ancestors. What is Ye Xingchen supposed to be? How could he possibly make me feel pressure?”

Such terrifying power caused the human race’s talented True Ancestors who had gone up before to all change expression drastically. If they had to face such an attack, they would melt and perish in an instant.

This was also his only medium chiliocosm spell at the peak of minor accomplishment; his other spells were mostly at the minor accomplishment or entry level.

The Star Dao Robe was dazzlingly brilliant, like a magnificent garment draped over his body.

The golden light of Great Sun Golden Light Technique struck the Star Dao Robe, only to collapse immediately. It could not break Ye Xingchen’s defenses at all.

“.

Medium chiliocosm spell—Star Dao Robe, and it’s already reached the minor accomplishment level!”

Prince Fengyang frowned.

With such terrifying defense, and with his overall strength seemingly also having reached the limit of invincible True Ancestors, defeating Ye Xingchen would be somewhat difficult for him.

But immediately after that, Ye Xingchen revealed a forbidden body at the minor accomplishment level, and Prince Fengyang was utterly shocked. Although it had only just been tempered to forty percent, it was still far beyond an ordinary forbidden body.

More importantly, Prince Fengyang did not possess a forbidden body. He merely used a special secret technique to imbue his True Ancestor power with a trace of forbidden properties. That was far from truly controlling dark forbidden power, much less possessing a forbidden body.

If this continued, he would very likely lose! “No, I cannot lose. He's just a weak human, a race that doesn't even have a powerful Dao Ancestor. If I lose to a human genius like this, then when I return, the Heavenly Emperor Palace will definitely punish me!”

Prince Fengyang thought to himself.

He knew very clearly that his every move had always been under the watch of certain Dao Ancestors; they were also observing this battle.

Some weapon-type forbidden artifacts could naturally serve as embryos, but weapon-type forbidden artifacts were too rare, and ordinary low-grade, medium-grade, or even high-grade forbidden artifacts were not qualified to serve as embryos. At the very least, it had to be a top-grade weapon-type forbidden artifact to qualify.

But obtaining a top-grade forbidden weapon was quite difficult, let alone one that happened to be a weapon-type forbidden artifact.

Therefore, the number of forbidden weapons in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm was currently very, very small.

On the other side.

Prince Fengyang hurriedly said, “I admit defeat, I admit defeat!”

How could he still dare fight Ye Xingchen? Ye Xingchen was now a Pinnacle True Ancestor. Even though he had only just broken through and his strength hadn't risen in some absurdly dramatic way, Prince Fengyang hadn't been Ye Xingchen's match before, and now he was even less so.

“Sorry, I don't accept your surren—”

Ye Xingchen said coldly.

Earlier, Prince Fengyang had ordered Ancestor Leiyun to kill him.

How could he possibly let Prince Fengyang go? “Help me stop him!”

Prince Fengyang ordered the Dao Ancestors of his guard squad.

But at that very moment, those guard Dao Ancestors were locked onto by Ye Tian.

“Move, and you die!”

Ye Tian threatened.

One Dao Ancestor moved, and with a single strike, Ye Tian's forbidden spear pierced straight through his body, pinning him dead in the void.

At this, the other Dao Ancestors no longer dared move.

Meanwhile, Ye Xingchen had arrived before Prince Fengyang and slashed down with the Starblade.

Prince Fengyang was already injured, and his wounds still hadn't recovered. His combat strength was no longer at its peak, and the gap in power between him and Ye Xingchen was enormous. Even after going all out to use a defensive Dao Art, he still couldn't block the Starblade.

With a ripping sound, Prince Fengyang's body was almost directly cut into two, and he was severely injured once again.

Slash slash slash!!!! The Starblade came down again and again. Prince Fengyang was completely unable to resist. He wanted to flee, but his speed was inferior to Ye Xingchen's.

Of course, he also wanted to use an escape-type treasure to flee, but Ye Xingchen deployed a Forbidden Domain and also used a binding-type Middle Thousand Dao Art, leaving him with no way to escape—unless he possessed a forbidden treasure like the Forbidden Void Leaf.

But how could he have such a treasure! Feeling death about to descend, Prince Fengyang hastily brought out his backing: “Ye Xingchen, I am an Imperial Prince of the Heavenly Emperor Palace! Even your father, Ancestor Wanfa, is nothing but an ant before the Heavenly Emperor Palace! If you kill me, the Heavenly Emperor Palace will be enraged, and your human race will definitely be exterminated!”

Ye Xingchen was not threatened in the slightest by Prince Fengyang's words. His father had already said that he would bear all consequences.

Since Father hadn't stopped him, why should he hold back? Pfft! The Starblade swept across Prince Fengyang's neck, and a large head flew out.

Then Ye Xingchen used a Middle Thousand Dao Art—Star Divine Spear. With one strike, the Star Divine Spear directly pinned Prince Fengyang's head in place... At the same time.

Prince Fengyang's body was also continuously attacked by Ye Xingchen until it was completely pulverized.

At this moment.

Prince Fengyang's head was still roaring: he still had not died.

As an expert at the peak of Invincible True Ancestor, Prince Fengyang was naturally not so easy to kill. Unless Ye Xingchen had cultivated a forbidden technique and accumulated more years at the Supreme True Ancestor level, only then would he be able to kill a peak Invincible True Ancestor expert in a short time.

After a while longer, the Starblade had nearly chopped Prince Fengyang's head into countless fragments, and his soul too was sliced into pieces and completely collapsed.

Only then was Prince Fengyang truly dead.

All of this seemed to have taken a long time, but in reality only a little over ten minutes had passed.

When Prince Fengyang fell, none of Prince Fengyang's Dao Ancestor guards dared move an inch.

But Ye Tian knew very well that the Heavenly Emperor Palace must already have learned of Prince Fengyang's death by now.

After all, Prince Fengyang and those Dao Ancestor guards would have informed the Heavenly Emperor Palace, and among those Dao Ancestors watching, some would also contact the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Now, all that remained was... to wait for a powerful Dao Ancestor from the Heavenly Emperor Palace to arrive.

Boom!!!!! The void shook, and a figure stepped out from the nothingness. A pair of cold eyes fixed on Ye Tian as he said, “Ancestor Wanfa, your human race is quite bold indeed. You actually dared kill an Imperial Prince of our Heavenly Emperor Palace. Do you simply not place our Heavenly Emperor Palace in your eyes?”

The newcomer was a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor from the Heavenly Emperor Palace—2.

—Ancestor Fenghuo, belonging to the Heavenly Dragon Hall of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, in charge of warfare.

“Only one Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor came?”

Ye Tian muttered.

He had thought the Heavenly Emperor Palace would directly send a pinnacle Dao Ancestor. It seemed that one Imperial Prince was still not enough for the Heavenly Emperor Palace to mobilize a pinnacle Dao Ancestor.

“Ancestor Fenghuo, if Prince Fengyang had fought my son normally, then even if he lost, our human race would not have done anything to him.

Unfortunately, he couldn't afford to lose. The moment he lost, he ordered a Fifth-Heaven Dao Ancestor to kill my son! So what, does that mean the Imperial Princes of your Heavenly Emperor Palace are not allowed to lose, and whoever wins must be wiped out? From now on, does that mean if someone from your Heavenly Emperor Palace kills someone, and then is killed in turn, your Heavenly Emperor Palace will exterminate the other party's sect? If that's the case, then your Heavenly Emperor Palace is far too overbearing, isn't it!”

Ye Tian mocked.

As soon as those words were spoken, they immediately resonated with many Dao Ancestors. They secretly praised Ye Tian one after another, and the way they looked at Ancestor Fenghuo changed.

Chapter 1171: The Wind King Steps In!

Chapter 1171: The Wind King Steps In

!【Sixth Update】

“No matter what Prince Fengyang did, even if it was wrong, only our Heavenly Emperor Palace has the right to punish him. You humans have no right to deal with members of our Heavenly Emperor Palace!”

Dao Ancestor Fenghuo said coldly.

“We already... dealt with him. What are you going to do about it?”

Ye Tian shot back without the slightest fear.

“Then I’ll take you to the Heavenly Emperor Palace and leave you to the Emperors for judgment!”

Dao Ancestor Fenghuo made his move directly, using the power of a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor to capture Ye Tian.

Although Ye Tian had once killed a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor before, that was when the other party had been suppressed by the laws of the Mysterious Void Ancient Realm and couldn’t bring out much of his true strength....

But now things were different. A Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor could fully unleash all of his power.

Boom!!! An ancient phoenix carrying endless flames charged toward Ye Tian. This was Dao Ancestor Fenghuo’s famous grand thousand dao art—the Great Ancient Phoenix Art, a grand thousand dao art created by imitating an Ancient Chaos Phoenix at the level of an ultimate Dao Ancestor. Its power was terrifying, enough to burn away laws themselves.

“Nine Revolutions Indestructible Golden Body!”

“Primordial Desolate Body!”

Ye Tian unleashed two grand thousand dao arts in succession, and together with his major-completion Forbidden Body, he forcibly resisted Dao Ancestor Fenghuo’s Great Ancient Phoenix Art.

With a thunderous boom!!!! Ye Tian’s body was forced backward again and again. The Nine Revolutions Indestructible Golden Body dimmed, and the Primordial Desolate Body was also shattered, but his major-completion Forbidden Body weakened much of the attack, so he only suffered light injuries and forcibly endured the move.

“A major-completion Forbidden Body!!!”

Dao Ancestor Fenghuo’s expression changed.

This was a goal even many invincible Dao Ancestors had failed to achieve, yet Ye Tian had actually done it! And on top of that, both his Nine Revolutions Indestructible Golden Body and Primordial Desolate Body had reached the minor-completion level. Wasn’t his cultivation speed a bit too ridiculous? How long had Dao Ancestor Myriad Laws been a Dao Ancestor? In such a short time, even with a defensive-type Dao-level natal talent and forbidden treasures that constantly enhanced comprehension, it should have been impossible to cultivate two grand thousand dao arts to minor completion! This was simply breaking the rules! In truth, Ye Tian had advanced to Dao Ancestor from the level of a pinnacle True Ancestor, so his comprehension was already terrifying. On top of that, he had copied so many Dao-level natal talents, and quite a few of them involved defense, so his speed in comprehending grand thousand dao arts was far beyond what other pinnacle True Ancestors could compare to.

Of course, there was no way he would tell any of this to Dao Ancestor Fenghuo.

At this moment.

Dao Ancestor Fenghuo took out a forbidden weapon containing the forbidden law of fire—the Fenghuo Blade! From the previous exchange, it was clear that Ye Tian’s strength had already reached the level of a Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor, and not just any Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor, but one at the very peak. Coupled with his major-completion Forbidden Body, even ordinary Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors would find it hard to kill him.

Although he himself was a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, he was not among the very strongest of that level. If he didn’t use a forbidden weapon, he likely wouldn’t be able to capture Ye Tian.

Whoosh...!! Dao Ancestor Fenghuo closed in and attacked at close range.

Ye Tian also stopped hiding his own forbidden weapon—the Heaven-Slaying Spear.

Rumble rumble rumble!!!! The two began battling fiercely. Not long after clashing, Dao Ancestor Fenghuo discovered that his Fenghuo Blade was showing faint signs of cracking. If not for his own power protecting it, Ye Tian might have shattered his Fenghuo Blade with a single spear strike.

“Your spear is a mid-grade forbidden weapon!”

Dao Ancestor Fenghuo finally recognized it and was instantly shocked.

In the Heavenly Emperor Palace, not even all Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors like him possessed forbidden weapons. Only a small number did. Even some ultimate Dao Ancestors didn’t have mid-grade forbidden weapons. Only invincible Dao Ancestors had the resources to forge one, and even then it would consume so many treasures that many were reluctant to do so.

Yet Ye Tian had only broken through to Dao Ancestor not long ago, and he already had the wealth to forge a mid-grade forbidden weapon! Moreover, Ye Tian’s son, Ye Xingchen, also had a forbidden weapon! He really wanted to curse—were the human race this rich? In battle, Ye Tian went all out. He even unleashed his Forbidden Domain, and also used the binding-type grand thousand dao art, the Ten Directions Space-Fixing Art, but Dao Ancestor Fenghuo was too powerful. He simply couldn’t be restrained, only slightly affected.

“Primordial Cleaving Art!”

Ye Tian slashed through the void with the Heaven-Slaying Spear and used this grand thousand dao art. This was a technique he had recently worked out, one that could preliminarily fuse a forbidden weapon with a grand thousand dao art, slightly increasing its power.

Whoosh...!! A line of golden light sliced out and slashed toward Dao Ancestor Fenghuo.

However, the Primordial Cleaving Art only left a mark on Dao Ancestor Fenghuo’s grand thousand dao art, the Flame-Extinguishing True Armor, and did not injure him at all.

Throughout the entire fight, Ye Tian was being suppressed. If not for relying on his major-completion Forbidden Body to preserve his life, he would have been defeated long ago.

“There’s still quite a gap in strength!”

Ye Tian sighed.

But there was nothing he could do. Strength couldn’t be raised to a higher level in a single step; it still required gradual cultivation.

In such a short time, the fact that he could fight a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor without losing was already terrifying enough! Suddenly.

A voice rang out.

“Fenghuo, stand down!”

Hearing this voice, Dao Ancestor Fenghuo stopped fighting Ye Tian and withdrew.

Then, a barefoot middle-aged man appeared. He wore a dao robe, a blue-gold crown with golden trim on his head, and stood with his hands behind his back, showing a smile that seemed inscrutable, though it carried even more coldness than mystery.

“Greetings, Lord Lantian!”

Dao Ancestor Fenghuo bent at the waist respectfully.

“Heavenly Emperor Palace, Dao Ancestor Lantian!”

Ye Tian frowned.

This was no Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, but an Eighth-Heaven ultimate Dao Ancestor, enough to rival one of Black Wind Mountain’s Ten Kings.

“Dao Ancestor Myriad Laws, if you are willing to join our Heavenly Emperor Palace, this matter can be forgotten. Otherwise, I won’t even take you back for punishment today—I’ll kill you where you stand!”

Dao Ancestor Lantian threatened coldly.

“Sorry, but 047, I will not join the Heavenly Emperor Palace!”

Ye Tian refused outright.

Around them, many watching Dao Ancestors felt that Ye Tian was in trouble and would likely fall here, and each of them sighed in regret.

Some Dao Ancestors even thought that joining the Heavenly Emperor Palace would be great—at least it would mean having a powerful backer! “Then die!”

Dao Ancestor Lantian made his move. A blue ray pierced forward in an instant, showing not the slightest mercy.

No Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor could block this strike, much less Ye Tian, who only had the strength of a Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor.

Ye Tian also knew he couldn’t stop it, but he wasn’t panicked in the slightest.

Suddenly.

A figure appeared in front of Ye Tian and easily blocked the attack.

This person wore a black battle robe and a mask. Forbidden characters were inscribed on the robe—Wind! He was... the Wind King of Black Wind Mountain.

The Wind King seemed to know Dao Ancestor Lantian and said with a smile, “Dao Ancestor Lantian, long time no see. Why is it that the moment you show up, you want to kill a Heavenly King of our Black Wind Mountain?”

Dao Ancestor Lantian asked in confusion, “A Heavenly King of Black Wind Mountain? Didn’t Dao Ancestor Myriad Laws say he wasn’t one of your Black Wind Mountain’s Nine Extremes Heavenly Kings? So how is he one now?”

The Wind King mocked, “Even if Dao Ancestor Myriad Laws isn’t one of Black Wind Mountain’s Nine Extremes Heavenly Kings, does that mean he can’t become a Heavenly King of Black Wind Mountain? You failed to recruit one of our Black Wind Mountain Heavenly Kings, and now you still want to make a move.

Could it be that you want to fight me? Then let’s fight!”

Dao Ancestor Lantian’s expression froze. If he fought the Wind King, he was no match at all! For the version of the novel without underlines, please download Stone Novel

Chapter 1172: Hire the Hall of Slaughter!

Chapter 1172: Hire the Hall of Slaughter

!【Seventh Update】

Seeing that Ancestor Blue Sky was hesitant and didn’t dare make a move, King Feng declared domineeringly, “In any case, our Black Wind Mountain is protecting Ancestor Myriad Laws. If your Heavenly Emperor Palace dares declare war, then Black Wind Mountain will accept the challenge.

I just wonder whether your Heavenly Emperor Palace dares to go to war over a mere Imperial Son.”

His departure also represented that the Heavenly Emperor Palace was unwilling to go to war for the sake of a mere Imperial Son. After all, he was only an Imperial Son, not a Pinnacle True Ancestor. If one Imperial Son died, they could simply cultivate another.

The Heavenly Emperor Palace had ten Imperial Sons, as well as several candidate Imperial Sons, so they did not care about such a loss.

If they went to war with Black Wind Mountain over a mere Imperial Son and caused a large number of Dao Ancestors to fall, that would truly not be worth it.

It was not yet time for war, and there were no great benefits involved, so there was no need to fight Black Wind Mountain to the death.

After Ancestor Blue Sky left.

Therefore, winning over a Pinnacle True Ancestor was of great significance to Black Wind Mountain.

Moreover, Ye Xingchen’s background was clear, and his father was one of Black Wind Mountain’s Great Heavenly Kings. A genius like this was simply too suitable for Black Wind Mountain.

Not long after.

Ye Xingchen entered Black Wind Mountain, and King Feng personally conferred upon him the title of Heavenly General.

When General Bloodfiend and General Motian saw that Ye Tian’s son, Ye Xingchen, had also become a Heavenly General and now stood above them, each of them felt deeply ashamed.

They also knew that they had no way of advancing to become Pinnacle True Ancestors, so they all chose to attempt a breakthrough into the Dao Ancestor realm.

In truth, Black Wind Mountain had far more Invincible True Ancestors than just General Bloodfiend and the others. Other Invincible True Ancestors were in the legions of other Heavenly Kings and Great Kings, and those extremely mysterious Invincible True Ancestors and half-step Domain Ancestors likely also had legions of their own, though they had never exposed them.

Even Ye Tian did not know the full strength of Black Wind Mountain, nor did he know how many Invincible True Ancestors Black Wind Mountain actually had.

Although Ye Xingchen had become a Heavenly General and could command those generals and peaks, there were still many he could not truly manage. For example, the True Ancestors in the legions under Heavenly Kings, Great Kings, and Invincible True Ancestors were not under his authority.

A Heavenly General seemed to hold a high position, but in reality, it was still far from enough to enter the upper ranks of Black Wind Mountain.

Even though Ye Tian was now a Great Heavenly King, he still knew very, very little. Only if one day he could become one of Black Wind Mountain’s Ten Kings would he be qualified to know Black Wind Mountain’s true secrets and foundations.

....Heavenly Emperor Palace.

The death of Imperial Son Fengyang caused a stir within the inner circles. Many Dao Ancestors were furious, but that was all it was—anger. The three Palace Masters would never go to war with Black Wind Mountain over a mere Imperial Son Fengyang.

However, Imperial Son Fengyang was not without backing. He also had a family in the Heavenly Emperor Palace, belonging to a fairly powerful clan—the Feng Clan! The Feng Clan to which Imperial Son Fengyang belonged had dozens of Dao Ancestors, and the strongest among them was a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor. Fengyang had also received nearly all of the Feng Clan’s resources and nurturing, and he was the Feng Clan’s hope.

They had even hoped that Fengyang would one day become a pinnacle Dao Ancestor, take charge of one hall, and wield immense authority within the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

However, Fengyang was dead, and the Heavenly Emperor Palace would not even avenge him.

This completely enraged the Feng Clan, but they did not dare cause trouble in the Heavenly Emperor Palace. Otherwise, with a single order from the three Palace Masters, the Feng Clan would be reduced to ashes.

At this moment, the Feng Clan’s upper echelons were holding a discussion.

Presiding over the meeting was the Feng Clan’s ancestor—Feng Zhengde, also known as Ancestor Longfei. His true form was a dragon sparrow carrying the bloodline of the dragon race.

“Fengyang is dead!”

Ancestor Longfei said dejectedly.

Every Dao Ancestor present was in a terrible mood. In order to cultivate Fengyang, they had usually been reluctant even to spend large amounts of resources on their own cultivation, all so they could raise Fengyang as quickly as possible. They had never expected to receive such an outcome instead.

Ancestor Longfei continued, “I contacted one of the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s pinnacle Dao Ancestors. The Heavenly Emperor Palace will not avenge Fengyang, because the other party is from Black Wind Mountain, and Black Wind Mountain is protecting him. The Heavenly Emperor Palace is unwilling to go to war.

But we must avenge this!”

“We must have revenge!”

The many Dao Ancestors roared in anger.

At this time, one of the Feng Clan’s higher-ups asked, “Ancestor, the one who killed Fengyang is the human Ye Xingchen. It’s said that he is now already a Pinnacle True Ancestor and has also become a Heavenly General of Black Wind Mountain. If we kill him, Black Wind Mountain will definitely be enraged!”

“.

If Black Wind Mountain is enraged, could it be that they would really dare go to war with the Heavenly Emperor Palace?”

Ancestor Longfei said coldly.

That Feng Clan higher-up fell silent.

Ancestor Longfei continued, “Don’t worry. I know what you’re worried about—Black Wind Mountain, that Ancestor Myriad Laws, and also that the Heavenly Emperor Palace might abandon us.

I can guarantee that the Feng Clan will take revenge, but no one from the Feng Clan will make a move.”

“If we don’t make a move ourselves, then how are we supposed to kill Ye Xingchen?”

The Feng Clan’s upper echelon were all puzzled.

“Have you all been in the Daoshan Realm for so long that you’ve forgotten the situation in the Vast Sea Domain? Back then, when several factions offended our Feng Clan, did we use the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s power?”

Ancestor Longfei reminded them.

“Ancestor, you mean the Hall of Slaughter!”

One Dao Ancestor suddenly realized.

“That’s right, it’s... the Hall of Slaughter!”

Ancestor Longfei nodded.

Everyone present knew of the Hall of Slaughter. It was an assassin organization whose members were equally mysterious, and it was said that they came from various major factions.

Black Wind Mountain was a bandit force, while the Hall of Slaughter was similarly mysterious, a force of assassins.

Of course, the Hall of Slaughter’s strength was far inferior to Black Wind Mountain’s, but as long as they were given sufficient treasures, they would dare kill anyone. They would even dare assassinate a pinnacle Dao Ancestor—but only once. They would not dare do it a second time.

After all, once exposed, the Hall of Slaughter also feared being implicated.

There was no such thing as fighting to the death forever, nor could there be endless assassination attempts. That was too absurd! If there truly were such an arrogant assassin force, it would have long since been destroyed.

But once the Hall of Slaughter sent out an assassin, they completed the mission nearly ninety percent of the time. The remaining ten percent represented uncertainty, because accidents could happen in many situations.

For example, a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor might be sent to kill a First Heaven Dao Ancestor, only to discover that the target was protected by an Invincible Dao Ancestor. Situations like that fell under uncertainty.

After discussion, the Feng Clan decided to hire the Hall of Slaughter to assassinate Ye Xingchen. As for assassinating Ancestor Myriad Laws, the price was too high—the Feng Clan simply could not afford it.

Chapter 1173: Drawing Out the Assassin!

Chapter 1173: Drawing Out the Assassin

!【First Update】

Longfei Dao Ancestor had once asked the Hall of Assassins to kill a Dao Ancestor, and because of that, he came to know one of the people in the Hall of Assassins.

Fortunately, that high-ranking member of the Hall of Assassins was still alive. Otherwise, it would have been quite troublesome for him to even get in touch with the Hall of Assassins.

Feng Family, secret chamber.

Longfei Dao Ancestor took out a client token of the Hall of Assassins and activated it. A strand of consciousness crossed time and space and arrived in a special space.

Then, he called out to that high-ranking member of the Hall of Assassins.

Very soon, an illusory figure appeared, its entire body shrouded in darkness. And since this was a consciousness space, there was no way to discern the other party’s identity.

“Ming, you’ve come!”

Longfei Dao Ancestor said.

“Longfei Dao Ancestor, why have you come to me?”

Ming asked.

“I want to ask the Hall of Assassins to kill someone!”

Longfei Dao Ancestor stated his purpose directly.

“Who?”

Ming was straightforward and did not waste words.

“Ye Xingchen!”

Longfei Dao Ancestor spoke that name.

“Ye Xingchen?”

Ming smiled and said, “You mean Ye Xingchen, the son of the Human Race’s Myriad Laws Dao Ancestor?”

“That’s right!”

Longfei Dao Ancestor nodded.

Ming fell silent for a moment, then said, “Ye Xingchen is a Pinnacle True Ancestor. He has at least a ninety percent chance of becoming an Invincible Dao Ancestor in the future, and his father, Myriad Laws Dao Ancestor, has even greater potential. The price of killing Ye Xingchen is very high. One sentence: 10,000 Forbidden Dao Stones, or treasures of equivalent value. Are you willing to pay?”

“What? Ten thousand Forbidden Dao Stones? Your price is outrageous!”

Longfei Dao Ancestor found it hard to accept. The cost was simply too great—it would practically shake the very foundation of the Feng Family.

Although a Forbidden Dao Stone vein had previously appeared in the Forbidden Mountain Range, producing hundreds of thousands of Forbidden Dao Stones, and some Forbidden treasure lands had also gradually produced small amounts of Forbidden Dao Stones, the value of Forbidden Dao Stones remained enormous. Their value had not fallen just because they had begun appearing more frequently.

And the Feng Family did not have many Forbidden Dao Stones. If they were to use other treasures as payment instead, they would probably have to empty out more than half of the Feng Family’s treasury.

Just for revenge, they would have to pay such an enormous price. He was rather unwilling.

“If you’re unwilling, then forget it. Our Hall of Assassins isn’t all that eager to take on this kind of mission anyway!”

Ming said coldly.

“Let me think about it!”

Longfei Dao Ancestor hurriedly said.

“I’ll only give you three days to consider. Once the time is up, the offer is gone!”

After saying that, Ming disappeared.

Longfei Dao Ancestor’s consciousness withdrew from that void space and returned to his body.

“Three days, huh!”

Longfei Dao Ancestor sighed, then discussed it with the other Dao Ancestors and convened a meeting.

And this meeting lasted a full two days before they finally made their decision.

By a vote that was just barely over half, they decided to spend this wealth and ask the Hall of Assassins to take action.

Black Wind Mountain.

Ye Tian had originally been in secluded cultivation, but after receiving a message from Feng Xun, he could only come to the Feng King Small Domain.

“Feng King, why were you looking for me?”

Ye Tian asked curiously.

“Your son is in trouble!”

Feng King said.

“What?”

Ye Tian frowned and hurriedly asked, “Did something happen?”

“Someone has placed a bounty with the Hall of Assassins to kill your son, Ye Xingchen!”

Feng King said.

“The Hall of Assassins!”

Ye Tian knew of this force. It was an assassin organization whose members were all rather mysterious and came from various different factions.

Moreover, the Hall of Assassins was very powerful. Although it had no Invincible Dao Ancestor, it had several peak Dao Ancestors, making it comparable to an Eighth Heaven-level force.

However, since the members of the Hall of Assassins came from other factions, it could not be rated as an Upper Three Heavens force, and so it was merely considered a loose organization.

The reason Black Wind Mountain was not rated as an Upper Three Heavens force was similar. Some of its members came from Lower Three Heavens forces, and they were also bandits, so its force level was not evaluated.

Once targeted by the Hall of Assassins, Ye Xingchen was indeed in great danger, unless he stayed in Black Wind Mountain forever and never went out.

But that was unrealistic! “Feng King, I heard that the assassins of the Hall of Assassins all swear life-bound oaths and are forbidden from leaking mission information. Logically speaking, assassination missions shouldn’t be able to leak out, so how do you know about it?”

Ye Tian asked curiously.

“Hahaha, naturally the other assassins can’t leak the information. Otherwise, who would still dare to go to the Hall of Assassins to post missions?

But I’m different. To tell you the truth, I am one of the three vice hall masters of the Hall of Assassins!”

Feng King said with a smile.

“What? Feng King, you’re a vice hall master of the Hall of Assassins!”

Ye Tian was shocked.

This news was far too unexpected. He had thought Feng King had planted someone inside the Hall of Assassins and used some special method to pass on the information. He had never imagined that Feng King himself was actually... one of the vice hall masters of the Hall of Assassins.

“The other Ten Kings of Black Wind Mountain all know this secret, and since you are the Great Heavenly King of Black Wind Mountain, your status is second only to ours, so naturally you are qualified to know this secret!”

Feng King then explained why he had become one of the vice hall masters of the Hall of Assassins.

It turned out that.

Back at a certain level, Feng King had wanted to earn some extra money, so he became an assassin for Black Wind Mountain. As his strength grew, he gradually became a vice hall master of the Hall of Assassins and gained considerable authority. Even so, he still did not know who the hall master of the Hall of Assassins was. That person was far too mysterious.

“Feng King, do you know who posted the mission?”

Ye Tian asked.

He had a guess in his heart, but he did not dare confirm it.

“It was the Feng Family! That Feng Family from the Heavenly Emperor Palace... the family of Imperial Son Fengyang!”

Feng King replied.

“So it really was them!”

Ye Tian was furious.

“Feng King, then what should we do now?”

The Hall of Assassins will not send a second assassin, because they also fear implicating the Hall of Assassins.

Therefore, once one assassin fails, the mission is considered a failure.

And once an assassin fails, they either die or voluntarily withdraw from the Hall of Assassins!”

Feng King explained.

Then, Feng King also told Ye Xingchen about the matter.

Ye Xingchen did not feel much worry, but neither did he leave immediately. Instead, he waited a thousand years before leaving Black Wind Mountain and traveling around the various territories of the Human Race.

Ye Tian did not follow Ye Xingchen, otherwise it would very easily cause the assassin to not dare to attack.

Based on the information provided by Feng King, an assassin had indeed accepted the mission, and it was a Silver-ranked assassin whose strength was at the level of a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor.

For a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor to kill a Pinnacle True Ancestor, this was practically certain to succeed.

This was also why the Hall of Assassins had an assassination success rate of over ninety percent—strong experts killing weaker ones, and doing so through assassination. How could the success rate not be high? On this day.

Ye Xingchen was flying through a stretch of void.

Suddenly, the void froze, and a terrifying aura locked onto him.
