Chapter 1174: The Forbidden Void Realm!

Chapter 1174: The Forbidden Void Realm

!【Second Update】

“There’s no one else nearby—only Ye Xingchen. With my assassination speed, if I unleash the full power of a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor strike, it’ll be enough to kill Ye Xingchen instantly and then slip away. Completely safe!”

He was a Silver-ranked assassin, codename: Indifference! Without the slightest hesitation, Indifference struck at once, and the moment he moved, he used a Mid Thousand Dao Art he had once obtained by chance—Ghost Sting! He had not cultivated many... Dao Arts, only a few, and over countless years had focused solely on Ghost Sting, directly training this Mid Thousand Dao Art to the peak of major accomplishment, just one step away from perfection.

With a top-tier Dao artifact shortsword combined with Ghost Sting, he launched a ruthless killing blow.

“He’s dead for sure!”

Indifference judged by his own experience.

With a clang! the shortsword did not stab into Ye Xingchen’s body, but into a pair of unfamiliar large hands.

“Not good, the mission failed!”

When Indifference’s strike failed, he instantly fled into the distance.

However, he could no longer leave! A figure blocked his path! He recognized that battle robe and mask—they belonged to Fire King of Black Wind Mountain.

Fire King casually waved his hand, and a ball of flame enveloped Indifference.

Indifference, who had no real life-preserving abilities, was completely unable to withstand this terrifying flame Dao Art.

Before his consciousness was utterly annihilated, the question in Indifference’s heart was: “Who leaked the mission?”

Clearly, Fire King had been specifically protecting Ye Xingchen.

But what qualifications did Ye Xingchen have to receive Fire King’s protection? It had to be because someone wanted to assassinate Ye Xingchen, and so he needed to be protected.

This meant the Hall of Assassins’ mission had been leaked! Although he had no idea how it had been leaked, he no longer had the ability to think about it.

Because he was already dead! Casually killing a Silver-ranked assassin was nothing to Fire King. If it had been a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor with strong survival abilities, perhaps they could have endured one move, but an assassin like this, skilled only in assassination and not in preserving his own life, could be instantly killed with a single attack.

“Many thanks, Fire King!”

Ye Xingchen flew over and said gratefully.

It had been far too dangerous just now. The other party’s speed had been too fast; it felt as if his consciousness had been frozen, and he simply could not react.

If that stab had landed on him, no defense would have been able to stop it. Even his Forbidden Body could not have blocked it—he would have been annihilated in one strike, with not the slightest chance of survival.

“Just a small matter. The assassin is dead, and they won’t send anyone else. I’m leaving!”

Fire King left quickly and did not stay any longer.

He was busy as well. Last time, he had obtained the forbidden pinnacle treasure, the Forbidden Fire Lotus, and it had already allowed him to glimpse a sliver of hope of stepping into the level of an Invincible Dao Ancestor. Thus, he needed to go back and cultivate and comprehend it properly.

If not for the fact that Wind King needed to avoid suspicion and feared exposing his identity as a vice hall master of the Hall of Assassins, and therefore did not dare get involved, Fire King would not have stepped in to help either.

On the other side.

The Hall of Assassins quickly confirmed the death of the Silver-ranked assassin, and then canceled this missio.

Once a mission was canceled, only half the reward would be refunded. This was the Hall of Assassins’ rule. Anyone seeking their help had to be mentally prepared for that.

After all, the Hall of Assassins had suffered a significant loss as well—a heavy-heaven Dao Ancestor had fallen. If they got no benefits at all, the Hall of Assassins would have gone out of business long ago.

Heavenly Emperor Palace, the Feng Family.

The Feng Family’s patriarch, Dao Ancestor Longfei, was extremely furious. The Hall of Assassins’ assassination had failed, and the mission had been canceled.

“Damn Hall of Assassins! They can’t even kill a mere True Ancestor, and even lost a Silver-ranked assassin. This is absurd!”

It wasn’t that Dao Ancestor Longfei didn’t trust the Hall of Assassins’ information, but for a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor to assassinate a True Ancestor, the success rate should have been almost one hundred percent.

If the assassination had succeeded but the assassin failed to escape afterward, that would still have been understandable. But Ye Xingchen was completely unharmed while the Silver-ranked assassin was killed—what kind of nonsense was that?

He even suspected that the mission had been leaked, causing Ye Xingchen to be on guard.

This was the Hall of Assassins’ responsibility, yet they still swallowed half his payment. That was an enormous amount of wealth! But Dao Ancestor Longfei had no way to do anything to the Hall of Assassins, so he could only swallow this bitter outcome himself.

“Forget it, let it be for now. I’ll take revenge on Ye Xingchen and the human race later. There will be plenty of opportunities!”

Dao Ancestor Longfei comforted himself like this.

The Feng Family had temporarily given up, but they had no idea that they had already been exposed.

Human race.

When Ye Tian learned that his son Ye Xingchen had truly been assassinated, he was extremely furious. Although he had expected it and it had ended without real danger, that didn’t mean he wasn’t angry.

“The Feng Family, huh? In the future, I’ll kill you every time I see you!”

Ye Tian said coldly.

He did not take revenge immediately. After all, the Feng Family was on Heavenly Emperor Palace territory. If he dared to go there and kill, he could forget about coming back.

As for hiring the Hall of Assassins, there was no need. The cost was too high, and at most he could only kill a few people—what use was that? In the blink of an eye, tens of thousands of years passed.

Since the birth of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, the first major event had occurred.

The first Forbidden Void Realm had appeared! This major event immediately drew the attention of many great factions, all of whom set their sights on this Forbidden Void Realm.

What was a Forbidden Void Realm? Things like the Forbidden Forest, the Forbidden Mountain Range, and the Fireflame Forbidden Land from before all belonged to semi-spaces that overlapped with the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, and these forbidden treasure lands could be seen from outside.

Although these forbidden treasure lands could produce many forbidden wonders, their safety was not very good, making them unsuitable to serve as the headquarters of a faction.

But a Forbidden Void Realm was different. It belonged entirely to another void and was extremely, extremely well hidden. Once a faction occupied a Forbidden Void Realm, with a little modification it could be used as the faction’s headquarters.

0And after setting up grand formations, it would be very difficult for other factions to break into the Forbidden Void Realm.

In addition.

The laws of a Forbidden Void Realm were very powerful. Even if Invincible Dao Ancestors or even half-step Domain Ancestors fought there, it would still be difficult to damage the Forbidden Void Realm. It could easily withstand battles between many, many powerful experts without issue.

Most importantly... a Forbidden Void Realm could be refined. Once one refined a Forbidden Void Realm, one would become its Realm Lord and be able to mobilize the power of the Forbidden Void Realm.

At that time, even a Pinnacle Dao Ancestor who controlled a Forbidden Void Realm could suppress an Invincible Dao Ancestor.

If an Invincible Dao Ancestor controlled a Forbidden Void Realm, they could even contend against a half-step Domain Ancestor.

What kind of concept was that? Therefore, there was not a single faction that was not tempted by a Forbidden Void Realm; all wanted to occupy one.

One could well imagine that whichever faction occupied a Forbidden Void Realm would basically be able to develop rapidly in the future.

Even the Vast Sea Domain Realm of the past had never possessed a Forbidden Void Realm, so even Heavenly Emperor Palace would likely be tempted.

As for why the Forbidden Void Realm had been discovered, it was because when it had just been born, the spatial fluctuations were enormous, naturally drawing the attention of the outside world.

Once the Forbidden Void Realm stabilized, it would no longer be so easy to discover it.

After the Forbidden Void Realm was discovered, large numbers of Dao Ancestors arrived at the area where the Forbidden Void Realm’s fluctuations were strongest.

Mitian Sect, Tianhai Sect, Myriad Domain Divine Hall, Black Wind Mountain... these factions all sent Dao Ancestors one after another.

Chapter 1175: It's Only Small!

Chapter 1175: It's Only Small

!【Third Update】

Since the Forbidden Void Realm had not yet truly stabilized, the genuinely top experts had not descended, but some pinnaclely powerful Dao Ancestors had already arrived.

The three kings of Black Wind Mountain—Wind King, Fire King, and Time King—had come, along with Ancestor Xumi Dao and Ancestor Devouring Heaven Dao of the Vast Sky Sect, Ancestor Heavenly Artifact Dao and Ancestor Tianqi Dao of the Myriad Domain Divine Hall, Ancestor Divine Sea Dao and Ancestor Eight Clouds Dao of the Heavenly Sea Sect... These pinnaclely powerful Dao Ancestors were the first batch of experts to descend here and investigate the situation of the Forbidden Void Realm.

Once the Forbidden Void Realm stabilized, those invincible Dao Ancestors might appear immediately, and even half-step Domain Ancestors might make a move.

Ye Tian had also come here. After all, with such a major event taking place, there was no way he would stay away.

However, what Ye Tian had sent was a replicated body, arriving under the identity of the Nine Extremes Heavenly King.

....Ye Tian followed beside Wind King and Fire King, his gaze fixed on the area not far away, “0.47”

In that region, the laws were extremely chaotic, especially the spatial laws, which were constantly fluctuating. One could vaguely sense a vast world there.

This world contained powerful forbidden laws, clearly making it no ordinary world.

“Wind King, is our Black Wind Mountain going to compete for the Forbidden Void Realm as well?”

Ye Tian transmitted his voice to ask.

“That depends on the situation, but most likely we won’t fight for it. After all, our Black Wind Mountain has a small boundary realm whose concealment is even better than that of the Forbidden Void Realm.

However, the cultivation environment of the Forbidden Void Realm far surpasses that of a small boundary realm, and the Forbidden Void Realm possesses many forbidden treasures. In the future, it will also gradually give birth to forbidden wonders.

Therefore, in terms of value, a Forbidden Void Realm is enough to rival a small boundary realm! But at present, Black Wind Mountain does not lack small boundary realms.”

Wind King explained.

Black Wind Mountain might not care too much about a Forbidden Void Realm, but that did not mean the experts of Black Wind Mountain did not care about it personally.

Take Wind King for example—if he really managed to seize the Forbidden Void Realm, he would certainly be delighted! After all, a Forbidden Void Realm could be used to develop his own forces, serve as his main base, and expand his army.

As time passed, the law fluctuations born from the Forbidden Void Realm reached a peak and then gradually calmed down. Once they became completely calm, that would mean the Forbidden Void Realm had fully stabilized.

About half a month passed, and the Forbidden Void Realm finally stabilized completely.

At that point, the experts of the various major forces all began investigating this Forbidden Void Realm.

Wind King also investigated it. Using a special secret technique to cross the void, he sent a strand of consciousness into the Forbidden Void Realm, and soon came to understand its general condition.

“It’s a small Forbidden Void Realm!”

Wind King said with some disappointment.

“A small Forbidden Void Realm, huh!”

Ye Tian had also learned from the records of Black Wind Mountain about the classification of Forbidden Void Realms: they were divided into small, medium, and large Forbidden Void Realms, among which the most valuable were undoubtedly the large Forbidden Void Realms.

The differences between small Forbidden Void Realms and medium or large Forbidden Void Realms lay in the strength of their laws, the size of the world, and the quantity and quality of forbidden treasures.

Of course, these were not the true differences.

The laws of a small Forbidden Void Realm were incomplete, with special limitations.

Medium and large Forbidden Void Realms generally had relatively complete laws and almost no restrictions. A Forbidden Void Realm without restrictions was much easier to transform and perfect, while one with restrictions was somewhat difficult to remodel.

Of course, incomplete laws were not without benefits. Some Forbidden Void Realms with incomplete laws had relatively faster time flow, and that was an advantage! For example, cultivating inside such a Forbidden Void Realm was far faster than in the outside world, because time flowed more quickly within it, which was equivalent to cultivating inside a time array.

However, overall, the value of a small Forbidden Void Realm was far inferior to that of a medium Forbidden Void Realm.

As one pinnaclely powerful Dao Ancestor after another probed this small Forbidden Void Realm with their consciousness and investigated its incomplete laws, they gradually came to understand some of its basic conditions.

Boom!!! Ancestor Xumi Dao of the Vast Sky Sect was proficient in the Dao of Space. He tore through the void and attempted to step into the small Forbidden Void Realm, but he became stuck within the traversed space, unable to fully enter the Forbidden Void Realm, as though some unseen law was repelling his entry.

Thus, Ancestor Xumi Dao withdrew.

“The laws of this small Forbidden Void Realm are incomplete. It possesses laws that repel pinnaclely powerful Dao Ancestors. I’m afraid the strongest it allows are only Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors! In addition, the flow of time inside is roughly 100 times that of the outside world!”

Ancestor Xumi Dao judged.

“100 times time flow!”

Quite a few forces were immediately tempted. This was a very decent rate of time flow! Although time arrays could also be set up outside, and even ten-thousandfold time flow could be arranged with ease, setting up a time array required resources, and cultivating within one also consumed resources... But if one cultivated in a small Forbidden Void Realm, no resources were needed at all. That was time acceleration naturally built into the Forbidden Void Realm itself! Moreover, pinnaclely powerful Dao Ancestors could not enter, which meant there was an opportunity—those forces with Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors all had the qualifications to contend for this Forbidden Void Realm.

“How about letting our Heavenly Emperor Palace have this Forbidden Void Realm?”

A Dao Ancestor spoke up.

This man was the pinnaclely powerful Dao Ancestor of the Heavenly Emperor Palace—Ancestor Xuanhe Dao. He was much stronger than Ancestor Lantian Dao, and even among pinnaclely powerful Dao Ancestors, he was considered outstanding, in no way inferior to Wind King.

Ancestor Xumi Dao looked at Ancestor Xuanhe Dao and said somewhat displeased, “The Forbidden Void Realm is of such immense value. Your Heavenly Emperor Palace wants it, and we want it too. Let everyone compete fairly. Why should we hand it over just because your Heavenly Emperor Palace says so?”

Ancestor Xumi Dao’s words resonated with many people, and they all began criticizing Ancestor Xuanhe Dao.

At this moment, Wind King spoke: “I also suggest fair competition. Since this Forbidden Void Realm only allows at most Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors to enter, then let Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors and those below that level go in. Whoever obtains however many benefits, and whoever can refine the Forbidden Void Realm, that will depend on their own ability. How about it?”

Refining a Forbidden Void Realm was very difficult 2.

2Very difficult, and it required a long time. And before fully occupying a Forbidden Void Realm, who would have the time to refine it? Therefore, this time, at most, they would only be able to enter the Forbidden Void Realm and harvest some forbidden wonders. As for anything else, there was no way to accomplish it.

Of course, Wind King’s suggestion was also approved by most forces. Although Ancestor Xuanhe Dao of the Heavenly Emperor Palace was somewhat displeased, he had no way to stand against all the other forces.

“Fine, I agree.”

Ancestor Xuanhe Dao nodded.

After that.

One Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor after another arrived in succession. They had all received notice to enter the Forbidden Void Realm and seize resources. If there was any possibility, they were to do their utmost to refine the Forbidden Void Realm and take possession of it.

Of course, this was not being strictly demanded, because the chances were not very high.

Chapter 1176: Forbidden Spirit Root!

Chapter 1176: Forbidden Spirit Root

!【Fourth Update】

“Nine Extremes Heavenly King, are you going into the Forbidden Void Realm as well?”

Seeing that Ye Tian was about to enter, the Wind King asked.

The Wind King also knew that Ye Tian possessed a perfected forbidden body and forbidden weaponry, so his ability to preserve his life was naturally very strong. He could not be treated as an ordinary top-tier Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor.

“Be careful!”

the Wind King reminded him.

He did not know whether the one who had come was Ye Tian’s true body or a clone, so a reminder was still a good thing.

Ye Tian entered this small Forbidden Void Realm. However, before entering, he glanced toward the Heavenly Emperor Palace and saw one person—Dao Ancestor Longfei! Ye Tian had long since investigated the Feng Family to which Fengyang Imperial Son of the Heavenly Emperor Palace belonged, and the ancestor of the Feng Family was precisely Dao Ancestor Longfei.

“Ancestor of the Feng Family, a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor!”

If it were some powerful Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors, Ye Tian would have no confidence in killing them. But Dao Ancestor Longfei was relatively weak among Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors, the sort who had barely forced his way into the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor realm through certain special secret arts, with almost all his potential exhausted.

A Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor like that did not have particularly strong combat power, and his flaws were considerable.

However, he was still, after all, a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor. It would still be rather difficult for Ye Tian to kill him and would require a long time.

“I’ll go in first. If there’s a chance, I’ll kill him then!”

Ye Tian thought to himself.

Forbidden Void Realm.

One Dao Ancestor after another entered. Basically all of them were Dao Ancestors of the Fifth Heaven and above. Those below the Fifth Heaven did not dare come in, otherwise the mortality rate would be too high.

Of course, the majority were still Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors.

These Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors basically all came from major powers of the upper three heavens, with a small number being independent cultivators.

As soon as all the Dao Ancestors entered, they scattered in all directions, afraid of being surrounded and killed by others.

“The laws here are so powerful. Space is far too stable!”

As soon as Ye Tian entered, he sensed the laws here and muttered.

And this was only a small Forbidden Void Realm, with incomplete laws. One could well imagine just how powerful the laws of a true medium-sized Forbidden Void Realm would be.

No wonder it was said that even invincible Dao Ancestors and half-step Domain Ancestors could not shake a Forbidden Void Realm. Once one controlled a Forbidden Void Realm, it basically meant possessing a secure rear base.

Since this Forbidden Void Realm had only recently been born, it was relatively empty. Many regions took the form of whirlpools, as if they were gestating certain continents and stars.

This place was just like a real world! Many Dao Ancestors immediately began searching for continents and planets that had already formed, because only there would forbidden treasures be born.

Before long, the Dao Ancestors had all disappeared from sight, and Ye Tian casually chose a direction and flew off.

He could not kill Dao Ancestor Longfei in a short time anyway, so there was no need to chase after him. It would be better to first search for some forbidden treasures.

Since the Forbidden Void Realm had only just come into being, there were indeed quite a few treasures.

Sure enough, before Ye Tian had flown for long, he discovered a void continent.

Whoosh! Above the void continent, Ye Tian descended.

Sweeping it with his divine sense, he discovered quite a few forbidden treasures.

“About more than thirty forbidden treasures!”

Ye Tian was overjoyed.

To find more than thirty forbidden treasures this easily was far easier than searching for them one by one.

Suddenly.

Ye Tian turned his gaze into the distance and looked at a Dao Ancestor rapidly flying over.

Judging from his aura, the other party was a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor, not too powerful.

“Get lost!”

Ye Tian gripped the Forbidden Spear and hurled it viciously.

In the distance, when that Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor saw the Forbidden Spear stabbing toward him, he defended with all his strength and kept retreating.

Moreover, he recognized Ye Tian’s identity. He was a top-tier Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor and also possessed a perfected forbidden body—someone he could not afford to offend.

So, he left! Seeing that Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor depart, Ye Tian sped up and collected these forbidden treasures.

Inside his inner world, he had long since raised a batch of forbidden bloodline creatures, and now he happened to release them to draw away the great terrors triggered by the forbidden treasures.

Of course, not all forbidden treasures contained great terror, so Ye Tian did not waste too many forbidden bloodline creatures.

Before long, Ye Tian took away all thirty-plus forbidden treasures and then left.

After Ye Tian departed, a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor arrived. Seeing that there were no forbidden treasures left on this void continent, he could not help but sigh regretfully before flying away again.

And so it went.

One forbidden treasure after another in the Forbidden Void Realm was taken away by the Dao Ancestors. Occasionally, certain void continents containing large quantities of forbidden treasures attracted multiple Dao Ancestors, and the Dao Ancestors fought each other madly just to seize the treasures.

If they were only low-grade forbidden treasures, then they would not be worth the Dao Ancestors fighting over.

But many of the forbidden treasures born in the Forbidden Void Realm were mid-grade forbidden treasures. High-grade forbidden treasures were also plentiful, and even top-grade forbidden treasures were not particularly rare.

If one were lucky, one might even find a forbidden pinnacle treasure! On this day.

Ye Tian was searching for forbidden treasures. By now, he had already obtained nearly several thousand forbidden treasures, including even dozens of top-grade forbidden treasures. His harvest could be said to be extremely abundant.

Abruptly.

Waves of battle fluctuations came from afar, and the auras were extremely chaotic. Clearly, multiple Dao Ancestors were fighting.

“I’ll go take a look!”

Ye Tian flew over.

Very quickly, he saw the scene of the battle.

Roughly several hundred Dao Ancestors were fighting over a giant tree. The giant tree had been chopped into sections, and from every section of its trunk and branches flowed drops of black substance, radiating forbidden aura.

“That is...”

Ye Tian’s pupils suddenly contracted, his eyes filled with excitement and greed.

If his guess was correct, then that giant tree should be the exceedingly rare, almost legendary forbidden spirit root! Heaven-and-earth spirit roots were practically the best cultivation resources and treasures. For example, certain divine medicines also belonged to a kind of heaven-and-earth spirit root. Among forbidden treasures, there were also forbidden spirit roots. They were the finest cultivation treasures and could greatly increase one’s cultivation.

For example, with Ye Tian’s current cultivation of the Nine Extremes Dao Canon, he still needed to slowly accumulate forbidden dao power; there was no way to achieve it in a single leap.

But forbidden spirit roots were different. They could allow Ye Tian’s forbidden dao power to grow rapidly, sparing him countless years of bitter cultivation.

Once one obtained a forbidden spirit root, as long as one’s potential was sufficient, one’s strength could soar very quickly.

For instance, if a newly advanced Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor obtained a forbidden spirit root, then although there would be basically no hope of reaching the level of a pinnacle Dao Ancestor, he could still step into the peak level of the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor realm in a short time.

“Fight for it!”

Ye Tian made his decision.

He too would fight for the forbidden spirit root. Even if he could seize only one section of it, it would still greatly increase his forbidden dao power. With his potential, he could quickly break through the shackles and advance to Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, instead of needing to slowly cultivate bitterly for endless years before advancing.

Chapter 1177: Breakthrough in Strength, Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor!..

Chapter 1177: Breakthrough in Strength, Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor

!【Fifth Update】

Ye Tian unleashed the Great Thousand Dao Art—Heaven Phantom Divine Step, and rushed into the battlefield with a speed so fast and movement so ghostly it was almost impossible to track.

At the same time, he activated his perfected Forbidden Body, as well as the defensive Dao Arts Nine Revolutions Indestructible Golden Body and Primordial Desolate Body. No matter how the attacks of the other Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors bombarded him, he did not care in the slightest.

The Nine Revolutions Indestructible Golden Body was shattered! The Primordial Desolate Body was also broken! Yet Ye Tian remained completely calm, forcibly enduring the injuries with his Forbidden Body while mobilizing the power of his Forbidden Origin to continuously repair his wounds.

When it came to staying alive, he could be called unrivaled! Just like that, Ye Tian charged through the attacks of one Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor after another and reached the Forbidden Spirit Root. With a single strike of the Primordial Severing Technique, he directly cut off a section of the Forbidden Spirit Root’s branch—and it was no short piece, either.

The Forbidden Spirit Root was extremely sturdy and very difficult to sever, but the Primordial Severing Technique, this Great Thousand Dao Art, specialized in cutting hard objects. That was why it could sever the Forbidden Spirit Root in a single blow. Although the attacks of the other Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors were stronger than Ye Tian’s, it was very difficult for them to cut through the Forbidden Spirit Root in one strike.

For example, fire-element Dao Arts and ice-element Dao Arts—how were those supposed to sever the Forbidden Spirit Root? After Ye Tian cut off the Forbidden Spirit Root, he immediately put away that section of the branch, then used Heaven Phantom Divine Step to flee at high speed.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly King, leave the Forbidden Spirit Root behind!!!”

One Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor after another roared in fury.

Boom!!! Streams of Dao Art attacks slammed into Ye Tian’s body, including attacks from top-tier Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors.

Ye Tian’s body was repeatedly heavily injured and even pierced through. If not for his perfected Forbidden Body and the power of his Forbidden Origin repairing his body, he would likely have been instantly killed long ago.

Even so, after enduring so many attacks, his injuries were extremely severe.

Ye Tian naturally did not dare continue trying to snatch the remaining Forbidden Spirit Root—that would have been suicidal behavior.

As Ye Tian broke out of the encirclement, far fewer Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors continued to pursue him. After all, Ye Tian’s ability to survive was far too strong. If others chased after him, they would instead lose the chance to continue fighting over the Forbidden Spirit Root, and that simply was not worth it.

Before long, no one was chasing Ye Tian anymore.

....In the Forbidden Void Realm, within an uninhabited stretch of void.

Ye Tian set up a simple concealment formation, then hid inside it and began treating his injuries.

At this moment, Ye Tian looked utterly miserable. One of his arms had vanished, his body was riddled with holes, and his blood had nearly run dry.

And those were only the surface injuries. Inside his body, strands of law power were wreaking havoc on his flesh. If not for his perfected Forbidden Body offsetting much of the damage, he would probably already be dead beyond doubt.

Moreover, if an ordinary Dao Ancestor had suffered injuries like these, they would have had to sleep for hundreds of millions of years before even thinking of recovering.

Ye Tian activated a forbidden technique and circulated the power of his Forbidden Origin to repair his body.

Gradually, his injuries recovered. “The power of Forbidden Origin is unbelievably effective at healing injuries!”

Ye Tian said joyfully.

It was precisely because he had an endless supply of Forbidden Origin power that he had dared to charge in like that to seize the Forbidden Spirit Root.

In short, this time his harvest had been enormous.

Accelerating time, before long, Ye Tian’s injuries were completely healed.

After that, he found a relatively hidden place, took out a palace, shrank it down, then cast a concealment formation and began secluded cultivation there.

Inside the palace.

Ye Tian took out the Forbidden Spirit Root. A section of the Forbidden Spirit Root’s trunk nearly three hundred meters long lay on the ground, and drops of Forbidden Spirit Root fluid trickled out from within it.

Ye Tian took out the Forbidden Gourd to collect this Forbidden Spirit Root fluid, and before long he had gathered all of it, leaving behind only the shell of the Forbidden Spirit Root.

This shell also counted as a cultivation resource. If refined, it could likewise increase one’s cultivation, but its usefulness was still far inferior to the Forbidden Spirit Root fluid.

Thus, Ye Tian stored the shell inside his internal world.

Next, Ye Tian began using the Forbidden Spirit Root fluid to cultivate the Nine Extremes Dao Canon.

Boom! A drop of Forbidden Spirit Root fluid entered his mouth: a vast surge of energy flooded through his entire body. Under the refinement of the Nine Extremes Dao Canon, it became newly born forbidden dao power, which then slowly tempered his body and soul and strengthened his cultivation.

Just refining a single drop of Forbidden Spirit Root fluid was enough to rival a thousand years of bitter cultivation in the past.

And refining one drop of Forbidden Spirit Root fluid did not even take an hour. One could well imagine just how astonishingly fast that cultivation speed was.

More importantly, using Forbidden Spirit Root fluid for cultivation came with almost no bottlenecks, whereas bitter cultivation did have bottlenecks and would often lead to periods where one’s cultivation was difficult to improve.

Day after day passed. Ye Tian’s cultivation rose at an incomparably fast speed, and he also accelerated time by ten thousand times. After cultivating for a long time under time acceleration, only a short while had passed in the outside world... so it would not delay anything.

In the blink of an eye, three days had passed in the outside world, while Ye Tian had already cultivated bitterly for 30,000 days under the time formation.

By now, he had refined more than half of the Forbidden Spirit Root fluid. His forbidden dao power had become dozens of times more abundant, and his combat strength had directly crossed the bottleneck between a Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestor and a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor.

Now, he was already a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, and a fairly powerful one at that.

“.

I can bring the remaining Forbidden Spirit Root fluid back for Yue’er, Xingchen, Xingyue, and the others. Besides, even if I refine all of what remains, I won’t be able to increase my... strength by much more!”

Ye Tian muttered.

This time, the Forbidden Void Realm had produced a rare forbidden treasure like the Forbidden Spirit Root, which meant this Forbidden Void Realm absolutely had other Forbidden Spirit Roots as well.

He still wanted to seize more Forbidden Spirit Roots. If that happened, his growth speed would definitely become astonishingly fast. Even if he wanted to advance into the ranks of the Pinnacle Dao Ancestors, it would not take too long. Otherwise, no matter how monstrous his talent was, it would still be difficult for him to enter the Pinnacle Dao Ancestor level in a short time.

In addition, he also wanted to kill Dao Ancestor Long Fei.

With his current strength, he was absolutely nearly ninety percent certain he could kill the other party, and he did not need to worry about the man escaping.

“My next two goals: find Forbidden Spirit Roots and kill Dao Ancestor Long Fei!”

Ye Tian came out of seclusion, put away the palace, removed the formation, and turned into a streak of light that vanished without a trace.

Does Zhao Shao “Damn it, my injuries are too severe!”

Dao Ancestor Long Fei dragged his heavily wounded body through the void, constantly darting and changing direction.

He had already used several life-saving treasures to barely avoid being surrounded and killed by several Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors. If he did not still have some reserves left, he would already have been finished.

Then, he became excited again.

This time, he had been the first to spot a black flower containing 108 petals. After appraising it, he determined that the black flower was no ordinary forbidden oddity, but an extremely rare Forbidden Spirit Root. Every single petal was enough to greatly increase one’s cultivation.

He knew that his own potential was nearly exhausted, and he had no hope of entering the ranks of the Supreme Dao Ancestors. But if he could refine that Forbidden Spirit Root flower, then it would allow his dao power to break through its shackles and continue rising.

He had hope of becoming one of the very strongest Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors, looking down upon those weaker Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors.

Chapter 1178: Dao Ancestor Long Fei, Delivering Himself and Treasure..

Chapter 1178: Dao Ancestor Long Fei, Delivering Himself and Treasure

!【Sixth Update】

To ensure his absolute safety, Dao Ancestor Long Fei changed direction several more times, erased all traces of his travel, concealed his aura, and opened up a tiny hidden space inside a small star to hide himself.

With that, he felt he should be completely safe now and absolutely wouldn’t be discovered.

“First, heal my injuries, then use that forbidden spirit root flower to raise my cultivation!”

Dao Ancestor Long Fei thought to himself.

Not long after, a figure passed by this tiny star.

That person was Ye Tian.

As usual, Ye Tian swept his divine sense over this small star, then covered it with his replication talent for a moment. This was his habit.

Originally, he didn’t think he would gain anything.

But the key point was that his replication talent had actually detected the presence of a Dao Ancestor.

Judging by the name displayed through the talent’s information, the other party was shockingly Dao Ancestor Long Fei of the Feng family.

Ye Tian was very surprised.

And from the looks of it, Dao Ancestor Long Fei seemed to be injured, and his wounds had yet to recover.

Boom! The star shattered, and the concealed formation arranged by Dao Ancestor Long Fei was broken as well, revealing his figure.

At this moment, Dao Ancestor Long Fei was furious. He had hidden himself so carefully on this star, blending in almost completely, yet someone had still blown up the star and exposed him.

But when he looked closer, he became even more enraged.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly King, it’s you!”

Dao Ancestor Long Fei was extremely irritated.

Although the outside world said that the Nine Extremes Heavenly King and Dao Ancestor Myriad Laws were two different people, and the two of them had indeed appeared together on many occasions, their methods of attack were just too similar, almost exactly the same.

Therefore, even if they really were two different people, their relationship had to be extremely close—perhaps even blood brothers.

So, Dao Ancestor Long Fei also hated the Nine Extremes Heavenly King deeply.

However, he was sensible enough not to fight the Nine Extremes Heavenly King and instead fled at once.

There was no helping it. Earlier, when Ye Tian had fought Dao Ancestor Fenghuo, a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor from the Heavenly Emperor Palace, he had not been at a disadvantage at all, while Long Fei himself was weaker than Dao Ancestor Fenghuo.

He believed that the Nine Extremes Heavenly King’s strength should be no weaker than Dao Ancestor Myriad Laws, so there was no way he could kill the Nine Extremes Heavenly King.

What’s more, his injuries still hadn’t recovered, and he needed to heal as soon as possible.

Once he fully healed and refined the forbidden spirit root flower, after his strength soared, it still wouldn’t be too late to come back and kill the Nine Extremes Heavenly King.

“Trying to run?”

Ye Tian let out a cold laugh.

His forbidden domain unfolded, covering the area and suppressing and binding Dao Ancestor Long Fei.

Unlike when he had fought Dao Ancestor Fenghuo before, back then Ye Tian had only been a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor, so the binding effect had been poor. But now he was a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, and his strength surpassed Dao Ancestor Long Fei’s. Thus, under the suppression of the forbidden domain and the Ten Directions Fixing Space Art, Dao Ancestor Long Fei was directly left with no way to escape.

“Primordial Slash Technique!”

A thread of light instantly swept across Dao Ancestor Long Fei’s body, breaking through layer after layer of his defenses and cutting him directly into two halves.

“Infinite Spatial Divine Spear!”

Another offensive Great Thousand Dao Technique was unleashed, piercing through Dao Ancestor Long Fei’s body at an inconceivable speed.

Dao Ancestor Long Fei was terrified.

After killing Dao Ancestor Long Fei, Ye Tian began sorting through his belongings.

Dao Ancestor Long Fei was very, very poor. He had nothing particularly good on him, only the more than 200 forbidden artifacts he had found during this trip into the Forbidden Void Realm.

Even so, Ye Tian was already very satisfied. After all, the value of 200 forbidden artifacts was already enormous.

“Eh, this forbidden treasure is...”

Ye Tian saw that black flower. The forbidden laws it emitted were different from those of the other forbidden artifacts, and just by smelling it, the power of his Dao throughout his body surged, as if it had improved ever so slightly.

A little.

“A forbidden spirit root!!!”

Ye Tian was greatly shocked.

He had not expected Dao Ancestor Long Fei to actually have a forbidden spirit root on him, and a complete one at that! Although the grade of this forbidden spirit root flower might not compare to that forbidden spirit root tree, the forbidden spirit root tree he had obtained was incomplete, so the forbidden spirit root liquid he got from it wasn’t very much. In terms of value, it was absolutely not as valuable as this forbidden spirit root flower.

At this moment, Ye Tian finally understood where Dao Ancestor Long Fei’s injuries had come from! As a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, if Dao Ancestor Long Fei had merely been competing with other Dao Ancestors for ordinary forbidden artifacts, he wouldn’t have been injured this badly.

But if he had been fighting over a forbidden spirit root, then suffering such heavy injuries was only natural.

“Dao Ancestor Long Fei really is a good man. Not only did he deliver himself to me, he even specially delivered a forbidden spirit root as well!”

Ye Tian couldn’t help sighing.

He had decided—when he took revenge on the Feng family in the future, he would be a little merciful and at least leave them an intact corpse.

Dao Ancestor Long Fei naturally had no idea what Ye Tian was thinking. Otherwise, he would probably have been angered into vomiting blood even in death.

Soon after.

Ye Tian left this place and continued searching for forbidden artifacts.

At present, with his strength, he no longer needed to fear other Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors unless they were the truly monstrous kind. Otherwise, there was simply no way they could kill him.

In the blink of an eye, ten days passed.

In the Heavenly Demon Sect, Young Master Gui’s status was in no way inferior to that of those few Eighth Heaven pinnacle Dao Ancestors.

As time slowly passed, Young Master Ghost accumulated more and more injuries, and his combat strength also began to decline. This was a very bad sign.

Young Master Ghost hurled out a black long nail. It was astonishingly a top-tier forbidden relic, and a one-time-use offensive forbidden relic at that. Driven by his peak Seventh Heaven power, it was enough to be considered a terrifying killing weapon.

And the target he threw it at was not Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw, Dao Ancestor Evil Buddha, or Dao Ancestor Subduing Demon, but Nine Extremes Heavenly King Ye Tian.

Although Ye Tian sensed the attack, he had no time to dodge it.

The Primordial Desolate Body was shattered, and even the Nine Revolutions Indestructible Golden Body failed to block it. Layer after layer of defenses was blown apart before it directly pierced through Ye Tian’s forbidden body.

Even his major-completion-level forbidden body was severely injured, which showed just how terrifying the power of this strike was.

However, this strike still did not kill him; it only severely wounded Ye Tian.

“Power of forbidden origin, restore!”

Under the repair of an enormous amount of forbidden origin power, his injuries recovered at a speed visible to the naked eye.

Seeing this, Young Master Ghost was dumbfounded. His strike had actually failed to kill Ye Tian.

“Damn it, this guy is actually a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, and a very strong one at that. Didn’t the intelligence say this guy was at most a Sixth Heaven Dao Ancestor, only a little stronger than ordinary Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors?”

Young Master Ghost said furiously.

Although Young Master Ghost had failed to kill Ye Tian, Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw, Dao Ancestor Evil Buddha, and Dao Ancestor Subduing Demon seized the opening created when Young Master Ghost had gone all out to attack Ye Tian and directly unleashed their trump-card attacks.

Three terrifying killing moves pierced straight through Young Master Ghost’s body, instantly inflicting heavy injuries on him.

This severe injury immediately pushed Young Master Ghost into a desperate situation.

Young Master Ghost continuously flickered through the Ghost Domain, while Ye Tian and Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw’s group relentlessly pursued him.

More importantly, keeping the Ghost Domain active continuously consumed Young Master Ghost’s power.

Very soon, Young Master Ghost directly withdrew the Ghost Domain.

“You deal with Young Master Ghost. I’ll go help the other Dao Ancestors!”

Dao Ancestor Evil Buddha said.

“Alright!”

Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw nodded.

Anyway... Young Master Ghost had already been heavily injured. With just him and Dao Ancestor Subduing Demon, the two of them were enough to suppress Young Master Ghost.

Besides, just now the Ghost Domain had enveloped the whole battlefield, and the Dao Ancestors of the three Ninth Heaven factions and the three Eighth Heaven factions had been suppressed miserably. Now each of them was badly injured. If they did not help those Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors, the major factions would probably lose quite a few Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors.

Swish! Dao Ancestor Evil Buddha joined the battlefield of the other Dao Ancestors and helped them kill the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace and the Heavenly Demon Sect.

Dao Ancestor Evil Buddha was immensely powerful. Joining forces with the other Dao Ancestors, he easily suppressed one Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor after another, and the situation reversed in an instant.

Very soon, one Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor after another fell.

Before long, the number of Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors from the Heavenly Emperor Palace who had fallen reached twenty. Such losses were enough to make the Heavenly Emperor Palace truly feel the pain.

On the other side.

Under the combined assault of Ye Tian, Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw, and Dao Ancestor Subduing Demon, Young Master Ghost kept coughing up blood.

Ye Tian was no longer afraid of the heavily injured Young Master Ghost and no longer needed to stay in the rear. Instead, he attacked while supporting, battering Young Master Ghost until cracks continuously spread across his body.

“No, if this goes on, I’m afraid I’ll die here!”

Young Master Ghost thought to himself.

He did not want to die. He still wanted to advance to a pinnacle Dao Ancestor, then rise further to an invincible Dao Ancestor. How could he possibly fall here? As for the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s orders, what did that have to do with him?

The Heavenly Demon Sect and the Heavenly Emperor Palace were only cooperating. On the surface they had submitted, but the Heavenly Demon Sect still had ample autonomy.

Now that he was on the verge of falling, it was only normal for him not to help the Heavenly Emperor Palace, and the Heavenly Emperor Palace would have no grounds to rebuke him for it.

Immediately.

Young Master Ghost used an escape-type pinnacle treasure to tear through space and leave, not daring to remain here any longer.

“Don’t chase him! Young Master Ghost has no shortage of treasures on him. If we really try to pursue him, who knows how long we’d have to chase. Stopping Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle from refining the Forbidden Void Realm is the urgent matter!”

Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw hurriedly said.

Ye Tian and Dao Ancestor Subduing Demon also had no intention of chasing him. The three of them rushed toward Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle’s location, intending to break the great array protecting him.

At this moment, the other Dao Ancestors of the Heavenly Emperor Palace were completely tied down and had no way to stop Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw and the others. “Not good, this great array won’t hold for long!”

Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle’s expression changed drastically.

But he was currently focusing all his power on refining the Forbidden Void Realm and could at most spare a sliver of attention; there was simply no way for him to counterattack.

Rumble!!! Dao Ancestor Heavenly Claw and the others attacked the great array continuously. After only a few strikes, the formation was already on the verge of shattering.

At this moment.

Gritting his teeth, Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle painfully took out a forbidden pinnacle treasure that the Heavenly Emperor Palace had entrusted to him.

This was a forbidden pinnacle treasure that could trap people, and it only had a one-time effect. Even a pinnacle Dao Ancestor could be trapped with ease by it, making it unimaginably valuable.

Once used, this forbidden pinnacle treasure would be gone.

The Heavenly Emperor Palace had instructed that this forbidden pinnacle treasure was not to be used unless absolutely necessary.

“What is this?”

Heavenly Claw Dao Ancestor looked at that layer of light with great confusion.

He tried attacking it, but he could not shake the light curtain at all. Moreover, under the light curtain’s coverage, the void in this area was completely sealed, their speed became extremely slow, and they were utterly unable to use other treasures to warp out.

In other words, they were trapped in this region.

Heavenly Claw Dao Ancestor said coldly.

Chapter 1183: Half the Authority!

Chapter 1183: Half the Authority

! [Fourth Update]

Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle was taken away by Dao Ancestor Black Crane. He did not resist, because even if he had, he would not have been able to.

Dao Ancestor Black Crane was a top-tier Pinnacle Dao Ancestor. No matter how powerful Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle was, he was still far from being a match for Dao Ancestor Black Crane.

At first glance, the gap between a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor and an Eighth-Heaven Dao Ancestor was only one level, but in truth, the difference in strength was enormous.

Eighth-Heaven Dao Ancestors were known as Pinnacle Dao Ancestors, while Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors had no such title at all. That alone was enough to explain the issue.

Under normal circumstances, if Dao Ancestors differed by one heaven in cultivation, even if one could not win, escape was still possible. But when a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor encountered an Eighth-Heaven Supreme Dao Ancestor, escape was generally impossible. Unless it was a peak Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor meeting a newly advanced Eighth-Heaven Dao Ancestor, there might be a chance to contend for a bit—but only for a few exchanges. Once the fight dragged on, defeat and death would still be inevitable.

Therefore, Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle knew that resistance had no meaning whatsoever.

....Many people from other factions all thought that Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle had brought this upon himself. He had clearly refined the Forbidden Void Realm, yet deliberately pretended he had not. Some people may have had suspicions, but none dared be certain.

But Ye Tian felt that Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle perhaps really had not refined the Forbidden Void Realm. After all, Stone Eagle was a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor and would likely advance to an Eighth-Heaven Dao Ancestor before long. He would not be foolish enough to betray the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Moreover, while the Forbidden Void Realm was important to a faction, it was not all that important to an individual. There was no need for Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle to monopolize Forbidden Void Realm 047.

Thus, he believed that someone else must have taken control of the Forbidden Void Realm.

This small Forbidden Void Realm only allowed Dao Ancestors below the Eighth Heaven to enter, and ordinary Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors indeed did not have the ability to secretly refine a Forbidden Void Realm without attracting anyone’s attention.

But Ye Tian believed there was one person who could accomplish such a feat, and that was Ouyang Jiu'er.

Since the Forbidden Void Realm had opened until now, he had not seen Ouyang Jiu'er at all.

Given Ouyang Jiu'er's temperament, she should not have missed such an opportunity. After all, she never thought there were too many forbidden treasures and would certainly come to gather them.

At this moment.

The Forbidden Void Realm had already been refined by someone and was completely sealed off.

Not to mention that the Pinnacle Dao Ancestors could not enter in the first place—even if they could have, now they still would not be able to.

Therefore, the Dao Ancestors of the various factions left one after another.

Ye Tian also returned to human territory. He did not go looking for Ouyang Jiu'er. Even if Ouyang Jiu'er had refined the Forbidden Void Realm, it had nothing to do with him. So, not asking was the best choice.

However, after several months had passed, Ouyang Jiu'er unexpectedly came to find Ye Tian on her own initiative.

“Big Brother Ye, I’ll take you somewhere!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said mysteriously.

Ye Tian already had a guess in his heart, and followed Ouyang Jiu'er away.

Very soon, the two crossed through the void and arrived in an empty world.

The moment Ye Tian entered, he knew this place was the Forbidden Void Realm.

“This is the Forbidden Void Realm. So it really was you, Jiu'er, who refined the Forbidden Void Realm!”

Ye Tian muttered.

“That’s right, I’m the one who refined the Forbidden Void Realm!”

Ouyang Jiu'er nodded.

From Ouyang Jiu'er's explanation, Ye Tian finally understood how she had refined the Forbidden Void Realm.

As it turned out, Ouyang Jiu'er possessed a treasure—the World-Suppressing Stele—originating from the Dark Forbidden Domain. It could suppress the origin of any world; even the origin of the Forbidden Void Realm could likewise be suppressed by it.

Thus, Ouyang Jiu'er brought the World-Suppressing Stele into the Forbidden Void Realm, directly suppressed the origin of the Forbidden Void Realm, then secretly infiltrated the place where its origin was located and forcibly refined the origin of the Forbidden Void Realm, thereby taking control of it.

Because its origin had been suppressed, the Forbidden Void Realm was completely unable to produce any anomalies, and there was no way for Ouyang Jiu'er's presence to be exposed.

As for Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle refining the Forbidden Void Realm, Ouyang Jiu'er had known about it from the very beginning and had deliberately let him do it in order to draw attention away for her.

In reality, Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle had no way of succeeding in refining it at all.

In order to make Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle take the blame, Ouyang Jiu'er deliberately made him feel that he was about to succeed in refining it, then silently moved the other Dao Ancestors out one by one, leaving Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle to be moved out last.

This way, everyone would think that Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle had refined the Forbidden Void Realm, and no one would suspect her. In fact, suspicion would never fall on her at all.

“Big Brother Ye, I’ll transfer half of the authority over the Forbidden Void Realm to you!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said.

“Why? This is the Forbidden Void Realm!”

Ye Tian was greatly shocked.

“To me, the Forbidden Void Realm is only so-so. I’m not building a faction, so what use do I have for such a Forbidden Void Realm? Besides, it won’t be long before I advance to Pinnacle Dao Ancestor. Once that happens, my true body won’t be able to come in either! Unless I use the authority of the realm lord to let an avatar come in, but that would be meaningless!”

Ouyang Jiu'er said.

After Ouyang Jiu'er persuaded him again and again, Ye Tian finally accepted half of the authority over this Forbidden Void Realm.

To him, the Forbidden Void Realm held great significance.

He could completely and secretly transfer a portion of the human race’s geniuses into the Forbidden Void Realm, then secretly train the Nine Extremes Legion. Not even Black Wind Mountain would know the true strength of the Nine Extremes Legion. These were all his private forces.

More importantly, the Forbidden Void Realm was highly suitable for cultivation. If the human race cultivated here, their cultivation speed would be extraordinarily fast.

Next, Ye Tian began preparing to relocate some of the human race’s elites as well as some geniuses from the Nine Extremes Legion, sending them into the Forbidden Void Realm.

Ordinary human geniuses did not know what the Forbidden Void Realm was. Their level was too low, and they had no access to secrets of this caliber. That was something only Dao Ancestors concerned themselves with.

But the Nine Extremes Legion had heard some things about the Forbidden Void Realm, so they were extremely shocked. After all, the outside world said that the Forbidden Void Realm had been refined by the Heavenly Emperor Palace, yet unexpectedly it had fallen into Ye Tian’s hands.

Immediately, their admiration for Ye Tian became boundless, and they also felt fortunate that they could enter the Forbidden Void Realm to cultivate.

On the other side.

Heavenly Emperor Palace.

After discussion among multiple Emperors, they ultimately approved Dao Ancestor Black Crane’s request to extract the memories from Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle’s soul origin. This was the final judgment, and no one could plead for mercy.

On the judgment platform.

An Emperor personally carried out the extraction of Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle’s soul-origin memories. Before the extraction began, Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle cried out loudly in supplication: “Emperor Minghe, it really wasn’t me! I beg you, don’t extract my soul-origin memories! I can swear a life-bound oath!!!!”

However, it was useless! Life-bound oaths still had some effect on lower-level Dao Ancestors, but for Supreme Dao Ancestors they were of little use. And although Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle was not a Pinnacle Dao Ancestor, he still had ways to circumvent a life-bound oath.

Therefore, extracting soul-origin memories was the most reliable method, bar none.

Emperor Minghe placed one hand on Dao Ancestor Stone Eagle’s forehead and began forcibly extracting his soul-origin memories.

0Under the refining of the Nine Extremes Dao Canon, Ye Tian’s forbidden dao power continuously absorbed the energy of the Forbidden Spiritual Root Flower petal, rising rapidly, then tempering his body and soul as his overall cultivation steadily soared.

In the blink of an eye, ten thousand years had passed in the outside world.

But for Ye Tian and the others, an incomparably long span of time had passed.

First was the Human Race. A great number of geniuses cultivated within the Forbidden Void Realm, and one after another they became pinnacle True Ancestors. It was just a pity that these Human Race geniuses had limited potential and lacked the support of Dao-level innate talents, so they had no way to break into the invincible True Ancestor level. Otherwise, the Human Race might have produced some invincible True Ancestors as well! According to what Ye Tian had learned, the Human Race currently possessed seventy-two pinnacle True Ancestors and several thousand top-tier True Ancestors.

Moreover, the number of Dao Ancestors in the Human Race had also increased quite a lot, already reaching several hundred. Among them, there were already six Third Heaven Dao Ancestors 66, and dozens of Second Heaven Dao Ancestors.

These figures did not include the Nine Extremes Legion! The Nine Extremes Legion had been cultivated on a large scale by Ye Tian, and its growth speed was even more astonishing. A full three invincible True Ancestors had been born, and those three invincible True Ancestors had been granted Dao-level innate talents by Ye Tian, bestowed in the name of special treasures.

Moreover, those three invincible Dao Ancestors had also made soulbound oaths never to divulge the secret and to remain loyal to Ye Tian. Otherwise, Ye Tian would not possibly have spent such a great price to nurture them.

Aside from that, the number of True Ancestors in the Nine Extremes Legion had already reached sixty thousand, all of them powerful True Ancestors of elite level or above, including over a thousand pinnacle True Ancestors.

And for this, the resources Ye Tian had spent were beyond calculation刀.

Chapter 1185: The Limit of the Seventh Heaven!

Chapter 1185: The Limit of the Seventh Heaven

!【Sixth Update】

In truth, the Jiuji Legion’s sixty thousand True Ancestors was not a large number, but what mattered to a legion was quality, not quantity.

Every one of these sixty thousand True Ancestors had the potential to advance into a top-tier True Ancestor. From that alone, one could tell just how terrifying these sixty thousand True Ancestors were.

It could be said that, at the True Ancestor level, the human race’s strength was no weaker than that of ordinary Upper Three Heavens factions. Only at the Dao Ancestor level were they still much weaker, but that required time to accumulate and could not be made up for in a short period.

And Ye Tian’s family had improved tremendously as well.

With vast amounts of resources piled onto them, Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue had greatly increased their strength by cultivating forbidden arts, and they had also cultivated one Medium Thousand Dao Art after another to the limit. Their strength had both reached the very peak of Pinnacle True Ancestors, and their combat power was enough to rival Fourth Heaven Dao Ancestors.

If they were given a little more time to stabilize their realms “0.4.7”

afterward, they could begin trying to break into the Dao Ancestor level. Once they succeeded in becoming Dao Ancestors, they would certainly become Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestors, and after cultivating for some time more, they could advance to Sixth or Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors.

Xiao Yue had improved even faster. She had now broken through her realm and was already a Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestor.

Ye Yu’s improvement was slightly slower, and she had only just reached the peak of Pinnacle True Ancestor.

Ye Tian’s strength had also risen enormously. His forbidden Dao power had increased many times over, and his progress in Major Thousand Dao Arts was also very fast.

Now, one Major Thousand Dao Art after another had reached the major accomplishment realm, and a few of them had even advanced to the perfected realm. For example, the three Major Thousand Dao Arts—Primeval Severing Art, Primeval Desolate Body, and Heavenly Illusion Divine Step—had all been cultivated by Ye Tian to the perfected realm.

However, if he wanted to cultivate Major Thousand Dao Arts to the limit level, that would be much more difficult and would require a very long time.

Yet in terms of combat power, Ye Tian had now already reached the limit of Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor. Even the Heaven Claw Dao Ancestor, Evil Buddha Dao Ancestor, and Demon-Subduing Dao Ancestor from back then, the three of them together, were no longer his match.

After all, even among those at the limit of Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, combat strength could still vary greatly, and that was the result of differences in potential.

But in terms of battle power, Ye Tian felt he was on par with Young Master Gui. Yet if it came to a prolonged life-and-death battle, then with his major accomplishment-level forbidden body and power of forbidden origin, he could definitely wear Young Master Gui down to death.

“If I can comprehend a pinnacle Dao Art, my strength will probably undergo a world-shaking transformation!”

Ye Tian thought to himself.

However, for the time being, he would not try to create a pinnacle Dao Art. After all, his Major Thousand Dao Arts had not yet been cultivated to the limit level. Trying to create a pinnacle Dao Art now would be too big a step, and it would do him no good.

A foundation was extremely important. Only by laying it well could one improve rapidly in the future.

Otherwise, one would end up like Young Master Gui, who had exhausted himself trying to create Ghost Domain. In the end, he had indeed created the pinnacle Dao Art Ghost Domain, but his control over it was poor. It was merely a defective pinnacle Dao Art, and he could only create this one pinnacle Dao Art, having almost completely exhausted all of his inspiration.

Moreover, Young Master Gui’s attainments in his other Major Thousand Dao Arts were not high, so he had clearly overreached himself. Although he had won fame, it had not brought him much actual benefit.

As for the Jiuji Legion and the human race experts, Ye Tian had them remain in the Forbidden Void Realm, otherwise it would be easy for some things to be exposed.

After all, if the human race suddenly became this powerful, there would definitely be a problem. Previously, the development of the human race had been proceeding at a normal rate, but if that speed suddenly increased by a thousandfold, that would be abnormal.

Therefore, Ye Tian had them cultivate here, and they were more than willing to do so. After all, they could cultivate a thousand times faster than those outside, and the energy contained in the Forbidden Void Realm was perfect for cultivation. Occasionally, one could even discover a forbidden wonder-item.

In such a wonderful place, even if told to leave, they would all be reluctant.

Heavenly Emperor Palace, the Feng Family.

At this moment, the Feng family was shrouded in gloom. Every one of them was dejected and in very poor spirits.

Previously, when Imperial Son Fengyang had fallen, the Feng family’s status in the Heavenly Emperor Palace had already dropped considerably. Then ten thousand years ago, the Feng family’s ancestor, the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor Longfei Dao Ancestor, had died in the Forbidden Void Realm, which only made things worse for the Feng family.

Now, the strongest Dao Ancestor in the Feng family was only a Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestor, whose status in the Heavenly Army was not very high.

More importantly, one of the Imperial Lords to whom the Feng family had pledged allegiance had already abandoned them.

Now, the upper echelons of the Heavenly Emperor Palace had made a decision: the Feng family had no real potential left and could no longer remain in the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

The Heavenly Emperor Palace was indeed vast and could accommodate many people, but it was currently recruiting geniuses from the entire Xuanxu Ancient Realm, and thus developing rapidly. Many geniuses were settling into the Heavenly Emperor Palace, and they needed to occupy certain regions as residences. The Feng family, however, no longer had any potential, yet still occupied such a large area as their clan grounds... Thus, the Heavenly Emperor Palace intended to expel the Feng family and have them move to one of the ancient continents under the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s command, handing that ancient continent over to them for management.

In the words of the upper echelons of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, the land the Feng family occupied had expanded by no one knew how many times over, and being given such an ancient continent as their clan grounds was a reward.

But the Feng family knew very well what kind of reward this was—it was exile! Remaining in the Heavenly Emperor Palace meant an excellent cultivation environment and complete safety. No force could attack the Heavenly Emperor Palace, and from time to time the family’s descendants could even listen to the Imperial Lords’ lectures on the Dao. But once exiled to an ancient continent, all of those benefits would be gone, and it would even become difficult to receive intelligence and news in a timely manner.

Moreover, if any enemies wanted to deal with the Feng family, the Heavenly Emperor Palace might not be able to send aid in time.

Even more importantly, in the future, if the Feng family wanted to place their descendants into good positions within the Heavenly Emperor Palace, it would become incomparably difficult.

But the Feng family had no way to resist the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s decision and could only choose to withdraw.

On this day.

After countless members of the Feng family had finished packing up, they boarded an ancient warship and left the Heavenly Emperor Palace, arriving at an ancient continent located 2.

2 far from the Heavenly Emperor Palace—the Luanfeng Continent.

Not long after the Feng family settled into Luanfeng Continent, the Jiuji Legion’s intelligence personnel gathered this information and reported it to Ye Tian.

Human race.

“The Feng family has been expelled from the Heavenly Emperor Palace and is now settled on Luanfeng Continent!”

Ye Tian smiled.

He had not forgotten that he intended to destroy the Feng family. It was just that under the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s protection, never mind if he were a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor—even if he were an invincible Ninth Heaven Dao Ancestor, he would still have had no way to wipe out the Feng family.

But now that the Feng family had left the Heavenly Emperor Palace, they no longer had its protection.

For him to destroy the Feng family now would be as easy as turning over his hand! Whoosh...!! Ye Tian’s figure vanished, and he quickly left the human race, heading for Luanfeng Continent.

Chapter 1187 Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor Was Set Up to Death! Pt..

Chapter 1187: Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor Was Set Up to Death

!【First Update】

“Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor!”

Emperor Guangling was furious. The person shown in the Spacetime Emperor Mirror was none other than Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor, the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor whose soul-origin memories had been extracted ten thousand years ago.

“Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor just so happens to possess an ice-element Dao-level innate talent. He was once an Imperial Son of the Heavenly Emperor Palace and had once been highly valued by the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Last time, the Heavenly Emperor Palace wrongly blamed him and crippled his potential. To make up for it, they also gave him a decent position, putting him in command of a hundred thousand heavenly troops and having him train them at a newly established training base.

But who would have thought that he would actually dare slaughter a family under the Heavenly Emperor Palace!”

Emperor Guangling muttered coldly to himself.

As for why Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor had massacred the Feng Family, he did not know very clearly, nor did he care to find out.

He understood all too well what kind of treasure the Spacetime Emperor Mirror was. It was a top-tier forbidden weapon forged by Vast Sea Domain Ancestor from a top-tier forbidden treasure. No concealment method could escape the Spacetime Emperor Mirror’s detection.

Unless the other party had left behind no traces at all, in which case the Spacetime Emperor Mirror would be unable to absorb any aura and naturally would not be able to detect anything.

But now, after absorbing the other party’s aura, the one it detected was precisely Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor. This kind of detection method was even more reliable than directly extracting soul-origin memories.

Therefore, this matter was a hundred percent certain—it was... done by Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor! With a wave of Emperor Guangling’s hand, he directly shattered Luanfeng Continent into pieces, reducing it completely to ashes, then turned and returned to the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

As soon as he returned to the Heavenly Emperor Palace, Emperor Guangling took out the Spacetime Emperor Mirror avatar and showed the detected scene to the many Emperors.

Instantly, every single Emperor was enraged.

....Heavenly Emperor Palace, No. 6 Heavenly Army Training Camp.

Rumble!!!! One Emperor after another descended, and all the heavenly troops and reserve heavenly troops immediately knelt in worship.

“Greetings, Emperors!”

“Greetings, Emperors!”

Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor also appeared and quickly bowed, saying, “Stone Eagle greets all the Emperors!”

But he soon realized that something was wrong. These Emperors were radiating anger, and every one of their auras was locked onto him.

“What’s going on? Could it be because I’ve been slacking off lately and haven’t trained the heavenly troops properly? But that shouldn’t be enough for so many Emperors to come question me, right?”

Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor was utterly puzzled.

At this moment.

Emperor Guangling said coldly, “Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor, you slaughtered the Feng Family under the Heavenly Emperor Palace. Your conduct is extremely vile. The Heavenly Emperor Palace has now issued a heavenly decree to execute you!”

“What!”

Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor was incomparably bewildered. When had he ever... “Your Excellencies, I really did not slaughter the Feng Family! Don’t kill me—extract my soul-origin memories and you’ll know I’m not lying!” Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor hurriedly said.

He felt that extracting his soul-origin memories could prove his innocence. That way, he would not have to die.

Although extracting his soul-origin memories again would worsen his soul defect, he anyway... could no longer advance to become a Pinnacle Dao Ancestor, so he did not care about that anymore.

However, Emperor Guangling sneered, “Stone Eagle, very impressive. I suspect you possess some rare method that can directly alter your soul-origin aura. Perhaps you really did refine the Forbidden Void Realm.

To tell you the truth, this time we used the Spacetime Emperor Mirror. You may not know much about it, but in short, once the Spacetime Emperor Mirror is used, as long as it detects you, even an Invincible Dao Ancestor cannot hide their identity.

The Spacetime Emperor Mirror detected that it was you who personally destroyed the Feng Family.

Enough. We have no time to listen to your explanations!”

Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor still wanted to explain something, but Emperor Guangling directly made his move.

Bang! Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor’s body exploded on the spot. At the ultimate level of a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, he had no chance whatsoever to resist and was directly suppressed and killed by Emperor Guangling.

After killing Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor, the Emperors departed one after another.

With Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor’s death, this matter came to an end, and the Heavenly Emperor Palace could be said to have given an explanation to the countless families under its command.

And the Heavenly Emperor Palace did not suspect Ye Tian in the slightest. After all, the ability of Copy Talent was far too terrifying. Even the Spacetime Emperor Mirror could not detect Ye Tian’s identity and could only determine from the copied body that this was Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor.

Human Race.

Ye Tian soon learned that Stone Eagle Dao Ancestor had been executed by the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

In response, he could only express regret.

In the days that followed, Ye Tian devoted himself wholeheartedly to cultivation and comprehending Dao arts, striving to cultivate each Great Thousand Dao Art to the limit as soon as possible.

As for breaking through to Pinnacle Dao Ancestor, he was not in a hurry.

He had mastered dark forbidden power and the forbidden body, and had also comprehended the Endless Forbidden Dao. For him, breaking through to become a Pinnacle Dao Ancestor was not difficult at all.

But he did not want to enter the Pinnacle Dao Ancestor level so hastily, because he still wanted to accumulate a bit more foundation.

At the Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor level, the stronger one’s power, the more one’s strength would surge by a huge margin once one broke through to the Pinnacle Dao Ancestor level.

Strictly speaking, the difference between a Pinnacle Dao Ancestor and a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor was not merely a difference in strength, but rather akin to two separate realms.

Once one broke through to Pinnacle Dao Ancestor, the Dao Ancestor body would transform into a Pinnacle Dao Body, and one would automatically comprehend a Supreme Great Dao. Yet what Ye Tian had comprehended was the Endless Forbidden Dao, which stood above the Supreme Great Dao.

Therefore, if he broke through to the Pinnacle Dao Ancestor level, his forbidden body would improve by a small margin, and the Endless Forbidden Dao would also instantly gain countless insights and improve by a small margin.

In addition, his Dao Ancestor body, forbidden dao power, and soul would all undergo transformation.

Thus, many Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors who clearly had a great chance of breaking through to become Supreme Dao Ancestors still delayed doing so, simply because... they wanted to accumulate a little more.

Ye Tian’s current battle power had reached the ultimate level of a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor, but that standard was the battle-power standard of the Mysterious Void Ancient Realm. It did not mean that he himself had reached the limit of a Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestor. He could still continue improving, so why rush to break through? While Ye Tian was in seclusion, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and Ye Yu also successively began to break through to the Dao Ancestor level, and each one succeeded, becoming Fifth Heaven Dao Ancestors.

At this point, the Human Race’s high-end strength had increased quite a bit.

In the days that followed, the Mysterious Void Ancient Realm once again successively gave birth to some forbidden treasure lands. On several occasions, Ye Tian did not participate, instead allowing some Human Race True Ancestors and Dao Ancestors to compete for them.

Perhaps because the major factions had established rules, the slaughter had decreased quite a bit. But every time a forbidden treasure land appeared, no matter how much restrictions were imposed, bloodshed still could not be completely forbidden.

On the surface, however, everyone had established one rule: Dao Ancestors were not allowed to attack True Ancestors unless that True Ancestor took the initiative to provoke a Dao Ancestor.

If there were no restrictions, and Dao Ancestors slaughtered large numbers of True Ancestors, then how could True Ancestors rise? How could they grow? In the blink of an eye, another tens of thousands of years passed.

On this day.

The Mysterious Void Ancient Realm had calmed down, but in the Dark Forbidden Domain not too far from the Mysterious Void Ancient Realm, a slight disturbance had appeared.
