Chapter 1188 The Forbidden Insect Race! Big Trouble! Part..

Chapter 1188: The Forbidden Insect Race

! Big Trouble! [Second Update]

The Dark Forbidden Region had always been extremely mysterious. True Ancestors did not dare step into it, and ordinary Dao Ancestors were also unwilling to enter the Dark Forbidden Region. On top of that, the current Profound Void Ancient Realm was filled with countless opportunities, so there were even fewer people willing to enter the Dark Forbidden Region.

But ever since the Heavenly Emperor Palace emerged, it had dispatched a group of Dao Ancestors and True Ancestors to station themselves along the edge of the Dark Forbidden Region. There, they forcibly opened up a small world, and with the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s foundation, accomplishing this was naturally not difficult.

The Dao Ancestor in charge of managing this small world was the Heavenly Emperor Palace’s strongest Dao Ancestor—Black Desolation Dao Ancestor.

On this day.

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor sensed that the power of dark forbidden near the Dark Forbidden Region was surging, far more violently than usual, and he was immediately filled with confusion.

“I’d better go take a look!”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor stepped out of the small world and began walking through the Dark Forbidden Region to investigate the situation.

This was the edge of the Dark Forbidden Region, not far from the boundary realm. The power of dark forbidden here was not terribly frightening, and there were not many dangers either. With his strength as a strongest Dao Ancestor, it was impossible for any major danger to arise here—unless he was truly unlucky enough to encounter a real forbidden creature.

Those forbidden creatures, the powerful ones, were comparable to half-step Realm Ancestors, while even the weaker ones could be called invincible Dao Ancestors. Only in that case would his life truly be in danger.

But real forbidden creatures were also extremely rare in the Dark Forbidden Region, so it was unlikely he would run into one.

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor flew for a long time, and finally047 found the source of the disturbance in the power of dark forbidden—“This is....”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor saw a... creature. It was not an illusion; with his strength as a strongest Dao Ancestor, if it were an illusion, he would have been able to detect some flaw.

However, the insect-like creature not far away was a real living being, not something illusory.

“Could this be a forbidden creature?”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor felt chilled all over, and his heart filled with terror.

After all, if he really had encountered a forbidden creature, he was probably doomed.

Forbidden creatures were not... forbidden bloodline creatures. True forbidden creatures were entirely composed of the power of dark forbidden, and within the Dark Forbidden Region they were born with mastery over the Forbidden Dao. Their strength was terrifying beyond measure.

For cultivators, the bodies of forbidden creatures were equivalent to perfect forbidden bodies. Not only were they immensely powerful, they were also extremely hard to kill.

Moreover, the speed of forbidden creatures was comparable to that of Realm Ancestors, making it impossible to evade their pursuit.

“No, that’s not right!”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor suddenly realized something was wrong.

This creature’s aura was still far inferior to his own, so it could not possibly be a forbidden creature.

Forbidden creatures did not cultivate. They were born powerful, and naturally they would not possess methods for concealing their aura, nor did they know how to hide their strength.

But the aura of the creature before him was only at a fairly ordinary Dao Ancestor level—far too weak. It was unlikely to be a forbidden creature.

However, this creature also did not seem much like a forbidden bloodline creature. Such bloodline creatures almost all lived in forbidden worlds, some forbidden small worlds, or certain forbidden lands. They were unlikely to appear in the Dark Forbidden Region.

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor did not dare attack. Even though the other party was weak, he still did not dare act. Instead, he returned to the small world and reported what he had discovered.

Not long after, an Emperor Lord arrived here.

“Greetings, Emperor Lord Nether River!”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor said respectfully.

Emperor Lord Nether River ranked among the top ten in combat power within the Heavenly Emperor Palace. He was even somewhat stronger than invincible Dao Ancestors such as Emperor Lord Guangling. He was a truly terrifying and incomparably ancient Emperor Lord, and legend had it that he had followed the ancient Vast Sea Realm Ancestor into battle.

Unfortunately, fate had not favored him, so he had never managed to break through to become a half-step Realm Ancestor. But there were also rumors that Emperor Lord Nether River could step into half-step Realm Ancestor combat power at any time.

“Black Desolation Dao Ancestor, recreate the appearance of that creature. Let me examine it carefully!”

Emperor Lord Nether River said.

“Yes!”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor recreated the appearance of that insect.

After looking at it, Emperor Lord Nether River frowned, his expression somewhat off.

“Emperor Lord Nether River, do you recognize this thing?”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor asked.

“I have a guess!”

Emperor Lord Nether River sighed. “I hope it isn’t true, otherwise there’ll be big trouble!”

Afterward, Emperor Lord Nether River brought Black Desolation Dao Ancestor to the place where the insect creature had first been discovered. But the insect was no longer there, so the two of them followed the area where the power of dark forbidden was in turmoil and continued investigating.

Soon, they discovered the insect creatures again, and there was not just one, but six or seven.

As they went deeper and deeper into the area where the power of dark forbidden was erupting, they found more and more insect creatures. However, because Emperor Lord Nether River’s concealment methods were quite brilliant, they were able to avoid detection by those insect creatures.

Suddenly.

A massive insect creature’s pair of pupils seemed to cross the forbidden void of darkness and lock onto Emperor Lord Nether River, launching a pupil technique through the air at him.

Emperor Lord Nether River also counterattacked, and the two pupil techniques collided in the forbidden void, yet neither gained the upper hand.

“Retreat!”

Emperor Lord Nether River, his expression grave, took Black Desolation Dao Ancestor and left the area. He also led the Dao Ancestors from the small world to withdraw from the Dark Forbidden Region, stationing themselves only in the boundary void outside the Dark Forbidden Region.

“Emperor Lord Nether River, could that just now have been a real forbidden creature?”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor asked in alarm.

It was no wonder he was alarmed. The strength of that massive insect was probably not the slightest bit weaker than Emperor Lord Nether River’s. It possessed invincible Dao Ancestor-level combat power. He was far from being its opponent.

Fortunately, he had not continued investigating back then. Otherwise, had he encountered that massive insect, he would probably have died for sure.

“It was not a forbidden creature!”

Emperor Lord Nether River said. “According to my speculation, that should be one of the forbidden races—the Forbidden Insect Race!”

“Forbidden race? Forbidden Insect Race?”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor had never heard of it, and so was utterly puzzled.

At this time, Emperor Lord Nether River explained, “Let me put it this way. A world will give birth to two types of living beings. One type is innate lifeforms, the innate gods and demons of a world.

The other type is ordinary acquired lifeforms. Although weak, their reproductive ability is incredibly strong, and their potential is very high—they may even surpass the innate gods and demons.

And the Dark Forbidden Region is the same. Forbidden creatures are equivalent to true forbidden innate gods and demons, while forbidden races are acquired lifeforms.

Under normal circumstances, the Dark Forbidden Region cannot give birth to acquired lifeforms. But if there appears a... forbidden race nest, then it can continuously produce forbidden races.”

“Among forbidden races, the most common is the Forbidden Insect Race. But the Forbidden Insect Race is an even greater threat than forbidden creatures, because forbidden creatures rarely enter the boundary realms. They do not like the environment of the boundary realms. But the Forbidden Insect Race is different—they devour everything. Once they find the Daoshan Boundary Realm, they will likely launch a massive invasion.

And they grow by devouring life. Once they find the Daoshan Boundary Realm, they will probably be able to grow rapidly within a short time.

Back in the Shentian Boundary Realm, the Realm Ancestor once mentioned the Forbidden Insect Race. He said that in the Dark Forbidden Region, they had found fragments drifting over from other boundary realms, and on them were traces of the Forbidden Insect Race as well as some records.

But never could I have imagined that a branch of the Forbidden Insect Race would also appear in the Dark Forbidden Region here in the Daoshan Boundary Realm. Fortunately, it was discovered early. Otherwise, if they had grown to a certain extent before invading the Daoshan Boundary Realm, we might not necessarily have been able to stop them!”

After Emperor Lord Nether River finished speaking, Black Desolation Dao Ancestor finally understood just how serious the matter was.

Chapter 1189: Joint Interception!

Chapter 1189: Joint Interception

!【Third Update】

“Black Desolation Dao Ancestor, continue standing guard here. I’ll return to the Heavenly Emperor Palace first and discuss this with the three Palace Masters!”

Minghe Imperial Lord said.

“Yes!”

Black Desolation Dao Ancestor responded.

....Heavenly Emperor Palace.

After Minghe Imperial Lord returned, he immediately went to find the Azure Dragon Palace Master, the White Tiger Palace Master, and the True Martial Palace Master.

Heavenly Emperor Palace, Heavenly Emperor Hall.

Minghe Imperial Lord met the three Palace Masters and said, “Three Palace Masters, I just went to investigate the situation near the Dark Forbidden Region and discovered the Forbidden Insect Race!”

“Are you certain it was the Forbidden Insect Race?”

Azure Dragon Palace Master frowned.

“Yes!”

Minghe Imperial Lord said with certainty, “I saw many members of the Forbidden Insect Race, and I also saw a commander-level Forbidden Insect! However, I didn’t dare search for the Forbidden Insect Race’s nest!”

“It was the right decision not to go looking. Otherwise, if you had encountered a lord-level Forbidden Insect, you wouldn’t have come back!”

Azure Dragon Palace Master said.

“What should we do now? Is our Heavenly Emperor Palace going to attack that Forbidden Insect Race nest?”

Minghe Imperial Lord asked.

“Of course not!”

True Martial Palace Master shook his head. “If our Heavenly Emperor Palace attacks the Forbidden Insect Race nest, we’ll likely suffer grievous losses. By then, if we fight ourselves to the bitter end, we’ll only be benefiting other forces.

Besides, the Forbidden Insect Race threatens the entire Daoshan Realm Domain. Why should our Heavenly Emperor Palace be the one to fight them? We established that minor world for the sake of projecting the coordinates of the Forbidden Realm in the future, not to guard against the Forbidden Insect Race.

How about this—we’ll invite the other forces to discuss it. Every force must send a certain number of people to wage war against the Forbidden Insect Race at the edge of the Dark Forbidden Region.

That way, if there are losses, everyone shares them.”

The previously silent White Tiger Palace Master suddenly spoke. “Actually, the appearance of the Forbidden Insect Race is a good thing for the Xuanxu Ancient Realm!”

“A good thing? How is this a good thing?”

True Martial Palace Master asked in confusion.

White Tiger Palace Master explained, “Don’t forget, the Forbidden Insect Race can also be considered pseudo-forbidden lifeforms. This kind of lifeform is of great benefit to the birth of a Forbidden Realm. If we sacrifice a large number of Forbidden Insects, we can definitely accelerate the birth of the Forbidden Realm, and the success rate will certainly be much higher. That is far more worthwhile than killing some Dao Ancestors.

Killing Dao Ancestors would provoke resistance from other forces, making it not worth the cost.

But killing the Forbidden Insect Race—with other forces helping us kill them at that—can be said to kill two birds with one stone!”

Upon hearing this, Azure Dragon Palace Master and True Martial Palace Master immediately felt that this suggestion was excellent.

The ultimate goal of Heavenly Emperor Palace was to turn the Xuanxu Ancient Realm into a Forbidden Realm. Although the success rate was already very high, the time required was far too long. If they could sacrifice a large number of Forbidden Insects, they could increase the success rate and also shorten the time needed.

Moreover, by sacrificing the Forbidden Insect Race to the origin of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm, they could also obtain benefits from the Xuanxu Ancient Realm itself, such as gaining a portion of Xuanxu origin power to increase their strength, receiving cultivation boosts, and so on....

In short, the benefits were many! “If we’re going to sacrifice the Forbidden Insect Race, then our Heavenly Emperor Palace really should put in some serious effort this time!”

Azure Dragon Palace Master said with a smile.

White Tiger Palace Master and True Martial Palace Master also nodded in agreement.

Human race.

Chapter 1191: The Base in the Dark Forbidden Domain

!【Fifth Update】

The Forbidden Insect Nest was the true foundation of the Forbidden Insects. No matter how many Forbidden Insects were killed, the impact on them was not all that great; it merely limited their development.

But once the Forbidden Insect Nest was destroyed, the Forbidden Insects would no longer be able to continue breeding new Forbidden Insects, and their extinction would not be far off.

After all, the Forbidden Insects could only rely on the Forbidden Insect Nest to produce their kin; they had no way to reproduce through mating.

“Eternal Dao Ancestor, is there no way for us to destroy the Forbidden Insect Nest?”

If that happens, it can be considered a solution to the Forbidden Insect problem.”

So I do not recommend that weak Dao Ancestors go onto the battlefield to fight!”

In just ten short years, a large number of bases had been established in the edge region of the Dark Forbidden Domain, and a great many Dao Ancestors had set up countless grand formations in the Dao Mountain Realm’s void outside the edge of the Dark Forbidden Domain to prevent any Forbidden Insects from breaking out of the encirclement and entering the Dao Mountain Realm.

At the same time.

On this day.

After all, lord-level Forbidden Insectoids also needed to increase their strength, and they did not cultivate—they simply... devoured resources to strengthen themselves.

Moreover, lord-level Forbidden Insectoids also had to gather vast amounts of resources to supply the Forbidden Insectoid nest so that more Forbidden Insectoids could be bred, so their responsibilities were also heavy.

Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor’s goal was very simple: to lure away the two guarding lord-level Forbidden Insectoids, and then take the opportunity to let the Nine Extremes Heavenly King enter the interior of the Forbidden Insectoid nest.

With the Nine Extremes Heavenly King’s strength, even if he encountered elite-level Forbidden Insectoids, he would not be killed immediately. Only if he ran into commander-level Forbidden Insectoids would he be killed within a few moves.

Even so, the Nine Extremes Heavenly King would still be able to pry out at least some intelligence.

Along the way.

Ye Tian saw a great many Forbidden Insectoids. It seemed the Forbidden Insectoid race also knew that the Dao Ancestors of the Daoshan Realm Domain had come to kill them, and so they were gathering their insect army in preparation to wage war against the Dao Ancestors.

Although Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor could easily kill these Forbidden Insectoids, they did not make a move. Otherwise, if they attracted lord-level Forbidden Insectoids, this plan would fail.

The two half-step Domain Ancestors moved at incredible speed, and Ye Tian was carried along by the two of them the entire way as they traversed through space.

About an hour later, they finally arrived at the Forbidden Insectoid nest.

“What a huge nest!”

Ye Tian marveled inwardly.

This was a spherical nest, with passageways connecting to its interior. At this moment, Forbidden Insectoids could be seen entering and leaving through these passageways one after another; all of these passages were both entrances and exits.

By Ye Tian’s estimate, this nest was at least as large as the human territory. One could imagine just how vast that was—comparable to the size of an entire Dao Realm! Outside the nest, two Forbidden Insectoids emitting a golden luster were crouched there. The aura they gave off far surpassed that of the other Forbidden Insectoids, and even from far away, they exerted tremendous pressure on Ye Tian.

Forbidden Insectoids did not know how to restrain their auras, so these two lord-level Forbidden Insectoids, comparable to half-step Domain Ancestors, were fully releasing the pressure of half-step Domain Ancestors. One could imagine how terrifying that was! If Ye Tian got close to those two lord-level Forbidden Insectoids, he probably wouldn’t even need to reach them before being suppressed by their pressure to the point of being unable to move.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly King, we’ll draw away those two lord-level Forbidden Insectoids. You take the chance to find a passage and charge into the Forbidden Insectoid nest. Remember, we can only buy you ten minutes. After ten minutes, regardless of whether you have… fallen or not, we will leave!”

Eternal Dao Ancestor said.

This passage then!”

Chapter 1193 Forbidden Talent: Dark Spear! Pt..

Chapter 1193: Forbidden Talent

: Dark Spear! 【Second update, please subscribe in full】

The passage into the Forbidden Insectoid nest was not very long. Before long, Ye Tian passed through it and arrived in the inner space of the Forbidden Insectoid nest.

The interior of the insectoid nest was enormous—so vast that the end could not be seen at a glance. Even Ye Tian’s divine sense could not reach the core area; he could only see some Forbidden Insectoids moving about nearby.

Moreover, the suppression here was extremely strong. At most, he could only bring out thirty percent of his strength.

Even a half-step Domain Ancestor would likely have a large portion of their power suppressed upon coming here. At that point, probably any... Lord-class Forbidden Insectoid would have the strength to kill a half-step Domain Ancestor.

“I have to get close to the core area before I can investigate the specific situation!”

Ye Tian thought to himself.

So he used the Heavenly Illusion Divine Step and flew toward the central region of the Forbidden Insectoid nest at top speed.

Along the way, one Forbidden Insectoid after another surrounded and attacked Ye Tian, but he ignored them completely, allowing them to strike him as they pleased.

He even unleashed the ultimate potential of this body, moving at a speed beyond its limits.

At last, with a heavily injured body, he arrived at the central region.

At that moment, his gaze focused on the gigantic divine tree inside the nest. Countless insect cocoons hung from the tree, each one representing a Forbidden Insectoid.

Ye Tian’s divine sense spotted the three most important cocoons—cocoons filled with golden radiance. They were clearly the cocoons of Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids. If these three cocoons were allowed to hatch, the Forbidden Insectoids would once again give birth to three more Lord-class insectoids.

But what made Ye Tian’s expression change drastically the most was that at the very top of the insectoid divine tree was a pure violet flower, and on that flower was a pure violet bud. It looked very much like a cocoon, though somewhat smaller.

Clearly, this pure violet bud was also a cocoon, and judging from its position, it should be an incomparably important one.

Ye Tian could clearly see two golden Forbidden Insectoids crouching on either side of the pure violet flower, apparently guarding that pure violet cocoon.

Those two golden Forbidden Insectoids were clearly Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids, comparable to half-step Domain Ancestors! “Could that be a King Insect cocoon?”

Ye Tian guessed.

If that were truly the case, then it was definitely not good news.

Although he did not know when that King Insect cocoon would hatch, once it did, it would absolutely be a disaster for the Daoshan Realm Domain.

Suddenly.

Those two Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids awakened and locked their eyes onto Ye Tian.

One of the Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids stretched out a long leg like a spear, instantly piercing through space and directly crossing the void to kill Ye Tian in a second, then went back to sleep.

It seemed that to them, only a tiny bug had entered, and crushing it to death was enough.

Somewhere in the Dark Forbidden Region.

Ye Tian was hunting Forbidden Insectoids together with Xiao Yue when his expression suddenly shifted, and he realized that his copied body had fallen.

The ability of his Copy Talent was extremely miraculous. Even the Forbidden Insectoid nest could not sever the connection between his true body and his copied body, so he knew very clearly everything that the copied body had experienced.

“As expected of a Lord-class Forbidden Insect.

With just one long leg, it killed me instantly with ease!”

Ye Tian muttered inwardly.

However, he soon became excited.

Previously, he had approached the Forbidden Insectoid nest together with Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor, but because they were wary of those two Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids, Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor had not allowed his copied body to get close to them.

Because the distance had been too great, his Copy Talent had been unable to cover the bodies of those two Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids, so he had been unable to see their talents.

But this time, the two Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids inside the Forbidden Insectoid nest had been relatively close to Ye Tian, so he had successfully probed their talent information.

Ordinary Forbidden Insectoids had no special talents, only Speed Talent, Defense Talent, and Strength Talent. They did not even have cultivation talent.

The strength of many Forbidden Insectoids was fixed the moment they were born, and it was very difficult for them to grow stronger. No matter how many resources they devoured, they could only rise to their current limit at most.

Therefore, Ye Tian had not copied any good talents from the other Forbidden Insectoids.

But this time was different. On the Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids, he actually saw a brand-new kind of talent.

【Forbidden Talent: Dark Spear】 Ye Tian had never seen any Forbidden Talent before, but from the description, he came to understand its general nature.

It was a type of talent that stood above Dao-level innate talents. Basically, every Forbidden creature possessed a Forbidden Talent.

But true Forbidden creatures were all existences comparable to Domain Ancestors, and Ye Tian had no chance to encounter such Forbidden creatures.

Yet Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids also possessed Forbidden Talents, though they had only a single Forbidden Talent.

The Forbidden Talents of those two Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids were both Dark Spear. Clearly, this was their racial Forbidden Talent.

Ye Tian immediately copied the Forbidden Talent of those two Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids. Once they were fused, his Forbidden Talent would become somewhat stronger than that of the Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids.

“If I could copy the Forbidden Talents of all the Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids, then I could possess an even more powerful Forbidden Talent: Dark Spear. It’s just a pity that next time, trying to come into contact with Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids will be incredibly, incredibly difficult!”

Ye Tian said regretfully.

He was still far too weak. Without Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor bringing him along, there was simply no way for him to get close to the Forbidden Insectoid nest. He would have been killed on the way by those Elite-class Forbidden Insectoids and Commander-class Forbidden Insectoids long ago.

What Ye Tian regretted even more was that he had not managed to probe the talent of the Insect King inside that pure violet cocoon. It was probably because it had not yet fully formed, so its talent information could not be seen.

Otherwise, the Forbidden Talent of an Insect King would definitely be even more powerful.

After Ye Tian and Xiao Yue killed three Forbidden Insectoids, they did not continue hunting, but quickly left that area and returned to the Black Wind Mountain base.

If they got greedy and kept killing, once they were surrounded by a large number of Forbidden Insectoids, even Ye Tian would not find it easy to break out. If they encountered Elite-class Forbidden Insectoids, the two of them would be in mortal danger.

So, it was best to stop while ahead! After returning to the Black Wind Mountain base, Xiao Yue rested for a while, while Ye Tian was soon summoned by Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor. Clearly, the two half-step Domain Ancestors had also returned.

Eternal Dao Ancestor’s residence.

Ye Tian once again saw the two half-step Domain Ancestors. “Greetings, Eternal Dao Ancestor. Greetings, Shenxu Dao Ancestor!”

Eternal Dao Ancestor asked, “Nine Extremes Heavenly King, your avatar entered the Forbidden Insectoid nest. Did you discover anything?”

Ye Tian answered truthfully, “I have basically investigated the situation. In the central region inside the Forbidden Insectoid nest, there is an incomparably massive divine tree. I call it the Forbidden Insect Tree. On the Forbidden Insect Tree are countless Forbidden Insectoid cocoons, and every Forbidden Insectoid is birthed from those Forbidden cocoons! Moreover, I also saw two living Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids, as well as three Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids currently in the process of gestation!”

Eternal Dao Ancestor and Shenxu Dao Ancestor both showed slight changes in expression upon hearing this.

If that was the case, then the Forbidden Insectoids possessed a total of eight Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids. If those three Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids were born, then the number of Lord-class Forbidden Insectoids among the Forbidden Insectoids would reach eleven.

But next, Ye Tian’s words made their expressions change drastically.

Chapter 1194 Reporting the Situation, Insect King!

Chapter 1194: Reporting the Situation, Insect King

!【Third Update】

“I also saw a pure purple cocoon on the forbidden insect tree inside the forbidden insect race’s nest. Those two lord-level forbidden insects were guarding that pure purple cocoon.

That pure purple cocoon was located at the very top of the insect tree. I suspect that it may be the Insect King’s cocoon!”

Ye Tian voiced his speculation.

“What, the Insect King!!!!”

Eternal Dao Ancestor and Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor were both greatly alarmed.

The Insect King was an existence comparable to a Domain Ancestor. Once the Insect King was born, even if the two of them joined forces, they would not be able to withstand a single move and would be killed instantly.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly King, are you certain?”

Eternal Dao Ancestor asked solemnly.

“Certain!”

Ye Tian said firmly.

Eternal Dao Ancestor and Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor fell silent. This news was deeply shocking to them and left them extremely stunned.

At present, the only good news was that the Insect King’s cocoon was still in the process of incubation. As long as they slaughtered the forbidden insects on a large scale and did not give them time to search for resources, the forbidden insect race’s breeding progress would be interrupted, and it would become... a mere luxury for that Insect King to be born.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly King, at regular intervals, we will have your avatar enter the interior of the forbidden insect race’s nest to investigate the incubation status of the Insect King’s cocoon. Can you agree to this?”

Eternal Dao Ancestor asked.

“No problem!”

Ye Tian agreed without hesitation.

He just so happened to want to copy the forbidden talents of other lord-level forbidden insects. If he could encounter other lord-level forbidden insects, then he would really strike it rich.

Therefore, he would naturally agree to such a request.

Having learned the forbidden insect race’s combat strength, Eternal Dao Ancestor and Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor now had a rough understanding of it. At the very least, they would not fall into a desperate situation in the future due to insufficient intelligence.

Under the current circumstances, the forbidden insect race possessed eight lord-level forbidden insects. Of them, two needed to guard the Insect King’s cocoon and generally would not come out to fight unless the half-step Domain Ancestors were truly on the verge of breaking into the forbidden insect nest.

In addition, the interior of the forbidden insect nest greatly suppressed outsiders. One could not enter lightly, otherwise it would be very easy to lose one’s life. That was the forbidden insect race’s home ground, and they held an enormous advantage fighting there.

Moreover, Ye Tian had only scouted as far as the forbidden insect tree and had not fully investigated all the circumstances inside the forbidden insect race’s nest. Therefore, the current information was only partial. It could be trusted, but not completely trusted.

So, Black Wind Mountain still needed to proceed with caution.

After Ye Tian came out of Eternal Dao Ancestor’s residence, he did not rest after returning, nor did he go cultivate. Instead, he began fusing two forbidden talents: Dark Spear.

“Fuse!”

Ye Tian willed inwardly.

Boom!!!! Terrifying pain surged over him, making him feel as if he had returned to the time when he first fused talents, though it was still something he could endure.

This fusion took quite a long time. A full day passed before the fusion was finally completed.

After that, Ye Tian fused the second Dark Spear as well, which likewise took a whole day.

However, to fuse the two forbidden talents into one forbidden talent took dozens of years, and all of this was carried out inside the time array, so not much time passed in the outside world.

This forbidden talent, Dark Spear, was not like Ye Tian’s previous understanding of it as merely condensing a single dark spear. Rather, it was an indestructible property that could be applied both to a forbidden spear and to one’s own body.

For example, that lord-level forbidden insect had applied the Dark Spear forbidden talent to its long legs, making the attacking power and might of those legs become unimaginably terrifying. They could easily pierce through his body; even a half-step Domain Ancestor probably would not dare receive a blow from Dark Spear head-on.

Ye Tian tried applying the Dark Spear forbidden talent to a forbidden spear, instantly increasing the forbidden spear’s power by tenfold. This meant that Ye Tian’s combat strength had risen dramatically in an instant.

Afterward, he applied the forbidden spear to his own finger, and with a single finger he could easily pierce through a Dao artifact.

Unfortunately, the forbidden spear represented offense, so it could not be applied to his body to form a defense.

Of course, using a talent directly was the stupidest and also the least efficient method.

For example, with Dao-level innate talents, if used directly, their power was not very great. Dao-level innate talents mainly allowed cultivators to quickly comprehend Dao techniques.

And forbidden talents—“What forbidden talents correspond to should be forbidden Dao techniques!”

Ye Tian murmured.

Forbidden Dao techniques had to be comprehended by oneself. Other people’s forbidden Dao techniques were unsuitable for oneself, and anyone qualified to cultivate forbidden Dao techniques would not possibly go learn someone else’s forbidden Dao techniques, because that would ruin their own forbidden Dao.

Therefore, the path after the Pinnacle Dao Ancestor stage almost entirely depended on personal comprehension and could not be taught. That was also why Invincible Dao Ancestors and half-step Domain Ancestors were so rare.

Although Ye Tian now possessed a forbidden talent, making his hope of creating a forbidden Dao technique many times greater than before, it was still not something he could create just by casually thinking about it. It would still require a very long time.

However, with the forbidden talent Dark Spear, Ye Tian’s current combat strength had skyrocketed and was enough to rival the weakest kind of... Pinnacle Dao Ancestor. If he encountered an elite-level forbidden insect, it was not as though he had no power to resist.

0Ye Tian and Xiao Yue rested at the Black Wind Mountain base for several months, and also learned more about the current situation on the battlefield.

At present, the battlefield was basically divided into the first-tier battlefield of Invincible Dao Ancestors, the second-tier battlefield of Pinnacle Dao Ancestors, and the lower third-tier battlefield.

The third-tier battlefield was relatively close to the major bases, and elite-level forbidden insects were extremely rare there. After all, elite-level forbidden insects were basically all held back by the Supreme Dao Ancestors, in order to prevent the elite-level insects from slaughtering ordinary Dao Ancestors on a massive scale.

Once too many Dao Ancestors fell, the forbidden insect race could carry off their bodies back to the forbidden insect race’s nest and cultivate even more forbidden insects. That was definitely not a good thing.

On this day.

Ye Tian received an order from Black Wind Mountain.

“Nine Extremes Heavenly King, immediately head to the third-tier battlefield and intercept a batch of forbidden insects!”

This was an order from Wind King.

According to Wind King, a team of more than three hundred Dao Ancestors had been slaughtered, and that batch of forbidden insects was taking the bodies of those three hundred Dao Ancestors back to the forbidden insect race’s nest. Therefore, they had to be intercepted on the third-tier battlefield.

Otherwise, if that group of forbidden insects escaped, they would definitely use those Dao Ancestor bodies to cultivate a large number of forbidden insects.

Of course.

Ye Tian was not the only one to receive this order. The Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors on the third-tier battlefield also received the message one after another, and they were all the top Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors. Ordinary Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors were not qualified to accept this mission; otherwise, going there would only be delivering corpses.

Chapter 1195: Intercepting the Forbidden Insect Race!

Chapter 1195: Intercepting the Forbidden Insect Race

!【Fourth Update】

In the Dark Forbidden Zone, on the Level 3 battlefield.

A group of roughly sixty to seventy Forbidden Insects was rapidly darting through space. They were heading straight toward the Forbidden Insect Nest in a direct line, so it was not difficult to determine their route.

This batch of Forbidden Insects was basically comparable to Sixth-Heaven Dao Ancestors, with a few on the level of Fifth-Heaven Dao Ancestors, while the leading few possessed the strength of Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors.

In the Dark Forbidden Zone, if one had not mastered a forbidden body, then an ordinary Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor would not even be able to do anything to a top-tier Sixth-Heaven Forbidden Insect. This was also the sorrow of the Dao Ancestors, since this place simply was not suited for their combat.

But they also did not dare allow the Forbidden Insects into the Daoshan Realm. Once they got in, driving them out would become difficult.

So even if this place was not suitable for Dao Ancestors to fight in, they still had to fight here.

Those few Seventh-Heaven Forbidden Insects posed the greatest threat, and only the most top-tier Seventh-Heaven “Zero Four Seven”

Dao Ancestors could contend with them. Otherwise, there was simply no way to withstand being besieged by them.

Qinghe Dao Ancestor of Mitian Sect happened to be not far from that batch of Forbidden Insects, and so he rushed over immediately.

Qinghe Dao Ancestor was not as powerful as Sky Claw Dao Ancestor, but among Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors he was still considered one of the very top, far surpassing ordinary Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors. Therefore, he had the strength to delay that batch of Forbidden Insects for a while.

As for killing them, there was no way he could do it alone.

....“Finally intercepted them!”

Qinghe Dao Ancestor appeared in front of the batch of Forbidden Insects, his expression extremely grave.

After all, the pressure on him was immense. He had to hold back so many Forbidden Insects by himself; one careless mistake and he could die here! But there was no helping it. It was an order from above, and he had to obey. If everyone feared death, then the growth of the Forbidden Insect Race could not be contained, and one day they would destroy the Daoshan Realm.

Therefore, Dao Ancestors who... feared death or disobeyed orders would definitely be severely punished by those above.

Boom!!! Qinghe Dao Ancestor began fighting this swarm of Forbidden Insects, and from the very start he was in a suppressed position.

There was no helping it. The Forbidden Insects had mastered forbidden bodies, and very advanced ones at that—one could even describe them as perfect forbidden bodies. Ordinary attacks found it difficult to injure them, and this was also their home ground.

It was already difficult enough to kill a single Forbidden Insect, let alone for Qinghe Dao Ancestor to face the siege of so many of them.

As time passed, Qinghe Dao Ancestor began suffering serious injuries, and all he had managed to kill were a few weaker Fifth-Heaven Forbidden Insects.

After a while... another Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor arrived.

“It’s Mad Shark Dao Ancestor!”

Qinghe Dao Ancestor was overjoyed.

Mad Shark Dao Ancestor was only a Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor from a Seventh-Heaven force—the Sand Sea Sect—but his strength was not weak either, only slightly inferior to Qinghe Dao Ancestor. Now that Mad Shark Dao Ancestor had come to support him, the pressure on him immediately lessened a great deal.

“Qinghe Dao Ancestor, I’ll help you!”

Mad Shark Dao Ancestor shot over and joined the battle, greatly easing the pressure on Qinghe Dao Ancestor.

However, their mission was to kill this batch of Forbidden Insects, and the power of just the two of them was nowhere near enough. They still needed more reinforcements.

Unfortunately, there were too few Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors who could come to assist.

Because there were too many Forbidden Insects, while the number of Dao Ancestors actually participating in the battle was not very large. Many Dao Ancestors had to face the threat of several or even many Forbidden Insects, and in addition, they also needed time to rest and heal.

Therefore, under such circumstances, every Dao Ancestor had their own duty or task. On top of that, weaker Dao Ancestors would be useless even if they came, so there were truly not many Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors able to provide support.

After all, if all the top Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors from other places were redeployed here one by one, then what would happen to the fighting elsewhere? If this had happened in the Shentian Realm, there would have been no need to worry at all—a few Realm Ancestors sent out by the Shentian Realm could easily sweep away the Forbidden Insect Race.

But this was the Daoshan Realm, whose strength was insufficient. That was simply a helpless reality.

On top of that, the various major forces could not possibly commit all of their strength either. If the losses became too severe, they would not be able to bear them.

Therefore, even after Qinghe Dao Ancestor and Mad Shark Dao Ancestor had fought for quite a long time, only then did the third Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor arrive.

This was a female Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, Yinyi Dao Ancestor from the Eighth-Heaven force Hundred Flowers Palace. Her strength was about the same as Qinghe Dao Ancestor’s, but she had come while injured, because not long before this she had been fighting another Forbidden Insect. Although she had killed it, she had suffered some injuries herself.

Even so, she was still able to bring out more than ninety percent of her combat strength.

The three great Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors fought this batch of Forbidden Insects and gained a decisive advantage. One weaker Forbidden Insect after another was slain.

At this rate, the final result would probably be the total annihilation of the Forbidden Insects, with the three of them heavily injured... The wish was beautiful, but reality was cruel.

“This is bad!”

Qinghe Dao Ancestor’s expression changed drastically.

“What is it?”

Yinyi Dao Ancestor and Mad Shark Dao Ancestor asked.

“Sense over there—another batch of Forbidden Insects is coming. They seem to be reinforcements for this batch!”

Qinghe Dao Ancestor said with utmost seriousness.

Yinyi Dao Ancestor and Mad Shark Dao Ancestor extended their senses toward the distant void of the Dark Forbidden Zone, and sure enough, they detected surging dark forbidden power over there. It was obvious that quite a few beings were traversing over, and in this region, the creatures capable of producing such a disturbance could not possibly be Dao Ancestors from the Daoshan Realm. They had to be Forbidden Insects.

“No idea how many... Forbidden Insects there are. If the number is large...”

Qinghe Dao Ancestor and the other two were extremely worried.

If things went badly, all three of them might die here.

Very soon, that batch of Forbidden Insects appeared.

“Sixty-three Forbidden Insects!”

The expressions of Qinghe Dao Ancestor and the other two changed drastically. More importantly, among those sixty-three Forbidden Insects were six on the level of Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors. For the three of them, this was absolutely a catastrophic disaster.

“Prepare to run!”

Qinghe Dao Ancestor shouted.

Faced with danger they could not withstand, risking their lives would be useless. It would only deliver... the corpses of three Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors to the Forbidden Insects.

Therefore, under such circumstances, even if they fled, those Invincible Dao Ancestors would not punish them.

However, these Forbidden Insects seemed unwilling to let them go.

As soon as they fled, the Forbidden Insects 2.

2 began pursuing them, slowing their speed to: an extreme degree, and very soon the second batch of Forbidden Insects caught up with them.

The two batches of Forbidden Insects joined forces, and their threat level instantly rose by several grades.

They could no longer hold out! Just then, a figure streaked over at incredible speed and quickly entered the range of their divine sense.

“It’s Wanfa Dao Ancestor, but even if he’s come, it won’t be of much use!”

Qinghe Dao Ancestor said in despair.

At that moment, Yinyi Dao Ancestor said joyfully, “No, Wanfa Dao Ancestor is very strong. The pinnacle Dao Ancestor of our sect once said that among Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors, the most terrifying now should be Wanfa Dao Ancestor and the Nine Extremes Heavenly King! Their strength has risen far too quickly—they’re probably no weaker than Sky Claw Dao Ancestor and the others!”

Hearing Yinyi Dao Ancestor say this, Qinghe Dao Ancestor and Mad Shark Dao Ancestor felt a trace of hope arise in their hearts.

Chapter 1196: Interception, Slay Them All!

Chapter 1196: Interception, Slay Them All!

【Fifth Update】

“So many forbidden insectoids!”

Ye Tian was shocked as well.

The intelligence from before had said there were nowhere near this many forbidden insectoids! The report had stated there were only sixty or seventy, but here there were well over a hundred forbidden insectoids, and quite a few of them were even Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids.

At this moment, Ye Tian also noticed Dao Ancestor Qinghe and the others. Seeing that they were in grave danger, he immediately flew over at top speed.

In the blink of an eye, Ye Tian arrived beside Dao Ancestor Qinghe and the others.

Boom!!! His forbidden domain spread out, completely suppressing those forbidden insectoids.

Immediately after, Ye Tian condensed a forbidden spear and empowered it with the forbidden talent: Dark Spear! Pfft! The forbidden spear instantly pierced through the body of a... Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoid. Its remaining force did not diminish, and it went on to pierce through the bodies of several Sixth-Heaven forbidden insectoids as well.

Those few Sixth-Heaven forbidden insectoids were directly killed in an instant by the forbidden spear, while that Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoid, though not dead, was gravely wounded and on the brink of death, with barely any power left to resist.

At this moment.

Dao Ancestor Qinghe, Dao Ancestor Silver Robe, and Dao Ancestor Mad Shark were all stunned silly. Instantly killing Sixth-Heaven forbidden insectoids in one strike was certainly shocking, but not too outrageous. But severely wounding and nearly killing a21 Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoid in a single strike—that was far too absurd.

The few of them had battled those Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids for so long and had barely inflicted any... injuries on them. In terms of survival ability, a Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoid was even harder to kill than they were.

Yet Ye Tian had nearly killed one with a single strike. That meant Ye Tian could also heavily injure or even kill them in one blow! “Even Dao Ancestor Skyclaw couldn’t heavily wound me in one strike!”

the three of Dao Ancestor Qinghe murmured inwardly.

Didn’t that mean Ye Tian’s combat power had already surpassed Dao Ancestor Skyclaw’s—and not by a little, but by a great deal?

Dao Ancestor Skyclaw and the others had already reached the ultimate level among Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors. Only Young Master Gui could suppress Dao Ancestor Skyclaw and the others, yet even Young Master Gui might not possess the power to heavily wound or kill them in a single blow.

Terrifying indeed! That was their evaluation of Ye Tian! After gravely wounding that Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoid with one strike, Ye Tian thrust out another spear and directly killed it.

At this time, the other forbidden insectoids seemed to realize how terrifying Ye Tian was, but they did not flee. Instead, they all charged over to besiege him together.

In their consciousness, the word fear did not exist.

Ye Tian used the Ten Directions Void-Fixing Art to seal the void, then activated the Primordial Desolate Body to amplify his combat strength.

“Primordial Severing Strike!”

This strike directly split open the body of a... Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoid, and then he used the forbidden spear empowered with the forbidden talent Dark Spear to kill it in one blow.

Just like that.

Ye Tian unleashed one Dao art after another, slaughtering one... insectoid after another. In no time at all, this stretch of dark forbidden void was littered with the corpses of forbidden insectoids.

Dao Ancestor Qinghe, Dao Ancestor Silver Robe, and Dao Ancestor Mad Shark simply stood there watching, with no need to go up and help at all.

Before long, only seven or eight of this group of forbidden insectoids remained, including three Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids.

Only then did they feel fear and begin to flee.

However, escape was impossible for them. Ye Tian was much faster than they were, and he also possessed a tracking-type Great Thousand Dao Art—the Three-Fruit Heavenly Eye Art—which allowed him to easily lock onto their positions. On top of that, they had no idea how to conceal themselves, so even if they fled far away, Ye Tian would still catch up to them and kill them one by one.

Before long, these last few forbidden insectoids were also all slain by Ye Tian one after another.

“Many thanks to Dao Ancestor Wanfa for saving our lives!”

Dao Ancestor Qinghe, Dao Ancestor Silver Robe, and Dao Ancestor Mad Shark said gratefully when they saw Ye Tian return after killing off all the forbidden insectoids.

“You also made a great contribution. If you hadn’t held this group of forbidden insectoids back, I wouldn’t have been able to kill them either!”

Ye Tian said with a smile, “Let’s take the corpses of those fallen Dao Ancestors out from the internal spaces of the forbidden insectoids!”

“Mm!”

The three of Dao Ancestor Qinghe nodded.

After some sorting, one Dao Ancestor corpse after another was removed from the internal spaces of the forbidden insectoids. These Dao Ancestor corpses had to be taken back for burial or cremation and could not be left for the forbidden insectoids.

“You can take the insectoid corpses you killed next; those will belong to you. I’ll take the rest. No problem with that, right?”

Ye Tian asked.

“No problem!”

The three of Dao Ancestor Qinghe agreed.

Whoever killed a forbidden insectoid got to keep it—this was the rule among the major factions, so naturally they would not object.

Besides, they and Ye Tian were not Dao Ancestors from the same faction. There was no reason for him to deliberately take care of them.

If not for the fact that all the major factions had joined forces this time, under normal circumstances, they might even have been enemies! Thus,

Ye Tian took away the forbidden insectoid corpses he had killed, while he and the three of Dao Ancestor Qinghe returned to their respective bases.

As for the Dao Ancestor corpses, Ye Tian brought them back to the base for processing.

Blackwind Mountain Base.

After Ye Tian returned and handed in the mission, Wind King returned the Dao Ancestor corpses to their respective factions. As for a few unaffiliated cultivators’ corpses, they were taken back to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm to be destroyed.

In the days that followed, Ye Tian occasionally went out to hunt forbidden insectoids and occasionally went to support other Dao Ancestors.

Before he knew it, a hundred years had passed, and he had accumulated nearly a hundred forbidden insectoid corpses.

On this day.

Ye Tian applied to return to the Xuanxu Ancient Realm to rest and recuperate for a period of time, and at the same time to offer those forbidden insect047oid corpses as sacrifices.

Very soon, the application was approved.

....Xuanxu Ancient Realm.

Ye Tian and Xiao Yue had returned, while their son Ye Xingchen and the others were still continuing the fight and had not come back with them.

As soon as he returned to the human race, Ye Tian and his wife Xiao Yue began sacrificing those forbidden insectoid corpses.

On the sacrificial grand array.

One forbidden insectoid corpse after another was placed on it, and as the array operated, those forbidden insectoid corpses were sacrificed away.

The next moment.

Ye Tian sensed the existence of the origin of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm. It granted him cultivation enhancement, and a large amount of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm’s origin surged into his body, tempering his fleshly body, forbidden Dao power, and soul.

Ye Tian preserved this origin power, waiting to slowly refine it in the future.

Once he refined all of this origin power, his strength would still improve to a certain extent.

More importantly, under the augmentation of the Xuanxu Ancient Realm’s origin, if he cultivated in the Xuanxu Ancient Realm in the future, his cultivation speed would far surpass what it had been before. That was the truly great benefit.

Afterward, Ye Tian entered the Forbidden Void Realm to cultivate for a period of time, then left the Xuanxu Ancient Realm and once again entered the Dark Forbidden Region to hunt forbidden insectoids.

In this way, coming and going, Ye Tian’s strength and fame continued to grow.

On this day.

Chapter 1197: Total War!

Chapter 1197: Total War

!【First Update】

“An Invincible Dao Ancestor has fallen.”

When Ye Tian heard this news, he simply couldn’t believe it! That was an Invincible Dao Ancestor, a being above the Pinnacle Dao Ancestors and second only to Half-Step Domain Ancestors. How could such an existence fall so easily? Unless one encountered a lord-level Forbidden Insect, an Invincible Dao Ancestor was not likely to perish.

And lord-level Forbidden Insects never concealed their aura. Once one appeared, the Half-Step Domain Ancestors would definitely move to stop it, so how could an Invincible Dao Ancestor have fallen? Very soon, Ye Tian received the detailed news.

The fallen Invincible Dao Ancestor was one from the Hall of Myriad Domains—Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor. Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor had been besieged by ten commander-level Forbidden Insects and trapped within an initial realm, unable to escape. Before the Half-Step Domain Ancestors could come to his aid, he was forcibly killed.

Logically speaking, even if Invincible Dao Ancestor Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor were besieged by ten commander-level Forbidden Insects, he should not have fallen so quickly. He should have been able to hold out until the Half-Step Domain Ancestors arrived! But afterward, based on the deductions of the various Half-Step Domain Ancestors, Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor was likely killed by an extraordinarily powerful commander-level insect. Its strength surpassed that of ordinary commander-level Forbidden Insects, and it also possessed a certain degree of intelligence. That was how it managed to engineer the encirclement of Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor and kill him in one stroke.

Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor had been killed, and his corpse had already been taken away. The Half-Step Domain Ancestors had not managed to recover the body in time.

One could well imagine that once Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor’s corpse was delivered to the Forbidden Insect nest, it would very likely facilitate the birth of a... lord-level Forbidden Insect. If that happened, the pressure on the Daoshan Realm would become even greater.

On this day.

King Feng informed Ye Tian that the major factions were preparing to launch an all-out war. If this total war was won, it would be enough to deal a devastating blow to the insect race and might even force them into recuperation for a period of time.

Ye Tian understood very clearly that the death of Blazing Fire Dao Ancestor was only a trigger. Those Half-Step Domain Ancestors did not necessarily care about it, but they were also unwilling to continue dragging things out. They wanted to deal the Forbidden Insects a severe blow. Otherwise, with Dao Ancestors constantly rotating in and out, manpower would remain insufficient, making it impossible to inflict heavy losses on the Forbidden Insects.

On some battlefields, the Forbidden Insects even held the advantage and instead plundered more corpses, developing themselves and growing stronger.

Therefore, by gathering all the Dao Ancestors from the various bases and requisitioning another batch from the Profound Void Ancient Realm, they could directly launch a full-scale war. In this way, they could completely suppress the Forbidden Insects and severely damage them.

Orders were issued from one base after another. The Dao Ancestors withdrew from the various battlefields and first took some time to regroup. Once all the Dao Ancestors had arrived, the total war could begin.

Before long, a large number of Dao Ancestors came over from the Profound Void Ancient Realm. They were basically Dao Ancestors belonging to the major factions, and even the Heavenly Emperor Palace had sent multiple Emperors.

Black Wind Mountain Base.

Black Wind Mountain sent a great many Dao Ancestors. This time, even Invincible Dao Ancestors numbered five. It should be known that previously they had sent only one, namely Flowing Fire Dao Ancestor.

“Six Invincible Dao Ancestors!”

Even Ye Tian was shocked by Black Wind Mountain’s reserves. Clearly, this was definitely not the full number of its Invincible Dao Ancestors.

These six Invincible Dao Ancestors had once also been kings, but now they had already shed the title of the Ten Kings.

This time, Black Wind Mountain dispatched six Invincible Dao Ancestors. Together with ten Invincible Dao Ancestors, several unaffiliated Invincible Dao Ancestors, and the Invincible Dao Ancestors of the three Ninth-Heaven-level factions, the entire Profound Void Ancient Realm had roughly more than twenty Invincible Dao Ancestors.

But even that number was still inferior to the Forbidden Insects, because the Forbidden Insects possessed at least more than fifty Invincible Dao Ancestor-level beings.

The only area where the major factions held an advantage was in the number of Half-Step Domain Ancestors. This time, a total of eight had appeared, and the White Tiger Palace Master of the Heavenly Emperor Palace had also joined the battlefield.

As for the lord-level Forbidden Insects participating in the battle, there were only six—or at least, in the eyes of the other factions, there were six. Black Wind Mountain naturally would not reveal the intelligence that there were still two lord-level Forbidden Insects inside the Forbidden Insect nest, otherwise it would be hard to explain.

Moreover, Black Wind Mountain did not believe those two lord-level Forbidden Insects would come out to fight.

Therefore, at the Half-Step Domain Ancestor level, the major factions held the advantage. They could completely spare one Half-Step Domain Ancestor to carry out a slaughter among the commander-level Forbidden Insects, thus compensating for their numerical disadvantage at the Invincible Dao Ancestor level.

On this day.

The Dao Ancestors were ready. Across the entire Profound Void Ancient Realm, nearly two million Dao Ancestors set out, a vast and mighty force advancing into the Dark Forbidden Region and pushing toward the Forbidden Insect nest.

Very soon.

Some scattered, wandering Forbidden Insects encountered the Profound Void Ancient Realm’s army of Dao Ancestors and were mercilessly suppressed and slain. Even several elite-level Forbidden Insects were erased in an instant.

At first, the Forbidden Insects had clearly not reacted in time, and more than a hundred thousand of them were swept away and killed.

But very quickly, the Forbidden Insects also seemed to begin gathering together, which represented that there were intelligent insects among them directing the battle.

“.

Be careful. Dao Ancestors, spread out—the Forbidden Insect army is coming!”

The voices of the Half-Step Domain Ancestors rang in the ears of every Dao Ancestor.

Immediately, the Dao Ancestors scattered so as to avoid being caught up in fighting at the Half-Step Domain Ancestor level.

The first wave of clashes was between six lord-level Forbidden Insects and seven Half-Step Domain Ancestors. The strongest among them, the Azure Dragon Palace Master, did not make a move and instead remained hidden.

Only the Azure Dragon Palace Master had the confidence to kill a commander-level Forbidden Insect in a single strike. None of the other Half-Step Domain Ancestors possessed that ability; commander-level Forbidden Insects were simply too hard to kill.

The second wave belonged to the battlefield of the Invincible Dao Ancestors, and the third wave was the battlefield of the Pinnacle Dao Ancestors.

Meanwhile, the other Dao Ancestors and the large numbers of ordinary Forbidden Insects also quickly began fighting, the battlefield stretching across the vast territory of the Dark Forbidden Region.

Ye Tian’s replicated body followed the Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain in battle against the Forbidden Insects, while his true body led his family into battle as well. As long as they did not encounter powerful elite-level or higher Forbidden Insects, he was fully capable of protecting his family from any threat to their safety.

On the battlefield of the Invincible Dao Ancestors.

More than twenty Invincible Dao Ancestors clashed with fifty commander-level Forbidden Insects and were completely suppressed—they were no match at all.

Suddenly.

The Azure Dragon Palace Master appeared and struck one commander-level Forbidden Insect, directly blasting it to death.

Then, wielding a forbidden weapon, the Azure Dragon Palace Master continuously sought out those commander-level Forbidden Insects. Even the strongest among them found it difficult to withstand a single blow from him, which was enough to show just how powerful he was.

As one commander-level Forbidden Insect after another fell, the six lord-level Forbidden Insects grew enraged and tried to go over and provide support.

However, how could Eternal Dao Ancestor and the others possibly allow those six lord-level Forbidden Insects to go reinforce them? They did everything in their power to hold them back, preventing them from going to help.

Chapter 1198 The Seventh Lord-Class!

Chapter 1198: The Seventh Lord-Class

!【Second Update】

In just a short while, more than a dozen commander-class forbidden insectoids had already fallen.

To the forbidden insectoids, such losses were enough to make their hearts ache. After all, even now, there were only a little over fifty commander-class forbidden insectoids in total.

Everyone had thought that with Palace Master Azure Dragon continuously carrying out assassinations, once all the commander-class forbidden insectoids were killed off, the forbidden insectoid forces would collapse on their own.

But at this moment, a sudden change occurred.

Boom!!!! A suddenly appearing forbidden insectoid abruptly erupted with power comparable to a lord-class forbidden insectoid and instantly launched an attack at an Invincible Dao Ancestor. This Invincible Dao Ancestor was Emperor Beilin of the Heavenly Emperor Palace, and among Invincible Dao Ancestors, he was considered relatively weak.

Pfft! One of its long legs turned into a deadly weapon and directly pierced through Emperor Beilin's body. The terrifying dark forbidden power instantly annihilated his vitality.

With a single strike, Emperor Beilin fell dead.

This scene was beyond everyone's expectations; even Palace Master Azure Dragon had not anticipated it.

“There’s still a seventh lord-class forbidden insectoid, and it concealed its aura—it can actually conceal its aura!!!!”

Palace Master Azure Dragon was utterly shocked.

Even Eternal Dao Ancestor and Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor, who were in the midst of battle, were deeply surprised. According to the information they had gathered, the forbidden insectoids should not have had such a lord-class forbidden insectoid capable of hiding its aura.

However, if a lord-class forbidden insectoid could conceal its aura, then the Nine Extremes Heavenly King naturally would have had no way of detecting it.

“It might be... that... forbidden insectoid with considerable intelligence!”

Several half-step Domain Ancestors guessed inwardly.

“Seeking death!”

Palace Master Azure Dragon was enraged.

If the one who had fallen had been an Invincible Dao Ancestor from some other force, he might not have been so furious. But this lord-class forbidden insectoid had killed an Invincible Dao Ancestor from their Heavenly Emperor Palace. The death of even one Invincible Dao Ancestor was an enormous loss to the Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Boom!!! Palace Master Azure Dragon charged at that lord-class forbidden insectoid. To everyone's astonishment, that lord-class forbidden insectoid was not the slightest bit weaker than Palace Master Azure Dragon; the two exchanged blows evenly.

Without Palace Master Azure Dragon carrying out sudden attacks, the pressure on the Invincible Dao Ancestors multiplied greatly.

“Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor, your speed is the fastest. Go continue killing the commander-class forbidden insectoids!”

Palace Master White Tiger suggested.

After all, their seven half-step Domain Ancestors were facing six lord-class forbidden insectoids, so they had one extra. It was only because they wanted to form a completely overwhelming advantage that they had used seven against six. But if it were six against six, even if they didn’t hold the advantage, it would still be enough to tie them down.

“Alright!”

Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor agreed.

Whoosh! Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor instantly withdrew from the half-step Domain Ancestor battlefield, tore through the void, and arrived at the battlefield of the Invincible Dao Ancestors, where he targeted one of the... commander-class forbidden insectoids.

However, Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor’s attack power was not as great as Palace Master Azure Dragon’s, so he could not kill a... commander-class forbidden insectoid in a single blow. But two attacks were still enough to kill one commander-class forbidden insectoid.

The attacks of a half-step Domain Ancestor were unimaginably swift, so going all out for two attacks took almost no time. Thus, as soon as Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor made his move, the commander-class forbidden insectoids began falling one after another again.

Before long, the commander-class forbidden insectoids had suffered grievous losses.

However.

At this moment, another Invincible Dao Ancestor still fell. It was Dao Ancestor Jingyin from the Vast Heaven Sect, who had been besieged and killed by six commander-class forbidden insectoids.

It couldn’t be helped—the commander-class forbidden insectoids were too numerous. The Invincible Dao Ancestors each had to deal with two or three, and Dao Ancestor Jingyin had suddenly been surrounded by six commander-class forbidden insectoids. Among them, one commander-class forbidden insectoid was far stronger than the others, with combat power not much inferior even to a half-step Domain Ancestor.

Therefore, Dao Ancestor Jingyin was unable to hold out and was directly force-killed.

After Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor discovered Dao Ancestor Jingyin’s fall, he immediately attacked that powerful commander-class forbidden insectoid. But the other side relied on its perfect forbidden body, attack power far beyond the commander class, and the coordination of the other five commander-class forbidden insectoids, and actually managed to withstand Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor’s attacks for a time.

At this rate, although they could not win, they could still hold out for a while...

!!!”

Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor was extremely puzzled.

If Ye Tian were here, he would know the reason, because this commander-class forbidden insectoid also possessed a forbidden talent. A forbidden insectoid with a forbidden talent far surpassed ordinary forbidden insectoids.

Just like half-step Domain Ancestors and lord-class forbidden insectoids, lord-class forbidden insectoids relied on their forbidden talents to contend against half-step Domain Ancestors who had created forbidden Dao arts. With their bodily advantages, if they fought for a long time, they could even gain a certain upper hand.

After all, the Dark Forbidden Domain was practically the most suitable battle environment for them, while half-step Domain Ancestors were still somewhat unaccustomed to the environment there and could not perfectly bring out their full combat strength.

If this were the Dao Mountain Realm, Divine Ruins Dao Ancestor would also have been able to kill this commander-class forbidden insectoid with a forbidden talent in a short time.

Ye Tian paid no attention to the war between the Invincible Dao Ancestors and half-step Domain Ancestors.

At this moment, by himself, he was fighting thirty Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids, easing the pressure on the others.

If it had been any other top Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestor, they would have long since been besieged to death. Yet Ye Tian could easily withstand the encirclement of so many Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids, and from time to time could even kill one or two.

Of course, the greatest source of confidence that let him dare face the siege of thirty Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids was not... his attack power. No matter how strong his attack power was, it still could not withstand the encirclement of that many Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids. Even a Pinnacle Dao Ancestor with weaker defenses might fall if even slightly careless.

But Ye Tian was a Dao Ancestor advanced from an Ultimate True Ancestor, possessing an ultimate Dao source. He could use the power of forbidden origin without limit to repair his injuries.

Therefore, Ye Tian was injured again and again, and again and again used forbidden origin power to heal himself. He simply could not be killed.

Unless a single attack exceeded his limit and caused him to be injured faster than he could recover, only then might he be killed.

As one Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoid after another died, the pressure on Ye Tian grew smaller and smaller, and the speed at which he killed them became faster and faster.

Likewise, Ye Tian’s copied body—the Nine Extremes Heavenly King—possessed equally terrifying combat power and was likewise fighting dozens of Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids.

Ye Tian’s overwhelming strength also drew the attention of quite a few Seventh-Heaven Dao Ancestors, each of them marveling in astonishment.

“My heavens, the Nine Extremes Heavenly King is way too terrifying, isn’t he? Fighting dozens of Seventh-Heaven forbidden insectoids alone and even slaughtering them!”

“The Nine Extremes Heavenly King’s combat power has already surpassed Young Master Ghost. He could even kill Young Master Ghost by himself. Compared with the weakest Pinnacle Dao Ancestor, the Nine Extremes Heavenly King is no weaker. If we're talking about survival ability, he’s even more terrifying than ordinary Supreme Dao Ancestors!”

“Hahaha, with the Nine Extremes Heavenly King here, the pressure on us is much less. Hurry and kill them—once we wipe out the forbidden insectoids here, we’ll go support the Dao Ancestors in the other areas!”

The same kind of praise was also happening over on Ye Tian’s true body’s side.

And Ye Tian was going all out to kill forbidden insectoids, not distracted in the slightest.

Chapter 1199: Two Forbidden Talents! Third Update..

Chapter 1199: Two Forbidden Talents

!【Third update, please subscribe in full】

The battle continued.

From time to time, forbidden insectoids fell, and from time to time, Dao Ancestors perished.

However, whenever a Dao Ancestor fell, the people nearby would put away the Dao Ancestor’s corpse to prevent it from being seized by the forbidden insectoids.

Since the Dao Ancestors cooperated with one another and also held the advantage in numbers, the number of Dao Ancestors who fell was far from comparable to that of the forbidden insectoids.

As time passed, more and more forbidden insectoids fell, and the Dao Ancestors’ advantage grew greater and greater.

But suddenly, the voices of the half-step Domain Ancestors spread across one battlefield after another.

“Retreat, all of you!”

The other Dao Ancestors did not know what had happened, but they guessed that something must have gone wrong on the half-step Domain Ancestor battlefield, so each and every one of them began to withdraw from the battlefield.

“We’re retreating too!”

Ye Tian said to Xiao Yue, Ye Xingchen, Ye Xingyue, and Ye Yu.

They followed Ye Tian and quickly withdrew. If any forbidden insectoids pursued them, Ye Tian alone could easily hold them off.

Very soon, they withdrew from this region.

“Two lord-level forbidden insectoids are coming over. We have to withdraw as well!”

Dao Ancestor Shenxu said grimly.

He knew that those two lord-level forbidden insectoids in the distance had to be the two forbidden insectoids inside the forbidden insectoid nest, but he had not expected them to actually come out.

Or rather, perhaps another lord-level forbidden insectoid had been born among the forbidden insectoids, and so one lord-level forbidden insectoid had been left behind to guard the forbidden insect tree.

If that was the case, then the forbidden insectoids had at least nine lord-level forbidden insectoids, perhaps even ten.

And the various bases had only eight half-step Domain Ancestors; they held no advantage at all.

Once those two lord-level forbidden insectoids joined the battlefield, they would be placed completely at a disadvantage, and at that time countless Dao Ancestors would fall and die.

At this moment.

The invincible Dao Ancestors also began withdrawing from the battlefield, not daring to remain here any longer, otherwise they too would perish here.

The eight half-step Domain Ancestors did their utmost to block those lord-level forbidden insectoids, and Dao Ancestor Shenxu also gave up hunting commander-level forbidden insectoids and instead went to intercept the two soon-to-arrive lord-level forbidden insectoids.

However, Dao Ancestor Shenxu quickly fell into a disadvantageous position and was suppressed. The two arriving lord-level ones were somewhat stronger than ordinary lord-levels, and with the two of them coming together, Dao Ancestor Shenxu was no match for them.

Still, holding on for a while seemed to be no problem.

The lord-level forbidden insectoids were intercepted, but those commander-level forbidden insectoids were not. Leading a large number of forbidden insectoids, they began to give chase.

Fortunately, nearly twenty commander-level forbidden insectoids had already been killed earlier, and only a little over thirty remained. Although they still greatly outnumbered the invincible Dao Ancestors, at least the gap was not as huge as before.

However, the commander-level forbidden insectoids were faster. The invincible Dao Ancestors could use some top-tier escape-type treasures to flee smoothly, but some weaker Dao Ancestors were too slow. Even if they fled, they could only scatter in all directions.

Once they were caught, those Dao Ancestors could only fall and die.

....A group of Dao Ancestors from Black Wind Mountain were in retreat, and Ye Tian was protecting these Sixth and Seventh Heaven Dao Ancestors as they withdrew. After all, at a time like this, Black Wind Mountain’s pinnacle Dao Ancestors had no way to concern themselves with these lower-Heaven Dao Ancestors.

Suddenly.

Ye Tian sensed the aura of a commander-level forbidden insectoid. Any Dao Ancestor attacked by it fell one after another, utterly unable to resist, and this commander-level forbidden insectoid was heading toward Ye Tian’s side.

“Hurry and go. Spare no cost to escape. Stop holding back those escape-type treasures!”

Ye Tian reminded the Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain.

“Ninth Extreme Heavenly King, you go first! You are the hope of our Black Wind Mountain!”

Quite a few Dao Ancestors hurriedly said.

“It’s fine. You all go. I have a way to save my life. These are the forbidden insectoids I hunted and the Dao Ancestor corpses I collected—take them all with you. Don’t waste time. This is an order! In my capacity as Great Heavenly King of Black Wind Mountain, I order you to leave at once!”

Ye Tian commanded.

The Dao Ancestors of Black Wind Mountain did not dare disobey. They took Ye Tian’s forbidden insectoids and Dao Ancestor corpses and quickly withdrew.

And at that moment, that commander-level forbidden insectoid also charged over.

Ye Tian unleashed his forbidden domain, the Great Desolate Dharma Body, and one Dao technique after another. He even activated the forbidden talent Dark Spear, empowering the forbidden spear in his hand and launching a terrifying strike.

Boom!!!! This strike directly slowed that commander-level forbidden insectoid’s speed, eventually bringing it to a halt.

And Ye Tian habitually enveloped it with his Copy Talent, only to discover something astonishing.

“It has forbidden talents!”

Ye Tian was shocked.

More importantly, it not only possessed the forbidden talent Dark Spear, but also the forbidden talent—Stealth! “Copy!”

“Copy!”

In an instant, Ye Tian copied both of its forbidden talents, and that commander-level forbidden insectoid also launched an attack at Ye Tian. One long leg, like a spear, instantly thrust over, leaving Ye Tian no way to dodge.

With a puff! Ye Tian’s body was pierced through, but he had long since gathered an enormous amount of forbidden origin power within his body. At the instant his body was pierced, he immediately mobilized the forbidden origin power to heal himself, and so he was not instantly killed, though he was heavily wounded and at death’s door.

This commander-level forbidden insectoid seemed to freeze for a moment, as if puzzled as to why Ye Tian had not been killed with one stab like the other ants.

0So, it raised its long leg again and stabbed toward Ye Tian.

Ye Tian recovered from his injuries at the fastest speed possible, and with all his might used the Heavenly Illusion Divine Step to shift a small step, barely avoiding the commander-level forbidden insectoid’s attack and surviving once again.

At this time.

This commander-level forbidden insectoid seemed to be enraged. It no longer toyed around and rapidly stabbed down with one long leg, turning it into one afterimage after another, and the speed was simply too fast.

This time, Ye Tian did not dodge it and was directly pierced through and killed in one blow.

After killing Ye Tian, this commander-level forbidden insectoid seemed very happy and prepared to take away Ye Tian’s corpse, but to its shock, Ye Tian’s corpse dissipated, leaving behind only a few broken Dao artifacts and a small amount of resources.

Roar!!! The commander-level forbidden insectoid roared, seemingly questioning who had stolen its corpse.

After that, it continued chasing and killing the other Dao Ancestors.

And with Ye Tian’s copy body blocking it, that group of Dao Ancestors from Black Wind Mountain successfully withdrew and were not caught by the commander-level forbidden insectoid, thus preserving their lives.

A long while later.

The Dao Ancestors from the various bases had almost all returned to their bases, and the half-step Domain Ancestors had returned as well, though each of them bore injuries, clearly having suffered a great loss.

However, the forbidden insectoids did not pursue them all the way.

Their losses were even more severe. If they continued attacking and their losses became too great, the whole race would be in danger.

Forbidden insectoids could reproduce quickly; there was no need for them to fight a one-off war. Fighting slowly and steadily was their style.
